     19 <p> plug.vim (84862B)</p><hr/><pre id="blob">
     20 <a href="#l1" class="line" id="l1">      1</a> &quot; vim-plug: Vim plugin manager
     21 <a href="#l2" class="line" id="l2">      2</a> &quot; ============================
     22 <a href="#l3" class="line" id="l3">      3</a> &quot;
     23 <a href="#l4" class="line" id="l4">      4</a> &quot; 1. Download plug.vim and put it in &#39;autoload&#39; directory
     24 <a href="#l5" class="line" id="l5">      5</a> &quot;
     25 <a href="#l6" class="line" id="l6">      6</a> &quot;   # Vim
     26 <a href="#l7" class="line" id="l7">      7</a> &quot;   curl -fLo ~/.vim/autoload/plug.vim --create-dirs \
     27 <a href="#l8" class="line" id="l8">      8</a> &quot;     https://raw.githubusercontent.com/junegunn/vim-plug/master/plug.vim
     28 <a href="#l9" class="line" id="l9">      9</a> &quot;
     29 <a href="#l10" class="line" id="l10">     10</a> &quot;   # Neovim
     30 <a href="#l11" class="line" id="l11">     11</a> &quot;   sh -c &#39;curl -fLo &quot;${XDG_DATA_HOME:-$HOME/.local/share}&quot;/nvim/site/autoload/plug.vim --create-dirs \
     31 <a href="#l12" class="line" id="l12">     12</a> &quot;     https://raw.githubusercontent.com/junegunn/vim-plug/master/plug.vim&#39;
     32 <a href="#l13" class="line" id="l13">     13</a> &quot;
     33 <a href="#l14" class="line" id="l14">     14</a> &quot; 2. Add a vim-plug section to your ~/.vimrc (or ~/.config/nvim/init.vim for Neovim)
     34 <a href="#l15" class="line" id="l15">     15</a> &quot;
     35 <a href="#l16" class="line" id="l16">     16</a> &quot;   call plug#begin()
     36 <a href="#l17" class="line" id="l17">     17</a> &quot;
     37 <a href="#l18" class="line" id="l18">     18</a> &quot;   &quot; List your plugins here
     38 <a href="#l19" class="line" id="l19">     19</a> &quot;   Plug &#39;tpope/vim-sensible&#39;
     39 <a href="#l20" class="line" id="l20">     20</a> &quot;
     40 <a href="#l21" class="line" id="l21">     21</a> &quot;   call plug#end()
     41 <a href="#l22" class="line" id="l22">     22</a> &quot;
     42 <a href="#l23" class="line" id="l23">     23</a> &quot; 3. Reload the file or restart Vim, then you can,
     43 <a href="#l24" class="line" id="l24">     24</a> &quot;
     44 <a href="#l25" class="line" id="l25">     25</a> &quot;     :PlugInstall to install plugins
     45 <a href="#l26" class="line" id="l26">     26</a> &quot;     :PlugUpdate  to update plugins
     46 <a href="#l27" class="line" id="l27">     27</a> &quot;     :PlugDiff    to review the changes from the last update
     47 <a href="#l28" class="line" id="l28">     28</a> &quot;     :PlugClean   to remove plugins no longer in the list
     48 <a href="#l29" class="line" id="l29">     29</a> &quot;
     49 <a href="#l30" class="line" id="l30">     30</a> &quot; For more information, see https://github.com/junegunn/vim-plug
     50 <a href="#l31" class="line" id="l31">     31</a> &quot;

    115 <a href="#l96" class="line" id="l96">     96</a> function! s:git_dir(dir) abort
    116 <a href="#l97" class="line" id="l97">     97</a>   let gitdir = s:trim(a:dir) . &#39;/.git&#39;
    117 <a href="#l98" class="line" id="l98">     98</a>   if isdirectory(gitdir)
    118 <a href="#l99" class="line" id="l99">     99</a>     return gitdir
    119 <a href="#l100" class="line" id="l100">    100</a>   endif
    120 <a href="#l101" class="line" id="l101">    101</a>   if !filereadable(gitdir)
    121 <a href="#l102" class="line" id="l102">    102</a>     return &#39;&#39;
    122 <a href="#l103" class="line" id="l103">    103</a>   endif
    123 <a href="#l104" class="line" id="l104">    104</a>   let gitdir = matchstr(get(readfile(gitdir), 0, &#39;&#39;), &#39;^gitdir: \zs.*&#39;)
    124 <a href="#l105" class="line" id="l105">    105</a>   if len(gitdir) &amp;&amp; !s:isabsolute(gitdir)
    125 <a href="#l106" class="line" id="l106">    106</a>     let gitdir = a:dir . &#39;/&#39; . gitdir
    126 <a href="#l107" class="line" id="l107">    107</a>   endif
    127 <a href="#l108" class="line" id="l108">    108</a>   return isdirectory(gitdir) ? gitdir : &#39;&#39;
    128 <a href="#l109" class="line" id="l109">    109</a> endfunction

    132 <a href="#l113" class="line" id="l113">    113</a>   let config = gitdir . &#39;/config&#39;
    133 <a href="#l114" class="line" id="l114">    114</a>   if empty(gitdir) || !filereadable(config)
    134 <a href="#l115" class="line" id="l115">    115</a>     return &#39;&#39;
    135 <a href="#l116" class="line" id="l116">    116</a>   endif
    136 <a href="#l117" class="line" id="l117">    117</a>   return matchstr(join(readfile(config)), &#39;\[remote &quot;origin&quot;\].\{-}url\s*=\s*\zs\S*\ze&#39;)
    137 <a href="#l118" class="line" id="l118">    118</a> endfunction
    138 <a href="#l119" class="line" id="l119">    119</a> 
    139 <a href="#l120" class="line" id="l120">    120</a> function! s:git_revision(dir) abort
    140 <a href="#l121" class="line" id="l121">    121</a>   let gitdir = s:git_dir(a:dir)
    141 <a href="#l122" class="line" id="l122">    122</a>   let head = gitdir . &#39;/HEAD&#39;
    142 <a href="#l123" class="line" id="l123">    123</a>   if empty(gitdir) || !filereadable(head)
    143 <a href="#l124" class="line" id="l124">    124</a>     return &#39;&#39;
    144 <a href="#l125" class="line" id="l125">    125</a>   endif
    145 <a href="#l126" class="line" id="l126">    126</a> 
    146 <a href="#l127" class="line" id="l127">    127</a>   let line = get(readfile(head), 0, &#39;&#39;)
    147 <a href="#l128" class="line" id="l128">    128</a>   let ref = matchstr(line, &#39;^ref: \zs.*&#39;)
    148 <a href="#l129" class="line" id="l129">    129</a>   if empty(ref)
    149 <a href="#l130" class="line" id="l130">    130</a>     return line
    150 <a href="#l131" class="line" id="l131">    131</a>   endif
    151 <a href="#l132" class="line" id="l132">    132</a> 
    152 <a href="#l133" class="line" id="l133">    133</a>   if filereadable(gitdir . &#39;/&#39; . ref)
    153 <a href="#l134" class="line" id="l134">    134</a>     return get(readfile(gitdir . &#39;/&#39; . ref), 0, &#39;&#39;)
    154 <a href="#l135" class="line" id="l135">    135</a>   endif
    155 <a href="#l136" class="line" id="l136">    136</a> 
    156 <a href="#l137" class="line" id="l137">    137</a>   if filereadable(gitdir . &#39;/packed-refs&#39;)
    157 <a href="#l138" class="line" id="l138">    138</a>     for line in readfile(gitdir . &#39;/packed-refs&#39;)
    158 <a href="#l139" class="line" id="l139">    139</a>       if line =~# &#39; &#39; . ref
    159 <a href="#l140" class="line" id="l140">    140</a>         return matchstr(line, &#39;^[0-9a-f]*&#39;)
    160 <a href="#l141" class="line" id="l141">    141</a>       endif
    161 <a href="#l142" class="line" id="l142">    142</a>     endfor
    162 <a href="#l143" class="line" id="l143">    143</a>   endif
    163 <a href="#l144" class="line" id="l144">    144</a> 
    164 <a href="#l145" class="line" id="l145">    145</a>   return &#39;&#39;
    165 <a href="#l146" class="line" id="l146">    146</a> endfunction

    177 <a href="#l158" class="line" id="l158">    158</a> function! s:git_origin_branch(spec)
    178 <a href="#l159" class="line" id="l159">    159</a>   if len(a:spec.branch)
    179 <a href="#l160" class="line" id="l160">    160</a>     return a:spec.branch

    181 <a href="#l162" class="line" id="l162">    162</a> 
    182 <a href="#l163" class="line" id="l163">    163</a>   &quot; The file may not be present if this is a local repository
    183 <a href="#l164" class="line" id="l164">    164</a>   let gitdir = s:git_dir(a:spec.dir)
    184 <a href="#l165" class="line" id="l165">    165</a>   let origin_head = gitdir.&#39;/refs/remotes/origin/HEAD&#39;
    185 <a href="#l166" class="line" id="l166">    166</a>   if len(gitdir) &amp;&amp; filereadable(origin_head)
    186 <a href="#l167" class="line" id="l167">    167</a>     return matchstr(get(readfile(origin_head), 0, &#39;&#39;),
    187 <a href="#l168" class="line" id="l168">    168</a>                   \ &#39;^ref: refs/remotes/origin/\zs.*&#39;)
    188 <a href="#l169" class="line" id="l169">    169</a>   endif
    189 <a href="#l170" class="line" id="l170">    170</a>

    191 <a href="#l172" class="line" id="l172">    172</a>   let result = s:lines(s:system(&#39;git symbolic-ref --short HEAD&#39;, a:spec.dir))
    192 <a href="#l173" class="line" id="l173">    173</a>   return v:shell_error ? &#39;&#39; : result[-1]

    196 <a href="#l177" class="line" id="l177">    177</a>   function! s:plug_call(fn, ...)

    226 <a href="#l207" class="line" id="l207">    207</a> 
    227 <a href="#l208" class="line" id="l208">    208</a> function! plug#begin(...)
    228 <a href="#l209" class="line" id="l209">    209</a>   if a:0 &gt; 0
    229 <a href="#l210" class="line" id="l210">    210</a>     let home = s:path(s:plug_fnamemodify(s:plug_expand(a:1), &#39;:p&#39;))
    230 <a href="#l211" class="line" id="l211">    211</a>   elseif exists(&#39;g:plug_home&#39;)
    231 <a href="#l212" class="line" id="l212">    212</a>     let home = s:path(g:plug_home)
    232 <a href="#l213" class="line" id="l213">    213</a>   elseif has(&#39;nvim&#39;)
    233 <a href="#l214" class="line" id="l214">    214</a>     let home = stdpath(&#39;data&#39;) . &#39;/plugged&#39;
    234 <a href="#l215" class="line" id="l215">    215</a>   elseif !empty(&amp;rtp)
    235 <a href="#l216" class="line" id="l216">    216</a>     let home = s:path(split(&amp;rtp, &#39;,&#39;)[0]) . &#39;/plugged&#39;
    236 <a href="#l217" class="line" id="l217">    217</a>   else
    237 <a href="#l218" class="line" id="l218">    218</a>     return s:err(&#39;Unable to determine plug home. Try calling plug#begin() with a path argument.&#39;)
    238 <a href="#l219" class="line" id="l219">    219</a>   endif
    239 <a href="#l220" class="line" id="l220">    220</a>   if s:plug_fnamemodify(home, &#39;:t&#39;) ==# &#39;plugin&#39; &amp;&amp; s:plug_fnamemodify(home, &#39;:h&#39;) ==# s:first_rtp
    240 <a href="#l221" class="line" id="l221">    221</a>     return s:err(&#39;Invalid plug home. &#39;.home.&#39; is a standard Vim runtime path and is not allowed.&#39;)
    241 <a href="#l222" class="line" id="l222">    222</a>   endif
    242 <a href="#l223" class="line" id="l223">    223</a> 
    243 <a href="#l224" class="line" id="l224">    224</a>   let g:plug_home = home
    244 <a href="#l225" class="line" id="l225">    225</a>   let g:plugs = {}
    245 <a href="#l226" class="line" id="l226">    226</a>   let g:plugs_order = []
    246 <a href="#l227" class="line" id="l227">    227</a>   let s:triggers = {}
    247 <a href="#l228" class="line" id="l228">    228</a> 
    248 <a href="#l229" class="line" id="l229">    229</a>   call s:define_commands()
    249 <a href="#l230" class="line" id="l230">    230</a>   return 1
    250 <a href="#l231" class="line" id="l231">    231</a> endfunction
    251 <a href="#l232" class="line" id="l232">    232</a> 
    252 <a href="#l233" class="line" id="l233">    233</a> function! s:define_commands()
    253 <a href="#l234" class="line" id="l234">    234</a>   command! -nargs=+ -bar Plug call plug#(&lt;args&gt;)
    254 <a href="#l235" class="line" id="l235">    235</a>   if !executable(&#39;git&#39;)
    255 <a href="#l236" class="line" id="l236">    236</a>     return s:err(&#39;`git` executable not found. Most commands will not be available. To suppress this message, prepend `silent!` to `call plug#begin(...)`.&#39;)
    256 <a href="#l237" class="line" id="l237">    237</a>   endif
    257 <a href="#l238" class="line" id="l238">    238</a>   if has(&#39;win32&#39;)
    258 <a href="#l239" class="line" id="l239">    239</a>   \ &amp;&amp; &amp;shellslash
    259 <a href="#l240" class="line" id="l240">    240</a>   \ &amp;&amp; (&amp;shell =~# &#39;cmd\(\.exe\)\?$&#39; || s:is_powershell(&amp;shell))
    260 <a href="#l241" class="line" id="l241">    241</a>     return s:err(&#39;vim-plug does not support shell, &#39; . &amp;shell . &#39;, when shellslash is set.&#39;)
    261 <a href="#l242" class="line" id="l242">    242</a>   endif
    262 <a href="#l243" class="line" id="l243">    243</a>   if !has(&#39;nvim&#39;)
    263 <a href="#l244" class="line" id="l244">    244</a>     \ &amp;&amp; (has(&#39;win32&#39;) || has(&#39;win32unix&#39;))
    264 <a href="#l245" class="line" id="l245">    245</a>     \ &amp;&amp; !has(&#39;multi_byte&#39;)
    265 <a href="#l246" class="line" id="l246">    246</a>     return s:err(&#39;Vim needs +multi_byte feature on Windows to run shell commands. Enable +iconv for best results.&#39;)
    266 <a href="#l247" class="line" id="l247">    247</a>   endif
    267 <a href="#l248" class="line" id="l248">    248</a>   command! -nargs=* -bar -bang -complete=customlist,s:names PlugInstall call s:install(&lt;bang&gt;0, [&lt;f-args&gt;])
    268 <a href="#l249" class="line" id="l249">    249</a>   command! -nargs=* -bar -bang -complete=customlist,s:names PlugUpdate  call s:update(&lt;bang&gt;0, [&lt;f-args&gt;])
    269 <a href="#l250" class="line" id="l250">    250</a>   command! -nargs=0 -bar -bang PlugClean call s:clean(&lt;bang&gt;0)
    270 <a href="#l251" class="line" id="l251">    251</a>   command! -nargs=0 -bar PlugUpgrade if s:upgrade() | execute &#39;source&#39; s:esc(s:me) | endif
    271 <a href="#l252" class="line" id="l252">    252</a>   command! -nargs=0 -bar PlugStatus  call s:status()
    272 <a href="#l253" class="line" id="l253">    253</a>   command! -nargs=0 -bar PlugDiff    call s:diff()
    273 <a href="#l254" class="line" id="l254">    254</a>   command! -nargs=? -bar -bang -complete=file PlugSnapshot call s:snapshot(&lt;bang&gt;0, &lt;f-args&gt;)
    274 <a href="#l255" class="line" id="l255">    255</a> endfunction
    275 <a href="#l256" class="line" id="l256">    256</a> 
    276 <a href="#l257" class="line" id="l257">    257</a> function! s:to_a(v)
    277 <a href="#l258" class="line" id="l258">    258</a>   return type(a:v) == s:TYPE.list ? a:v : [a:v]
    278 <a href="#l259" class="line" id="l259">    259</a> endfunction
    279 <a href="#l260" class="line" id="l260">    260</a> 
    280 <a href="#l261" class="line" id="l261">    261</a> function! s:to_s(v)
    281 <a href="#l262" class="line" id="l262">    262</a>   return type(a:v) == s:TYPE.string ? a:v : join(a:v, &quot;\n&quot;) . &quot;\n&quot;
    282 <a href="#l263" class="line" id="l263">    263</a> endfunction
    283 <a href="#l264" class="line" id="l264">    264</a> 
    284 <a href="#l265" class="line" id="l265">    265</a> function! s:glob(from, pattern)
    285 <a href="#l266" class="line" id="l266">    266</a>   return s:lines(globpath(a:from, a:pattern))
    286 <a href="#l267" class="line" id="l267">    267</a> endfunction
    287 <a href="#l268" class="line" id="l268">    268</a> 
    288 <a href="#l269" class="line" id="l269">    269</a> function! s:source(from, ...)
    289 <a href="#l270" class="line" id="l270">    270</a>   let found = 0
    290 <a href="#l271" class="line" id="l271">    271</a>   for pattern in a:000
    291 <a href="#l272" class="line" id="l272">    272</a>     for vim in s:glob(a:from, pattern)
    292 <a href="#l273" class="line" id="l273">    273</a>       execute &#39;source&#39; s:esc(vim)
    293 <a href="#l274" class="line" id="l274">    274</a>       let found = 1
    294 <a href="#l275" class="line" id="l275">    275</a>     endfor
    295 <a href="#l276" class="line" id="l276">    276</a>   endfor
    296 <a href="#l277" class="line" id="l277">    277</a>   return found
    297 <a href="#l278" class="line" id="l278">    278</a> endfunction
    298 <a href="#l279" class="line" id="l279">    279</a> 
    299 <a href="#l280" class="line" id="l280">    280</a> function! s:assoc(dict, key, val)
    300 <a href="#l281" class="line" id="l281">    281</a>   let a:dict[a:key] = add(get(a:dict, a:key, []), a:val)
    301 <a href="#l282" class="line" id="l282">    282</a> endfunction
    302 <a href="#l283" class="line" id="l283">    283</a> 
    303 <a href="#l284" class="line" id="l284">    284</a> function! s:ask(message, ...)
    304 <a href="#l285" class="line" id="l285">    285</a>   call inputsave()
    305 <a href="#l286" class="line" id="l286">    286</a>   echohl WarningMsg
    306 <a href="#l287" class="line" id="l287">    287</a>   let answer = input(a:message.(a:0 ? &#39; (y/N/a) &#39; : &#39; (y/N) &#39;))
    307 <a href="#l288" class="line" id="l288">    288</a>   echohl None
    308 <a href="#l289" class="line" id="l289">    289</a>   call inputrestore()
    309 <a href="#l290" class="line" id="l290">    290</a>   echo &quot;\r&quot;
    310 <a href="#l291" class="line" id="l291">    291</a>   return (a:0 &amp;&amp; answer =~? &#39;^a&#39;) ? 2 : (answer =~? &#39;^y&#39;) ? 1 : 0
    311 <a href="#l292" class="line" id="l292">    292</a> endfunction
    312 <a href="#l293" class="line" id="l293">    293</a> 
    313 <a href="#l294" class="line" id="l294">    294</a> function! s:ask_no_interrupt(...)
    314 <a href="#l295" class="line" id="l295">    295</a>   try
    315 <a href="#l296" class="line" id="l296">    296</a>     return call(&#39;s:ask&#39;, a:000)
    316 <a href="#l297" class="line" id="l297">    297</a>   catch
    317 <a href="#l298" class="line" id="l298">    298</a>     return 0
    318 <a href="#l299" class="line" id="l299">    299</a>   endtry
    319 <a href="#l300" class="line" id="l300">    300</a> endfunction
    320 <a href="#l301" class="line" id="l301">    301</a> 
    321 <a href="#l302" class="line" id="l302">    302</a> function! s:lazy(plug, opt)
    322 <a href="#l303" class="line" id="l303">    303</a>   return has_key(a:plug, a:opt) &amp;&amp;
    323 <a href="#l304" class="line" id="l304">    304</a>         \ (empty(s:to_a(a:plug[a:opt]))         ||
    324 <a href="#l305" class="line" id="l305">    305</a>         \  !isdirectory(a:plug.dir)             ||
    325 <a href="#l306" class="line" id="l306">    306</a>         \  len(s:glob(s:rtp(a:plug), &#39;plugin&#39;)) ||
    326 <a href="#l307" class="line" id="l307">    307</a>         \  len(s:glob(s:rtp(a:plug), &#39;after/plugin&#39;)))
    327 <a href="#l308" class="line" id="l308">    308</a> endfunction
    328 <a href="#l309" class="line" id="l309">    309</a> 
    329 <a href="#l310" class="line" id="l310">    310</a> function! plug#end()
    330 <a href="#l311" class="line" id="l311">    311</a>   if !exists(&#39;g:plugs&#39;)
    331 <a href="#l312" class="line" id="l312">    312</a>     return s:err(&#39;plug#end() called without calling plug#begin() first&#39;)
    332 <a href="#l313" class="line" id="l313">    313</a>   endif
    333 <a href="#l314" class="line" id="l314">    314</a> 
    334 <a href="#l315" class="line" id="l315">    315</a>   if exists(&#39;#PlugLOD&#39;)
    335 <a href="#l316" class="line" id="l316">    316</a>     augroup PlugLOD
    336 <a href="#l317" class="line" id="l317">    317</a>       autocmd!
    337 <a href="#l318" class="line" id="l318">    318</a>     augroup END
    338 <a href="#l319" class="line" id="l319">    319</a>     augroup! PlugLOD
    339 <a href="#l320" class="line" id="l320">    320</a>   endif
    340 <a href="#l321" class="line" id="l321">    321</a>   let lod = { &#39;ft&#39;: {}, &#39;map&#39;: {}, &#39;cmd&#39;: {} }
    341 <a href="#l322" class="line" id="l322">    322</a> 
    342 <a href="#l323" class="line" id="l323">    323</a>   if get(g:, &#39;did_load_filetypes&#39;, 0)
    343 <a href="#l324" class="line" id="l324">    324</a>     filetype off
    344 <a href="#l325" class="line" id="l325">    325</a>   endif
    345 <a href="#l326" class="line" id="l326">    326</a>   for name in g:plugs_order
    346 <a href="#l327" class="line" id="l327">    327</a>     if !has_key(g:plugs, name)
    347 <a href="#l328" class="line" id="l328">    328</a>       continue
    348 <a href="#l329" class="line" id="l329">    329</a>     endif
    349 <a href="#l330" class="line" id="l330">    330</a>     let plug = g:plugs[name]
    350 <a href="#l331" class="line" id="l331">    331</a>     if get(s:loaded, name, 0) || !s:lazy(plug, &#39;on&#39;) &amp;&amp; !s:lazy(plug, &#39;for&#39;)
    351 <a href="#l332" class="line" id="l332">    332</a>       let s:loaded[name] = 1
    352 <a href="#l333" class="line" id="l333">    333</a>       continue
    353 <a href="#l334" class="line" id="l334">    334</a>     endif
    354 <a href="#l335" class="line" id="l335">    335</a> 
    355 <a href="#l336" class="line" id="l336">    336</a>     if has_key(plug, &#39;on&#39;)
    356 <a href="#l337" class="line" id="l337">    337</a>       let s:triggers[name] = { &#39;map&#39;: [], &#39;cmd&#39;: [] }
    357 <a href="#l338" class="line" id="l338">    338</a>       for cmd in s:to_a(plug.on)
    358 <a href="#l339" class="line" id="l339">    339</a>         if cmd =~? &#39;^&lt;Plug&gt;.\+&#39;
    359 <a href="#l340" class="line" id="l340">    340</a>           if empty(mapcheck(cmd)) &amp;&amp; empty(mapcheck(cmd, &#39;i&#39;))
    360 <a href="#l341" class="line" id="l341">    341</a>             call s:assoc(lod.map, cmd, name)
    361 <a href="#l342" class="line" id="l342">    342</a>           endif
    362 <a href="#l343" class="line" id="l343">    343</a>           call add(s:triggers[name].map, cmd)
    363 <a href="#l344" class="line" id="l344">    344</a>         elseif cmd =~# &#39;^[A-Z]&#39;
    364 <a href="#l345" class="line" id="l345">    345</a>           let cmd = substitute(cmd, &#39;!*$&#39;, &#39;&#39;, &#39;&#39;)
    365 <a href="#l346" class="line" id="l346">    346</a>           if exists(&#39;:&#39;.cmd) != 2
    366 <a href="#l347" class="line" id="l347">    347</a>             call s:assoc(lod.cmd, cmd, name)
    367 <a href="#l348" class="line" id="l348">    348</a>           endif
    368 <a href="#l349" class="line" id="l349">    349</a>           call add(s:triggers[name].cmd, cmd)
    369 <a href="#l350" class="line" id="l350">    350</a>         else
    370 <a href="#l351" class="line" id="l351">    351</a>           call s:err(&#39;Invalid `on` option: &#39;.cmd.
    371 <a href="#l352" class="line" id="l352">    352</a>           \ &#39;. Should start with an uppercase letter or `&lt;Plug&gt;`.&#39;)
    372 <a href="#l353" class="line" id="l353">    353</a>         endif
    373 <a href="#l354" class="line" id="l354">    354</a>       endfor
    374 <a href="#l355" class="line" id="l355">    355</a>     endif
    375 <a href="#l356" class="line" id="l356">    356</a> 
    376 <a href="#l357" class="line" id="l357">    357</a>     if has_key(plug, &#39;for&#39;)
    377 <a href="#l358" class="line" id="l358">    358</a>       let types = s:to_a(plug.for)
    378 <a href="#l359" class="line" id="l359">    359</a>       if !empty(types)
    379 <a href="#l360" class="line" id="l360">    360</a>         augroup filetypedetect
    380 <a href="#l361" class="line" id="l361">    361</a>         call s:source(s:rtp(plug), &#39;ftdetect/**/*.vim&#39;, &#39;after/ftdetect/**/*.vim&#39;)
    381 <a href="#l362" class="line" id="l362">    362</a>         if has(&#39;nvim-0.5.0&#39;)
    382 <a href="#l363" class="line" id="l363">    363</a>           call s:source(s:rtp(plug), &#39;ftdetect/**/*.lua&#39;, &#39;after/ftdetect/**/*.lua&#39;)
    383 <a href="#l364" class="line" id="l364">    364</a>         endif
    384 <a href="#l365" class="line" id="l365">    365</a>         augroup END
    385 <a href="#l366" class="line" id="l366">    366</a>       endif
    386 <a href="#l367" class="line" id="l367">    367</a>       for type in types
    387 <a href="#l368" class="line" id="l368">    368</a>         call s:assoc(lod.ft, type, name)
    388 <a href="#l369" class="line" id="l369">    369</a>       endfor
    389 <a href="#l370" class="line" id="l370">    370</a>     endif
    390 <a href="#l371" class="line" id="l371">    371</a>   endfor
    391 <a href="#l372" class="line" id="l372">    372</a> 
    392 <a href="#l373" class="line" id="l373">    373</a>   for [cmd, names] in items(lod.cmd)
    393 <a href="#l374" class="line" id="l374">    374</a>     execute printf(
    394 <a href="#l375" class="line" id="l375">    375</a>     \ has(&#39;patch-7.4.1898&#39;)
    395 <a href="#l376" class="line" id="l376">    376</a>     \ ? &#39;command! -nargs=* -range -bang -complete=file %s call s:lod_cmd(%s, &quot;&lt;bang&gt;&quot;, &lt;line1&gt;, &lt;line2&gt;, &lt;q-args&gt;, &lt;q-mods&gt; ,%s)&#39;
    396 <a href="#l377" class="line" id="l377">    377</a>     \ : &#39;command! -nargs=* -range -bang -complete=file %s call s:lod_cmd(%s, &quot;&lt;bang&gt;&quot;, &lt;line1&gt;, &lt;line2&gt;, &lt;q-args&gt;, %s)&#39;
    397 <a href="#l378" class="line" id="l378">    378</a>     \ , cmd, string(cmd), string(names))
    398 <a href="#l379" class="line" id="l379">    379</a>   endfor
    399 <a href="#l380" class="line" id="l380">    380</a> 
    400 <a href="#l381" class="line" id="l381">    381</a>   for [map, names] in items(lod.map)
    401 <a href="#l382" class="line" id="l382">    382</a>     for [mode, map_prefix, key_prefix] in
    402 <a href="#l383" class="line" id="l383">    383</a>           \ [[&#39;i&#39;, &#39;&lt;C-\&gt;&lt;C-O&gt;&#39;, &#39;&#39;], [&#39;n&#39;, &#39;&#39;, &#39;&#39;], [&#39;v&#39;, &#39;&#39;, &#39;gv&#39;], [&#39;o&#39;, &#39;&#39;, &#39;&#39;]]
    403 <a href="#l384" class="line" id="l384">    384</a>       execute printf(
    404 <a href="#l385" class="line" id="l385">    385</a>       \ &#39;%snoremap &lt;silent&gt; %s %s:&lt;C-U&gt;call &lt;SID&gt;lod_map(%s, %s, %s, &quot;%s&quot;)&lt;CR&gt;&#39;,
    405 <a href="#l386" class="line" id="l386">    386</a>       \ mode, map, map_prefix, string(map), string(names), mode != &#39;i&#39;, key_prefix)
    406 <a href="#l387" class="line" id="l387">    387</a>     endfor
    407 <a href="#l388" class="line" id="l388">    388</a>   endfor
    408 <a href="#l389" class="line" id="l389">    389</a> 
    409 <a href="#l390" class="line" id="l390">    390</a>   for [ft, names] in items(lod.ft)
    410 <a href="#l391" class="line" id="l391">    391</a>     augroup PlugLOD
    411 <a href="#l392" class="line" id="l392">    392</a>       execute printf(&#39;autocmd FileType %s call &lt;SID&gt;lod_ft(%s, %s)&#39;,
    412 <a href="#l393" class="line" id="l393">    393</a>             \ ft, string(ft), string(names))
    413 <a href="#l394" class="line" id="l394">    394</a>     augroup END
    414 <a href="#l395" class="line" id="l395">    395</a>   endfor
    415 <a href="#l396" class="line" id="l396">    396</a> 
    416 <a href="#l397" class="line" id="l397">    397</a>   call s:reorg_rtp()
    417 <a href="#l398" class="line" id="l398">    398</a>   filetype plugin indent on
    418 <a href="#l399" class="line" id="l399">    399</a>   if has(&#39;vim_starting&#39;)
    419 <a href="#l400" class="line" id="l400">    400</a>     if has(&#39;syntax&#39;) &amp;&amp; !exists(&#39;g:syntax_on&#39;)
    420 <a href="#l401" class="line" id="l401">    401</a>       syntax enable
    421 <a href="#l402" class="line" id="l402">    402</a>     end
    422 <a href="#l403" class="line" id="l403">    403</a>   else
    423 <a href="#l404" class="line" id="l404">    404</a>     call s:reload_plugins()
    424 <a href="#l405" class="line" id="l405">    405</a>   endif
    425 <a href="#l406" class="line" id="l406">    406</a> endfunction
    426 <a href="#l407" class="line" id="l407">    407</a> 
    427 <a href="#l408" class="line" id="l408">    408</a> function! s:loaded_names()
    428 <a href="#l409" class="line" id="l409">    409</a>   return filter(copy(g:plugs_order), &#39;get(s:loaded, v:val, 0)&#39;)
    429 <a href="#l410" class="line" id="l410">    410</a> endfunction

    431 <a href="#l412" class="line" id="l412">    412</a> function! s:load_plugin(spec)
    432 <a href="#l413" class="line" id="l413">    413</a>   call s:source(s:rtp(a:spec), &#39;plugin/**/*.vim&#39;, &#39;after/plugin/**/*.vim&#39;)
    433 <a href="#l414" class="line" id="l414">    414</a>   if has(&#39;nvim-0.5.0&#39;)
    434 <a href="#l415" class="line" id="l415">    415</a>     call s:source(s:rtp(a:spec), &#39;plugin/**/*.lua&#39;, &#39;after/plugin/**/*.lua&#39;)
    435 <a href="#l416" class="line" id="l416">    416</a>   endif
    436 <a href="#l417" class="line" id="l417">    417</a> endfunction

    447 <a href="#l428" class="line" id="l428">    428</a> 
    448 <a href="#l429" class="line" id="l429">    429</a> function! s:version_requirement(val, min)
    449 <a href="#l430" class="line" id="l430">    430</a>   for idx in range(0, len(a:min) - 1)
    450 <a href="#l431" class="line" id="l431">    431</a>     let v = get(a:val, idx, 0)
    451 <a href="#l432" class="line" id="l432">    432</a>     if     v &lt; a:min[idx] | return 0
    452 <a href="#l433" class="line" id="l433">    433</a>     elseif v &gt; a:min[idx] | return 1
    453 <a href="#l434" class="line" id="l434">    434</a>     endif
    454 <a href="#l435" class="line" id="l435">    435</a>   endfor
    455 <a href="#l436" class="line" id="l436">    436</a>   return 1
    456 <a href="#l437" class="line" id="l437">    437</a> endfunction
    457 <a href="#l438" class="line" id="l438">    438</a> 
    458 <a href="#l439" class="line" id="l439">    439</a> function! s:git_version_requirement(...)
    459 <a href="#l440" class="line" id="l440">    440</a>   if !exists(&#39;s:git_version&#39;)
    460 <a href="#l441" class="line" id="l441">    441</a>     let s:git_version = map(split(split(s:system([&#39;git&#39;, &#39;--version&#39;]))[2], &#39;\.&#39;), &#39;str2nr(v:val)&#39;)
    461 <a href="#l442" class="line" id="l442">    442</a>   endif
    462 <a href="#l443" class="line" id="l443">    443</a>   return s:version_requirement(s:git_version, a:000)
    463 <a href="#l444" class="line" id="l444">    444</a> endfunction

    487 <a href="#l468" class="line" id="l468">    468</a>   &quot; Copied from fzf
    488 <a href="#l469" class="line" id="l469">    469</a>   function! s:wrap_cmds(cmds)
    489 <a href="#l470" class="line" id="l470">    470</a>     let cmds = [
    490 <a href="#l471" class="line" id="l471">    471</a>       \ &#39;@echo off&#39;,
    491 <a href="#l472" class="line" id="l472">    472</a>       \ &#39;setlocal enabledelayedexpansion&#39;]
    492 <a href="#l473" class="line" id="l473">    473</a>     \ + (type(a:cmds) == type([]) ? a:cmds : [a:cmds])
    493 <a href="#l474" class="line" id="l474">    474</a>     \ + [&#39;endlocal&#39;]
    494 <a href="#l475" class="line" id="l475">    475</a>     if has(&#39;iconv&#39;)
    495 <a href="#l476" class="line" id="l476">    476</a>       if !exists(&#39;s:codepage&#39;)
    496 <a href="#l477" class="line" id="l477">    477</a>         let s:codepage = libcallnr(&#39;kernel32.dll&#39;, &#39;GetACP&#39;, 0)
    497 <a href="#l478" class="line" id="l478">    478</a>       endif
    498 <a href="#l479" class="line" id="l479">    479</a>       return map(cmds, printf(&#39;iconv(v:val.&quot;\r&quot;, &quot;%s&quot;, &quot;cp%d&quot;)&#39;, &amp;encoding, s:codepage))
    499 <a href="#l480" class="line" id="l480">    480</a>     endif
    500 <a href="#l481" class="line" id="l481">    481</a>     return map(cmds, &#39;v:val.&quot;\r&quot;&#39;)
    501 <a href="#l482" class="line" id="l482">    482</a>   endfunction

    506 <a href="#l487" class="line" id="l487">    487</a>     let cmd = plug#shellescape(batchfile, {&#39;shell&#39;: &amp;shell, &#39;script&#39;: 0})
    507 <a href="#l488" class="line" id="l488">    488</a>     if s:is_powershell(&amp;shell)

    542 <a href="#l523" class="line" id="l523">    523</a> function! s:escrtp(path)
    543 <a href="#l524" class="line" id="l524">    524</a>   return escape(a:path, &#39; ,&#39;)

    545 <a href="#l526" class="line" id="l526">    526</a> 
    546 <a href="#l527" class="line" id="l527">    527</a> function! s:remove_rtp()
    547 <a href="#l528" class="line" id="l528">    528</a>   for name in s:loaded_names()
    548 <a href="#l529" class="line" id="l529">    529</a>     let rtp = s:rtp(g:plugs[name])
    549 <a href="#l530" class="line" id="l530">    530</a>     execute &#39;set rtp-=&#39;.s:escrtp(rtp)
    550 <a href="#l531" class="line" id="l531">    531</a>     let after = globpath(rtp, &#39;after&#39;)
    551 <a href="#l532" class="line" id="l532">    532</a>     if isdirectory(after)
    552 <a href="#l533" class="line" id="l533">    533</a>       execute &#39;set rtp-=&#39;.s:escrtp(after)
    553 <a href="#l534" class="line" id="l534">    534</a>     endif
    554 <a href="#l535" class="line" id="l535">    535</a>   endfor
    555 <a href="#l536" class="line" id="l536">    536</a> endfunction
    556 <a href="#l537" class="line" id="l537">    537</a> 
    557 <a href="#l538" class="line" id="l538">    538</a> function! s:reorg_rtp()
    558 <a href="#l539" class="line" id="l539">    539</a>   if !empty(s:first_rtp)
    559 <a href="#l540" class="line" id="l540">    540</a>     execute &#39;set rtp-=&#39;.s:first_rtp
    560 <a href="#l541" class="line" id="l541">    541</a>     execute &#39;set rtp-=&#39;.s:last_rtp
    561 <a href="#l542" class="line" id="l542">    542</a>   endif
    562 <a href="#l543" class="line" id="l543">    543</a> 
    563 <a href="#l544" class="line" id="l544">    544</a>   &quot; &amp;rtp is modified from outside
    564 <a href="#l545" class="line" id="l545">    545</a>   if exists(&#39;s:prtp&#39;) &amp;&amp; s:prtp !=# &amp;rtp
    565 <a href="#l546" class="line" id="l546">    546</a>     call s:remove_rtp()
    566 <a href="#l547" class="line" id="l547">    547</a>     unlet! s:middle
    567 <a href="#l548" class="line" id="l548">    548</a>   endif
    568 <a href="#l549" class="line" id="l549">    549</a> 
    569 <a href="#l550" class="line" id="l550">    550</a>   let s:middle = get(s:, &#39;middle&#39;, &amp;rtp)
    570 <a href="#l551" class="line" id="l551">    551</a>   let rtps     = map(s:loaded_names(), &#39;s:rtp(g:plugs[v:val])&#39;)
    571 <a href="#l552" class="line" id="l552">    552</a>   let afters   = filter(map(copy(rtps), &#39;globpath(v:val, &quot;after&quot;)&#39;), &#39;!empty(v:val)&#39;)
    572 <a href="#l553" class="line" id="l553">    553</a>   let rtp      = join(map(rtps, &#39;escape(v:val, &quot;,&quot;)&#39;), &#39;,&#39;)
    573 <a href="#l554" class="line" id="l554">    554</a>                  \ . &#39;,&#39;.s:middle.&#39;,&#39;
    574 <a href="#l555" class="line" id="l555">    555</a>                  \ . join(map(afters, &#39;escape(v:val, &quot;,&quot;)&#39;), &#39;,&#39;)
    575 <a href="#l556" class="line" id="l556">    556</a>   let &amp;rtp     = substitute(substitute(rtp, &#39;,,*&#39;, &#39;,&#39;, &#39;g&#39;), &#39;^,\|,$&#39;, &#39;&#39;, &#39;g&#39;)
    576 <a href="#l557" class="line" id="l557">    557</a>   let s:prtp   = &amp;rtp
    577 <a href="#l558" class="line" id="l558">    558</a> 
    578 <a href="#l559" class="line" id="l559">    559</a>   if !empty(s:first_rtp)
    579 <a href="#l560" class="line" id="l560">    560</a>     execute &#39;set rtp^=&#39;.s:first_rtp
    580 <a href="#l561" class="line" id="l561">    561</a>     execute &#39;set rtp+=&#39;.s:last_rtp
    581 <a href="#l562" class="line" id="l562">    562</a>   endif
    582 <a href="#l563" class="line" id="l563">    563</a> endfunction
    583 <a href="#l564" class="line" id="l564">    564</a> 
    584 <a href="#l565" class="line" id="l565">    565</a> function! s:doautocmd(...)
    585 <a href="#l566" class="line" id="l566">    566</a>   if exists(&#39;#&#39;.join(a:000, &#39;#&#39;))
    586 <a href="#l567" class="line" id="l567">    567</a>     execute &#39;doautocmd&#39; ((v:version &gt; 703 || has(&#39;patch442&#39;)) ? &#39;&lt;nomodeline&gt;&#39; : &#39;&#39;) join(a:000)
    587 <a href="#l568" class="line" id="l568">    568</a>   endif
    588 <a href="#l569" class="line" id="l569">    569</a> endfunction
    589 <a href="#l570" class="line" id="l570">    570</a> 
    590 <a href="#l571" class="line" id="l571">    571</a> function! s:dobufread(names)
    591 <a href="#l572" class="line" id="l572">    572</a>   for name in a:names
    592 <a href="#l573" class="line" id="l573">    573</a>     let path = s:rtp(g:plugs[name])
    593 <a href="#l574" class="line" id="l574">    574</a>     for dir in [&#39;ftdetect&#39;, &#39;ftplugin&#39;, &#39;after/ftdetect&#39;, &#39;after/ftplugin&#39;]
    594 <a href="#l575" class="line" id="l575">    575</a>       if len(finddir(dir, path))
    595 <a href="#l576" class="line" id="l576">    576</a>         if exists(&#39;#BufRead&#39;)
    596 <a href="#l577" class="line" id="l577">    577</a>           doautocmd BufRead
    597 <a href="#l578" class="line" id="l578">    578</a>         endif
    598 <a href="#l579" class="line" id="l579">    579</a>         return
    599 <a href="#l580" class="line" id="l580">    580</a>       endif
    600 <a href="#l581" class="line" id="l581">    581</a>     endfor
    601 <a href="#l582" class="line" id="l582">    582</a>   endfor
    602 <a href="#l583" class="line" id="l583">    583</a> endfunction
    603 <a href="#l584" class="line" id="l584">    584</a> 
    604 <a href="#l585" class="line" id="l585">    585</a> function! plug#load(...)
    605 <a href="#l586" class="line" id="l586">    586</a>   if a:0 == 0
    606 <a href="#l587" class="line" id="l587">    587</a>     return s:err(&#39;Argument missing: plugin name(s) required&#39;)
    607 <a href="#l588" class="line" id="l588">    588</a>   endif
    608 <a href="#l589" class="line" id="l589">    589</a>   if !exists(&#39;g:plugs&#39;)
    609 <a href="#l590" class="line" id="l590">    590</a>     return s:err(&#39;plug#begin was not called&#39;)
    610 <a href="#l591" class="line" id="l591">    591</a>   endif
    611 <a href="#l592" class="line" id="l592">    592</a>   let names = a:0 == 1 &amp;&amp; type(a:1) == s:TYPE.list ? a:1 : a:000
    612 <a href="#l593" class="line" id="l593">    593</a>   let unknowns = filter(copy(names), &#39;!has_key(g:plugs, v:val)&#39;)
    613 <a href="#l594" class="line" id="l594">    594</a>   if !empty(unknowns)
    614 <a href="#l595" class="line" id="l595">    595</a>     let s = len(unknowns) &gt; 1 ? &#39;s&#39; : &#39;&#39;
    615 <a href="#l596" class="line" id="l596">    596</a>     return s:err(printf(&#39;Unknown plugin%s: %s&#39;, s, join(unknowns, &#39;, &#39;)))
    616 <a href="#l597" class="line" id="l597">    597</a>   end
    617 <a href="#l598" class="line" id="l598">    598</a>   let unloaded = filter(copy(names), &#39;!get(s:loaded, v:val, 0)&#39;)
    618 <a href="#l599" class="line" id="l599">    599</a>   if !empty(unloaded)
    619 <a href="#l600" class="line" id="l600">    600</a>     for name in unloaded
    620 <a href="#l601" class="line" id="l601">    601</a>       call s:lod([name], [&#39;ftdetect&#39;, &#39;after/ftdetect&#39;, &#39;plugin&#39;, &#39;after/plugin&#39;])
    621 <a href="#l602" class="line" id="l602">    602</a>     endfor
    622 <a href="#l603" class="line" id="l603">    603</a>     call s:dobufread(unloaded)
    623 <a href="#l604" class="line" id="l604">    604</a>     return 1
    624 <a href="#l605" class="line" id="l605">    605</a>   end
    625 <a href="#l606" class="line" id="l606">    606</a>   return 0
    626 <a href="#l607" class="line" id="l607">    607</a> endfunction
    627 <a href="#l608" class="line" id="l608">    608</a> 
    628 <a href="#l609" class="line" id="l609">    609</a> function! s:remove_triggers(name)
    629 <a href="#l610" class="line" id="l610">    610</a>   if !has_key(s:triggers, a:name)
    630 <a href="#l611" class="line" id="l611">    611</a>     return
    631 <a href="#l612" class="line" id="l612">    612</a>   endif
    632 <a href="#l613" class="line" id="l613">    613</a>   for cmd in s:triggers[a:name].cmd
    633 <a href="#l614" class="line" id="l614">    614</a>     execute &#39;silent! delc&#39; cmd
    634 <a href="#l615" class="line" id="l615">    615</a>   endfor
    635 <a href="#l616" class="line" id="l616">    616</a>   for map in s:triggers[a:name].map
    636 <a href="#l617" class="line" id="l617">    617</a>     execute &#39;silent! unmap&#39; map
    637 <a href="#l618" class="line" id="l618">    618</a>     execute &#39;silent! iunmap&#39; map
    638 <a href="#l619" class="line" id="l619">    619</a>   endfor
    639 <a href="#l620" class="line" id="l620">    620</a>   call remove(s:triggers, a:name)
    640 <a href="#l621" class="line" id="l621">    621</a> endfunction
    641 <a href="#l622" class="line" id="l622">    622</a> 
    642 <a href="#l623" class="line" id="l623">    623</a> function! s:lod(names, types, ...)
    643 <a href="#l624" class="line" id="l624">    624</a>   for name in a:names
    644 <a href="#l625" class="line" id="l625">    625</a>     call s:remove_triggers(name)
    645 <a href="#l626" class="line" id="l626">    626</a>     let s:loaded[name] = 1
    646 <a href="#l627" class="line" id="l627">    627</a>   endfor
    647 <a href="#l628" class="line" id="l628">    628</a>   call s:reorg_rtp()
    648 <a href="#l629" class="line" id="l629">    629</a> 
    649 <a href="#l630" class="line" id="l630">    630</a>   for name in a:names
    650 <a href="#l631" class="line" id="l631">    631</a>     let rtp = s:rtp(g:plugs[name])
    651 <a href="#l632" class="line" id="l632">    632</a>     for dir in a:types
    652 <a href="#l633" class="line" id="l633">    633</a>       call s:source(rtp, dir.&#39;/**/*.vim&#39;)
    653 <a href="#l634" class="line" id="l634">    634</a>       if has(&#39;nvim-0.5.0&#39;)  &quot; see neovim#14686
    654 <a href="#l635" class="line" id="l635">    635</a>         call s:source(rtp, dir.&#39;/**/*.lua&#39;)
    655 <a href="#l636" class="line" id="l636">    636</a>       endif
    656 <a href="#l637" class="line" id="l637">    637</a>     endfor
    657 <a href="#l638" class="line" id="l638">    638</a>     if a:0
    658 <a href="#l639" class="line" id="l639">    639</a>       if !s:source(rtp, a:1) &amp;&amp; !empty(s:glob(rtp, a:2))
    659 <a href="#l640" class="line" id="l640">    640</a>         execute &#39;runtime&#39; a:1
    660 <a href="#l641" class="line" id="l641">    641</a>       endif
    661 <a href="#l642" class="line" id="l642">    642</a>       call s:source(rtp, a:2)
    662 <a href="#l643" class="line" id="l643">    643</a>     endif
    663 <a href="#l644" class="line" id="l644">    644</a>     call s:doautocmd(&#39;User&#39;, name)
    664 <a href="#l645" class="line" id="l645">    645</a>   endfor
    665 <a href="#l646" class="line" id="l646">    646</a> endfunction
    666 <a href="#l647" class="line" id="l647">    647</a> 
    667 <a href="#l648" class="line" id="l648">    648</a> function! s:lod_ft(pat, names)
    668 <a href="#l649" class="line" id="l649">    649</a>   let syn = &#39;syntax/&#39;.a:pat.&#39;.vim&#39;
    669 <a href="#l650" class="line" id="l650">    650</a>   call s:lod(a:names, [&#39;plugin&#39;, &#39;after/plugin&#39;], syn, &#39;after/&#39;.syn)
    670 <a href="#l651" class="line" id="l651">    651</a>   execute &#39;autocmd! PlugLOD FileType&#39; a:pat
    671 <a href="#l652" class="line" id="l652">    652</a>   call s:doautocmd(&#39;filetypeplugin&#39;, &#39;FileType&#39;)
    672 <a href="#l653" class="line" id="l653">    653</a>   call s:doautocmd(&#39;filetypeindent&#39;, &#39;FileType&#39;)
    673 <a href="#l654" class="line" id="l654">    654</a> endfunction
    674 <a href="#l655" class="line" id="l655">    655</a> 
    675 <a href="#l656" class="line" id="l656">    656</a> if has(&#39;patch-7.4.1898&#39;)
    676 <a href="#l657" class="line" id="l657">    657</a>   function! s:lod_cmd(cmd, bang, l1, l2, args, mods, names)
    677 <a href="#l658" class="line" id="l658">    658</a>     call s:lod(a:names, [&#39;ftdetect&#39;, &#39;after/ftdetect&#39;, &#39;plugin&#39;, &#39;after/plugin&#39;])
    678 <a href="#l659" class="line" id="l659">    659</a>     call s:dobufread(a:names)
    679 <a href="#l660" class="line" id="l660">    660</a>     execute printf(&#39;%s %s%s%s %s&#39;, a:mods, (a:l1 == a:l2 ? &#39;&#39; : (a:l1.&#39;,&#39;.a:l2)), a:cmd, a:bang, a:args)
    680 <a href="#l661" class="line" id="l661">    661</a>   endfunction
    681 <a href="#l662" class="line" id="l662">    662</a> else
    682 <a href="#l663" class="line" id="l663">    663</a>   function! s:lod_cmd(cmd, bang, l1, l2, args, names)
    683 <a href="#l664" class="line" id="l664">    664</a>     call s:lod(a:names, [&#39;ftdetect&#39;, &#39;after/ftdetect&#39;, &#39;plugin&#39;, &#39;after/plugin&#39;])
    684 <a href="#l665" class="line" id="l665">    665</a>     call s:dobufread(a:names)
    685 <a href="#l666" class="line" id="l666">    666</a>     execute printf(&#39;%s%s%s %s&#39;, (a:l1 == a:l2 ? &#39;&#39; : (a:l1.&#39;,&#39;.a:l2)), a:cmd, a:bang, a:args)
    686 <a href="#l667" class="line" id="l667">    667</a>   endfunction
    687 <a href="#l668" class="line" id="l668">    668</a> endif
    688 <a href="#l669" class="line" id="l669">    669</a> 
    689 <a href="#l670" class="line" id="l670">    670</a> function! s:lod_map(map, names, with_prefix, prefix)
    690 <a href="#l671" class="line" id="l671">    671</a>   call s:lod(a:names, [&#39;ftdetect&#39;, &#39;after/ftdetect&#39;, &#39;plugin&#39;, &#39;after/plugin&#39;])
    691 <a href="#l672" class="line" id="l672">    672</a>   call s:dobufread(a:names)
    692 <a href="#l673" class="line" id="l673">    673</a>   let extra = &#39;&#39;
    693 <a href="#l674" class="line" id="l674">    674</a>   while 1
    694 <a href="#l675" class="line" id="l675">    675</a>     let c = getchar(0)
    695 <a href="#l676" class="line" id="l676">    676</a>     if c == 0
    696 <a href="#l677" class="line" id="l677">    677</a>       break
    697 <a href="#l678" class="line" id="l678">    678</a>     endif
    698 <a href="#l679" class="line" id="l679">    679</a>     let extra .= nr2char(c)
    699 <a href="#l680" class="line" id="l680">    680</a>   endwhile
    700 <a href="#l681" class="line" id="l681">    681</a> 
    701 <a href="#l682" class="line" id="l682">    682</a>   if a:with_prefix
    702 <a href="#l683" class="line" id="l683">    683</a>     let prefix = v:count ? v:count : &#39;&#39;
    703 <a href="#l684" class="line" id="l684">    684</a>     let prefix .= &#39;&quot;&#39;.v:register.a:prefix
    704 <a href="#l685" class="line" id="l685">    685</a>     if mode(1) == &#39;no&#39;
    705 <a href="#l686" class="line" id="l686">    686</a>       if v:operator == &#39;c&#39;
    706 <a href="#l687" class="line" id="l687">    687</a>         let prefix = &quot;\&lt;esc&gt;&quot; . prefix
    707 <a href="#l688" class="line" id="l688">    688</a>       endif
    708 <a href="#l689" class="line" id="l689">    689</a>       let prefix .= v:operator
    709 <a href="#l690" class="line" id="l690">    690</a>     endif
    710 <a href="#l691" class="line" id="l691">    691</a>     call feedkeys(prefix, &#39;n&#39;)
    711 <a href="#l692" class="line" id="l692">    692</a>   endif
    712 <a href="#l693" class="line" id="l693">    693</a>   call feedkeys(substitute(a:map, &#39;^&lt;Plug&gt;&#39;, &quot;\&lt;Plug&gt;&quot;, &#39;&#39;) . extra)
    713 <a href="#l694" class="line" id="l694">    694</a> endfunction
    714 <a href="#l695" class="line" id="l695">    695</a> 
    715 <a href="#l696" class="line" id="l696">    696</a> function! plug#(repo, ...)
    716 <a href="#l697" class="line" id="l697">    697</a>   if a:0 &gt; 1
    717 <a href="#l698" class="line" id="l698">    698</a>     return s:err(&#39;Invalid number of arguments (1..2)&#39;)
    718 <a href="#l699" class="line" id="l699">    699</a>   endif
    719 <a href="#l700" class="line" id="l700">    700</a> 
    720 <a href="#l701" class="line" id="l701">    701</a>   try
    721 <a href="#l702" class="line" id="l702">    702</a>     let repo = s:trim(a:repo)
    722 <a href="#l703" class="line" id="l703">    703</a>     let opts = a:0 == 1 ? s:parse_options(a:1) : s:base_spec
    723 <a href="#l704" class="line" id="l704">    704</a>     let name = get(opts, &#39;as&#39;, s:plug_fnamemodify(repo, &#39;:t:s?\.git$??&#39;))
    724 <a href="#l705" class="line" id="l705">    705</a>     let spec = extend(s:infer_properties(name, repo), opts)
    725 <a href="#l706" class="line" id="l706">    706</a>     if !has_key(g:plugs, name)
    726 <a href="#l707" class="line" id="l707">    707</a>       call add(g:plugs_order, name)
    727 <a href="#l708" class="line" id="l708">    708</a>     endif
    728 <a href="#l709" class="line" id="l709">    709</a>     let g:plugs[name] = spec
    729 <a href="#l710" class="line" id="l710">    710</a>     let s:loaded[name] = get(s:loaded, name, 0)
    730 <a href="#l711" class="line" id="l711">    711</a>   catch
    731 <a href="#l712" class="line" id="l712">    712</a>     return s:err(repo . &#39; &#39; . v:exception)
    732 <a href="#l713" class="line" id="l713">    713</a>   endtry
    733 <a href="#l714" class="line" id="l714">    714</a> endfunction
    734 <a href="#l715" class="line" id="l715">    715</a> 
    735 <a href="#l716" class="line" id="l716">    716</a> function! s:parse_options(arg)
    736 <a href="#l717" class="line" id="l717">    717</a>   let opts = copy(s:base_spec)
    737 <a href="#l718" class="line" id="l718">    718</a>   let type = type(a:arg)
    738 <a href="#l719" class="line" id="l719">    719</a>   let opt_errfmt = &#39;Invalid argument for &quot;%s&quot; option of :Plug (expected: %s)&#39;
    739 <a href="#l720" class="line" id="l720">    720</a>   if type == s:TYPE.string
    740 <a href="#l721" class="line" id="l721">    721</a>     if empty(a:arg)
    741 <a href="#l722" class="line" id="l722">    722</a>       throw printf(opt_errfmt, &#39;tag&#39;, &#39;string&#39;)
    742 <a href="#l723" class="line" id="l723">    723</a>     endif
    743 <a href="#l724" class="line" id="l724">    724</a>     let opts.tag = a:arg
    744 <a href="#l725" class="line" id="l725">    725</a>   elseif type == s:TYPE.dict
    745 <a href="#l726" class="line" id="l726">    726</a>     for opt in [&#39;branch&#39;, &#39;tag&#39;, &#39;commit&#39;, &#39;rtp&#39;, &#39;dir&#39;, &#39;as&#39;]
    746 <a href="#l727" class="line" id="l727">    727</a>       if has_key(a:arg, opt)
    747 <a href="#l728" class="line" id="l728">    728</a>       \ &amp;&amp; (type(a:arg[opt]) != s:TYPE.string || empty(a:arg[opt]))
    748 <a href="#l729" class="line" id="l729">    729</a>         throw printf(opt_errfmt, opt, &#39;string&#39;)
    749 <a href="#l730" class="line" id="l730">    730</a>       endif
    750 <a href="#l731" class="line" id="l731">    731</a>     endfor
    751 <a href="#l732" class="line" id="l732">    732</a>     for opt in [&#39;on&#39;, &#39;for&#39;]
    752 <a href="#l733" class="line" id="l733">    733</a>       if has_key(a:arg, opt)
    753 <a href="#l734" class="line" id="l734">    734</a>       \ &amp;&amp; type(a:arg[opt]) != s:TYPE.list
    754 <a href="#l735" class="line" id="l735">    735</a>       \ &amp;&amp; (type(a:arg[opt]) != s:TYPE.string || empty(a:arg[opt]))
    755 <a href="#l736" class="line" id="l736">    736</a>         throw printf(opt_errfmt, opt, &#39;string or list&#39;)
    756 <a href="#l737" class="line" id="l737">    737</a>       endif
    757 <a href="#l738" class="line" id="l738">    738</a>     endfor
    758 <a href="#l739" class="line" id="l739">    739</a>     if has_key(a:arg, &#39;do&#39;)
    759 <a href="#l740" class="line" id="l740">    740</a>       \ &amp;&amp; type(a:arg.do) != s:TYPE.funcref
    760 <a href="#l741" class="line" id="l741">    741</a>       \ &amp;&amp; (type(a:arg.do) != s:TYPE.string || empty(a:arg.do))
    761 <a href="#l742" class="line" id="l742">    742</a>         throw printf(opt_errfmt, &#39;do&#39;, &#39;string or funcref&#39;)
    762 <a href="#l743" class="line" id="l743">    743</a>     endif
    763 <a href="#l744" class="line" id="l744">    744</a>     call extend(opts, a:arg)
    764 <a href="#l745" class="line" id="l745">    745</a>     if has_key(opts, &#39;dir&#39;)
    765 <a href="#l746" class="line" id="l746">    746</a>       let opts.dir = s:dirpath(s:plug_expand(opts.dir))
    766 <a href="#l747" class="line" id="l747">    747</a>     endif
    767 <a href="#l748" class="line" id="l748">    748</a>   else
    768 <a href="#l749" class="line" id="l749">    749</a>     throw &#39;Invalid argument type (expected: string or dictionary)&#39;
    769 <a href="#l750" class="line" id="l750">    750</a>   endif
    770 <a href="#l751" class="line" id="l751">    751</a>   return opts
    771 <a href="#l752" class="line" id="l752">    752</a> endfunction
    772 <a href="#l753" class="line" id="l753">    753</a> 
    773 <a href="#l754" class="line" id="l754">    754</a> function! s:infer_properties(name, repo)
    774 <a href="#l755" class="line" id="l755">    755</a>   let repo = a:repo
    775 <a href="#l756" class="line" id="l756">    756</a>   if s:is_local_plug(repo)
    776 <a href="#l757" class="line" id="l757">    757</a>     return { &#39;dir&#39;: s:dirpath(s:plug_expand(repo)) }
    777 <a href="#l758" class="line" id="l758">    758</a>   else
    778 <a href="#l759" class="line" id="l759">    759</a>     if repo =~ &#39;:&#39;
    779 <a href="#l760" class="line" id="l760">    760</a>       let uri = repo
    780 <a href="#l761" class="line" id="l761">    761</a>     else
    781 <a href="#l762" class="line" id="l762">    762</a>       if repo !~ &#39;/&#39;
    782 <a href="#l763" class="line" id="l763">    763</a>         throw printf(&#39;Invalid argument: %s (implicit `vim-scripts&#39;&#39; expansion is deprecated)&#39;, repo)
    783 <a href="#l764" class="line" id="l764">    764</a>       endif
    784 <a href="#l765" class="line" id="l765">    765</a>       let fmt = get(g:, &#39;plug_url_format&#39;, &#39;https://git::@github.com/%s.git&#39;)
    785 <a href="#l766" class="line" id="l766">    766</a>       let uri = printf(fmt, repo)
    786 <a href="#l767" class="line" id="l767">    767</a>     endif
    787 <a href="#l768" class="line" id="l768">    768</a>     return { &#39;dir&#39;: s:dirpath(g:plug_home.&#39;/&#39;.a:name), &#39;uri&#39;: uri }
    788 <a href="#l769" class="line" id="l769">    769</a>   endif
    789 <a href="#l770" class="line" id="l770">    770</a> endfunction
    790 <a href="#l771" class="line" id="l771">    771</a> 
    791 <a href="#l772" class="line" id="l772">    772</a> function! s:install(force, names)
    792 <a href="#l773" class="line" id="l773">    773</a>   call s:update_impl(0, a:force, a:names)
    793 <a href="#l774" class="line" id="l774">    774</a> endfunction
    794 <a href="#l775" class="line" id="l775">    775</a> 
    795 <a href="#l776" class="line" id="l776">    776</a> function! s:update(force, names)
    796 <a href="#l777" class="line" id="l777">    777</a>   call s:update_impl(1, a:force, a:names)
    797 <a href="#l778" class="line" id="l778">    778</a> endfunction
    798 <a href="#l779" class="line" id="l779">    779</a> 
    799 <a href="#l780" class="line" id="l780">    780</a> function! plug#helptags()
    800 <a href="#l781" class="line" id="l781">    781</a>   if !exists(&#39;g:plugs&#39;)
    801 <a href="#l782" class="line" id="l782">    782</a>     return s:err(&#39;plug#begin was not called&#39;)
    802 <a href="#l783" class="line" id="l783">    783</a>   endif
    803 <a href="#l784" class="line" id="l784">    784</a>   for spec in values(g:plugs)
    804 <a href="#l785" class="line" id="l785">    785</a>     let docd = join([s:rtp(spec), &#39;doc&#39;], &#39;/&#39;)
    805 <a href="#l786" class="line" id="l786">    786</a>     if isdirectory(docd)
    806 <a href="#l787" class="line" id="l787">    787</a>       silent! execute &#39;helptags&#39; s:esc(docd)
    807 <a href="#l788" class="line" id="l788">    788</a>     endif
    808 <a href="#l789" class="line" id="l789">    789</a>   endfor
    809 <a href="#l790" class="line" id="l790">    790</a>   return 1
    810 <a href="#l791" class="line" id="l791">    791</a> endfunction
    811 <a href="#l792" class="line" id="l792">    792</a> 
    812 <a href="#l793" class="line" id="l793">    793</a> function! s:syntax()
    813 <a href="#l794" class="line" id="l794">    794</a>   syntax clear
    814 <a href="#l795" class="line" id="l795">    795</a>   syntax region plug1 start=/\%1l/ end=/\%2l/ contains=plugNumber
    815 <a href="#l796" class="line" id="l796">    796</a>   syntax region plug2 start=/\%2l/ end=/\%3l/ contains=plugBracket,plugX,plugAbort
    816 <a href="#l797" class="line" id="l797">    797</a>   syn match plugNumber /[0-9]\+[0-9.]*/ contained
    817 <a href="#l798" class="line" id="l798">    798</a>   syn match plugBracket /[[\]]/ contained
    818 <a href="#l799" class="line" id="l799">    799</a>   syn match plugX /x/ contained
    819 <a href="#l800" class="line" id="l800">    800</a>   syn match plugAbort /\~/ contained
    820 <a href="#l801" class="line" id="l801">    801</a>   syn match plugDash /^-\{1}\ /
    821 <a href="#l802" class="line" id="l802">    802</a>   syn match plugPlus /^+/
    822 <a href="#l803" class="line" id="l803">    803</a>   syn match plugStar /^*/
    823 <a href="#l804" class="line" id="l804">    804</a>   syn match plugMessage /\(^- \)\@&lt;=.*/
    824 <a href="#l805" class="line" id="l805">    805</a>   syn match plugName /\(^- \)\@&lt;=[^ ]*:/
    825 <a href="#l806" class="line" id="l806">    806</a>   syn match plugSha /\%(: \)\@&lt;=[0-9a-f]\{4,}$/
    826 <a href="#l807" class="line" id="l807">    807</a>   syn match plugTag /(tag: [^)]\+)/
    827 <a href="#l808" class="line" id="l808">    808</a>   syn match plugInstall /\(^+ \)\@&lt;=[^:]*/
    828 <a href="#l809" class="line" id="l809">    809</a>   syn match plugUpdate /\(^* \)\@&lt;=[^:]*/
    829 <a href="#l810" class="line" id="l810">    810</a>   syn match plugCommit /^  \X*[0-9a-f]\{7,9} .*/ contains=plugRelDate,plugEdge,plugTag
    830 <a href="#l811" class="line" id="l811">    811</a>   syn match plugEdge /^  \X\+$/
    831 <a href="#l812" class="line" id="l812">    812</a>   syn match plugEdge /^  \X*/ contained nextgroup=plugSha
    832 <a href="#l813" class="line" id="l813">    813</a>   syn match plugSha /[0-9a-f]\{7,9}/ contained
    833 <a href="#l814" class="line" id="l814">    814</a>   syn match plugRelDate /([^)]*)$/ contained
    834 <a href="#l815" class="line" id="l815">    815</a>   syn match plugNotLoaded /(not loaded)$/
    835 <a href="#l816" class="line" id="l816">    816</a>   syn match plugError /^x.*/
    836 <a href="#l817" class="line" id="l817">    817</a>   syn region plugDeleted start=/^\~ .*/ end=/^\ze\S/
    837 <a href="#l818" class="line" id="l818">    818</a>   syn match plugH2 /^.*:\n-\+$/
    838 <a href="#l819" class="line" id="l819">    819</a>   syn match plugH2 /^-\{2,}/
    839 <a href="#l820" class="line" id="l820">    820</a>   syn keyword Function PlugInstall PlugStatus PlugUpdate PlugClean
    840 <a href="#l821" class="line" id="l821">    821</a>   hi def link plug1       Title
    841 <a href="#l822" class="line" id="l822">    822</a>   hi def link plug2       Repeat
    842 <a href="#l823" class="line" id="l823">    823</a>   hi def link plugH2      Type
    843 <a href="#l824" class="line" id="l824">    824</a>   hi def link plugX       Exception
    844 <a href="#l825" class="line" id="l825">    825</a>   hi def link plugAbort   Ignore
    845 <a href="#l826" class="line" id="l826">    826</a>   hi def link plugBracket Structure
    846 <a href="#l827" class="line" id="l827">    827</a>   hi def link plugNumber  Number
    847 <a href="#l828" class="line" id="l828">    828</a> 
    848 <a href="#l829" class="line" id="l829">    829</a>   hi def link plugDash    Special
    849 <a href="#l830" class="line" id="l830">    830</a>   hi def link plugPlus    Constant
    850 <a href="#l831" class="line" id="l831">    831</a>   hi def link plugStar    Boolean
    851 <a href="#l832" class="line" id="l832">    832</a> 
    852 <a href="#l833" class="line" id="l833">    833</a>   hi def link plugMessage Function
    853 <a href="#l834" class="line" id="l834">    834</a>   hi def link plugName    Label
    854 <a href="#l835" class="line" id="l835">    835</a>   hi def link plugInstall Function
    855 <a href="#l836" class="line" id="l836">    836</a>   hi def link plugUpdate  Type
    856 <a href="#l837" class="line" id="l837">    837</a> 
    857 <a href="#l838" class="line" id="l838">    838</a>   hi def link plugError   Error
    858 <a href="#l839" class="line" id="l839">    839</a>   hi def link plugDeleted Ignore
    859 <a href="#l840" class="line" id="l840">    840</a>   hi def link plugRelDate Comment
    860 <a href="#l841" class="line" id="l841">    841</a>   hi def link plugEdge    PreProc
    861 <a href="#l842" class="line" id="l842">    842</a>   hi def link plugSha     Identifier
    862 <a href="#l843" class="line" id="l843">    843</a>   hi def link plugTag     Constant
    863 <a href="#l844" class="line" id="l844">    844</a> 
    864 <a href="#l845" class="line" id="l845">    845</a>   hi def link plugNotLoaded Comment
    865 <a href="#l846" class="line" id="l846">    846</a> endfunction
    866 <a href="#l847" class="line" id="l847">    847</a> 
    867 <a href="#l848" class="line" id="l848">    848</a> function! s:lpad(str, len)
    868 <a href="#l849" class="line" id="l849">    849</a>   return a:str . repeat(&#39; &#39;, a:len - len(a:str))
    869 <a href="#l850" class="line" id="l850">    850</a> endfunction
    870 <a href="#l851" class="line" id="l851">    851</a>

    873 <a href="#l854" class="line" id="l854">    854</a> endfunction
    874 <a href="#l855" class="line" id="l855">    855</a> 
    875 <a href="#l856" class="line" id="l856">    856</a> function! s:lastline(msg)
