    877 <a href="#l858" class="line" id="l858">    858</a> endfunction
    878 <a href="#l859" class="line" id="l859">    859</a> 
    879 <a href="#l860" class="line" id="l860">    860</a> function! s:new_window()
    880 <a href="#l861" class="line" id="l861">    861</a>   execute get(g:, &#39;plug_window&#39;, &#39;-tabnew&#39;)
    881 <a href="#l862" class="line" id="l862">    862</a> endfunction
    882 <a href="#l863" class="line" id="l863">    863</a> 
    883 <a href="#l864" class="line" id="l864">    864</a> function! s:plug_window_exists()
    884 <a href="#l865" class="line" id="l865">    865</a>   let buflist = tabpagebuflist(s:plug_tab)
    885 <a href="#l866" class="line" id="l866">    866</a>   return !empty(buflist) &amp;&amp; index(buflist, s:plug_buf) &gt;= 0
    886 <a href="#l867" class="line" id="l867">    867</a> endfunction
    887 <a href="#l868" class="line" id="l868">    868</a> 
    888 <a href="#l869" class="line" id="l869">    869</a> function! s:switch_in()
    889 <a href="#l870" class="line" id="l870">    870</a>   if !s:plug_window_exists()
    890 <a href="#l871" class="line" id="l871">    871</a>     return 0
    891 <a href="#l872" class="line" id="l872">    872</a>   endif
    892 <a href="#l873" class="line" id="l873">    873</a> 
    893 <a href="#l874" class="line" id="l874">    874</a>   if winbufnr(0) != s:plug_buf
    894 <a href="#l875" class="line" id="l875">    875</a>     let s:pos = [tabpagenr(), winnr(), winsaveview()]
    895 <a href="#l876" class="line" id="l876">    876</a>     execute &#39;normal!&#39; s:plug_tab.&#39;gt&#39;
    896 <a href="#l877" class="line" id="l877">    877</a>     let winnr = bufwinnr(s:plug_buf)
    897 <a href="#l878" class="line" id="l878">    878</a>     execute winnr.&#39;wincmd w&#39;
    898 <a href="#l879" class="line" id="l879">    879</a>     call add(s:pos, winsaveview())
    899 <a href="#l880" class="line" id="l880">    880</a>   else
    900 <a href="#l881" class="line" id="l881">    881</a>     let s:pos = [winsaveview()]
    901 <a href="#l882" class="line" id="l882">    882</a>   endif
    902 <a href="#l883" class="line" id="l883">    883</a> 
    903 <a href="#l884" class="line" id="l884">    884</a>   setlocal modifiable
    904 <a href="#l885" class="line" id="l885">    885</a>   return 1
    905 <a href="#l886" class="line" id="l886">    886</a> endfunction
    906 <a href="#l887" class="line" id="l887">    887</a> 
    907 <a href="#l888" class="line" id="l888">    888</a> function! s:switch_out(...)
    908 <a href="#l889" class="line" id="l889">    889</a>   call winrestview(s:pos[-1])
    909 <a href="#l890" class="line" id="l890">    890</a>   setlocal nomodifiable
    910 <a href="#l891" class="line" id="l891">    891</a>   if a:0 &gt; 0
    911 <a href="#l892" class="line" id="l892">    892</a>     execute a:1
    912 <a href="#l893" class="line" id="l893">    893</a>   endif
    913 <a href="#l894" class="line" id="l894">    894</a> 
    914 <a href="#l895" class="line" id="l895">    895</a>   if len(s:pos) &gt; 1
    915 <a href="#l896" class="line" id="l896">    896</a>     execute &#39;normal!&#39; s:pos[0].&#39;gt&#39;
    916 <a href="#l897" class="line" id="l897">    897</a>     execute s:pos[1] &#39;wincmd w&#39;
    917 <a href="#l898" class="line" id="l898">    898</a>     call winrestview(s:pos[2])
    918 <a href="#l899" class="line" id="l899">    899</a>   endif
    919 <a href="#l900" class="line" id="l900">    900</a> endfunction
    920 <a href="#l901" class="line" id="l901">    901</a> 
    921 <a href="#l902" class="line" id="l902">    902</a> function! s:finish_bindings()
    922 <a href="#l903" class="line" id="l903">    903</a>   nnoremap &lt;silent&gt; &lt;buffer&gt; R  :call &lt;SID&gt;retry()&lt;cr&gt;
    923 <a href="#l904" class="line" id="l904">    904</a>   nnoremap &lt;silent&gt; &lt;buffer&gt; D  :PlugDiff&lt;cr&gt;
    924 <a href="#l905" class="line" id="l905">    905</a>   nnoremap &lt;silent&gt; &lt;buffer&gt; S  :PlugStatus&lt;cr&gt;
    925 <a href="#l906" class="line" id="l906">    906</a>   nnoremap &lt;silent&gt; &lt;buffer&gt; U  :call &lt;SID&gt;status_update()&lt;cr&gt;
    926 <a href="#l907" class="line" id="l907">    907</a>   xnoremap &lt;silent&gt; &lt;buffer&gt; U  :call &lt;SID&gt;status_update()&lt;cr&gt;
    927 <a href="#l908" class="line" id="l908">    908</a>   nnoremap &lt;silent&gt; &lt;buffer&gt; ]] :silent! call &lt;SID&gt;section(&#39;&#39;)&lt;cr&gt;
    928 <a href="#l909" class="line" id="l909">    909</a>   nnoremap &lt;silent&gt; &lt;buffer&gt; [[ :silent! call &lt;SID&gt;section(&#39;b&#39;)&lt;cr&gt;
    929 <a href="#l910" class="line" id="l910">    910</a> endfunction
    930 <a href="#l911" class="line" id="l911">    911</a> 
    931 <a href="#l912" class="line" id="l912">    912</a> function! s:prepare(...)
    932 <a href="#l913" class="line" id="l913">    913</a>   if empty(s:plug_getcwd())
    933 <a href="#l914" class="line" id="l914">    914</a>     throw &#39;Invalid current working directory. Cannot proceed.&#39;
    934 <a href="#l915" class="line" id="l915">    915</a>   endif
    935 <a href="#l916" class="line" id="l916">    916</a> 
    936 <a href="#l917" class="line" id="l917">    917</a>   for evar in [&#39;$GIT_DIR&#39;, &#39;$GIT_WORK_TREE&#39;]
    937 <a href="#l918" class="line" id="l918">    918</a>     if exists(evar)
    938 <a href="#l919" class="line" id="l919">    919</a>       throw evar.&#39; detected. Cannot proceed.&#39;
    939 <a href="#l920" class="line" id="l920">    920</a>     endif
    940 <a href="#l921" class="line" id="l921">    921</a>   endfor
    941 <a href="#l922" class="line" id="l922">    922</a> 
    942 <a href="#l923" class="line" id="l923">    923</a>   call s:job_abort(0)
    943 <a href="#l924" class="line" id="l924">    924</a>   if s:switch_in()
    944 <a href="#l925" class="line" id="l925">    925</a>     if b:plug_preview == 1
    945 <a href="#l926" class="line" id="l926">    926</a>       pc
    946 <a href="#l927" class="line" id="l927">    927</a>     endif
    947 <a href="#l928" class="line" id="l928">    928</a>     enew
    948 <a href="#l929" class="line" id="l929">    929</a>   else
    949 <a href="#l930" class="line" id="l930">    930</a>     call s:new_window()
    950 <a href="#l931" class="line" id="l931">    931</a>   endif
    951 <a href="#l932" class="line" id="l932">    932</a> 
    952 <a href="#l933" class="line" id="l933">    933</a>   nnoremap &lt;silent&gt; &lt;buffer&gt; q :call &lt;SID&gt;close_pane()&lt;cr&gt;
    953 <a href="#l934" class="line" id="l934">    934</a>   if a:0 == 0
    954 <a href="#l935" class="line" id="l935">    935</a>     call s:finish_bindings()
    955 <a href="#l936" class="line" id="l936">    936</a>   endif
    956 <a href="#l937" class="line" id="l937">    937</a>   let b:plug_preview = -1
    957 <a href="#l938" class="line" id="l938">    938</a>   let s:plug_tab = tabpagenr()
    958 <a href="#l939" class="line" id="l939">    939</a>   let s:plug_buf = winbufnr(0)
    959 <a href="#l940" class="line" id="l940">    940</a>   call s:assign_name()
    960 <a href="#l941" class="line" id="l941">    941</a> 
    961 <a href="#l942" class="line" id="l942">    942</a>   for k in [&#39;&lt;cr&gt;&#39;, &#39;L&#39;, &#39;o&#39;, &#39;X&#39;, &#39;d&#39;, &#39;dd&#39;]
    962 <a href="#l943" class="line" id="l943">    943</a>     execute &#39;silent! unmap &lt;buffer&gt;&#39; k
    963 <a href="#l944" class="line" id="l944">    944</a>   endfor
    964 <a href="#l945" class="line" id="l945">    945</a>   setlocal buftype=nofile bufhidden=wipe nobuflisted nolist noswapfile nowrap cursorline modifiable nospell
    965 <a href="#l946" class="line" id="l946">    946</a>   if exists(&#39;+colorcolumn&#39;)
    966 <a href="#l947" class="line" id="l947">    947</a>     setlocal colorcolumn=
    967 <a href="#l948" class="line" id="l948">    948</a>   endif
    968 <a href="#l949" class="line" id="l949">    949</a>   setf vim-plug
    969 <a href="#l950" class="line" id="l950">    950</a>   if exists(&#39;g:syntax_on&#39;)
    970 <a href="#l951" class="line" id="l951">    951</a>     call s:syntax()
    971 <a href="#l952" class="line" id="l952">    952</a>   endif
    972 <a href="#l953" class="line" id="l953">    953</a> endfunction
    973 <a href="#l954" class="line" id="l954">    954</a> 
    974 <a href="#l955" class="line" id="l955">    955</a> function! s:close_pane()
    975 <a href="#l956" class="line" id="l956">    956</a>   if b:plug_preview == 1
    976 <a href="#l957" class="line" id="l957">    957</a>     pc
    977 <a href="#l958" class="line" id="l958">    958</a>     let b:plug_preview = -1
    978 <a href="#l959" class="line" id="l959">    959</a>   elseif exists(&#39;s:jobs&#39;) &amp;&amp; !empty(s:jobs)
    979 <a href="#l960" class="line" id="l960">    960</a>     call s:job_abort(1)
    980 <a href="#l961" class="line" id="l961">    961</a>   else
    981 <a href="#l962" class="line" id="l962">    962</a>     bd
    982 <a href="#l963" class="line" id="l963">    963</a>   endif
    983 <a href="#l964" class="line" id="l964">    964</a> endfunction
    984 <a href="#l965" class="line" id="l965">    965</a> 
    985 <a href="#l966" class="line" id="l966">    966</a> function! s:assign_name()
    986 <a href="#l967" class="line" id="l967">    967</a>   &quot; Assign buffer name
    987 <a href="#l968" class="line" id="l968">    968</a>   let prefix = &#39;[Plugins]&#39;
    988 <a href="#l969" class="line" id="l969">    969</a>   let name   = prefix
    989 <a href="#l970" class="line" id="l970">    970</a>   let idx    = 2
    990 <a href="#l971" class="line" id="l971">    971</a>   while bufexists(name)
    991 <a href="#l972" class="line" id="l972">    972</a>     let name = printf(&#39;%s (%s)&#39;, prefix, idx)
    992 <a href="#l973" class="line" id="l973">    973</a>     let idx = idx + 1
    993 <a href="#l974" class="line" id="l974">    974</a>   endwhile
    994 <a href="#l975" class="line" id="l975">    975</a>   silent! execute &#39;f&#39; fnameescape(name)
    995 <a href="#l976" class="line" id="l976">    976</a> endfunction
    996 <a href="#l977" class="line" id="l977">    977</a> 
    997 <a href="#l978" class="line" id="l978">    978</a> function! s:chsh(swap)
    998 <a href="#l979" class="line" id="l979">    979</a>   let prev = [&amp;shell, &amp;shellcmdflag, &amp;shellredir]
    999 <a href="#l980" class="line" id="l980">    980</a>   if !s:is_win
   1000 <a href="#l981" class="line" id="l981">    981</a>     set shell=sh
   1001 <a href="#l982" class="line" id="l982">    982</a>   endif
   1002 <a href="#l983" class="line" id="l983">    983</a>   if a:swap
   1003 <a href="#l984" class="line" id="l984">    984</a>     if s:is_powershell(&amp;shell)
   1004 <a href="#l985" class="line" id="l985">    985</a>       let &amp;shellredir = &#39;2&gt;&amp;1 | Out-File -Encoding UTF8 %s&#39;
   1005 <a href="#l986" class="line" id="l986">    986</a>     elseif &amp;shell =~# &#39;sh&#39; || &amp;shell =~# &#39;cmd\(\.exe\)\?$&#39;
   1006 <a href="#l987" class="line" id="l987">    987</a>       set shellredir=&gt;%s\ 2&gt;&amp;1
   1007 <a href="#l988" class="line" id="l988">    988</a>     endif
   1008 <a href="#l989" class="line" id="l989">    989</a>   endif
   1009 <a href="#l990" class="line" id="l990">    990</a>   return prev
   1010 <a href="#l991" class="line" id="l991">    991</a> endfunction
   1011 <a href="#l992" class="line" id="l992">    992</a> 
   1012 <a href="#l993" class="line" id="l993">    993</a> function! s:bang(cmd, ...)
   1013 <a href="#l994" class="line" id="l994">    994</a>   let batchfile = &#39;&#39;
   1014 <a href="#l995" class="line" id="l995">    995</a>   try
   1015 <a href="#l996" class="line" id="l996">    996</a>     let [sh, shellcmdflag, shrd] = s:chsh(a:0)
   1016 <a href="#l997" class="line" id="l997">    997</a>     &quot; FIXME: Escaping is incomplete. We could use shellescape with eval,
   1017 <a href="#l998" class="line" id="l998">    998</a>     &quot;        but it won&#39;t work on Windows.
   1018 <a href="#l999" class="line" id="l999">    999</a>     let cmd = a:0 ? s:with_cd(a:cmd, a:1) : a:cmd
   1019 <a href="#l1000" class="line" id="l1000">   1000</a>     if s:is_win
   1020 <a href="#l1001" class="line" id="l1001">   1001</a>       let [batchfile, cmd] = s:batchfile(cmd)
   1021 <a href="#l1002" class="line" id="l1002">   1002</a>     endif
   1022 <a href="#l1003" class="line" id="l1003">   1003</a>     let g:_plug_bang = (s:is_win &amp;&amp; has(&#39;gui_running&#39;) ? &#39;silent &#39; : &#39;&#39;).&#39;!&#39;.escape(cmd, &#39;#!%&#39;)
   1023 <a href="#l1004" class="line" id="l1004">   1004</a>     execute &quot;normal! :execute g:_plug_bang\&lt;cr&gt;\&lt;cr&gt;&quot;
   1024 <a href="#l1005" class="line" id="l1005">   1005</a>   finally
   1025 <a href="#l1006" class="line" id="l1006">   1006</a>     unlet g:_plug_bang
   1026 <a href="#l1007" class="line" id="l1007">   1007</a>     let [&amp;shell, &amp;shellcmdflag, &amp;shellredir] = [sh, shellcmdflag, shrd]
   1027 <a href="#l1008" class="line" id="l1008">   1008</a>     if s:is_win &amp;&amp; filereadable(batchfile)
   1028 <a href="#l1009" class="line" id="l1009">   1009</a>       call delete(batchfile)
   1029 <a href="#l1010" class="line" id="l1010">   1010</a>     endif
   1030 <a href="#l1011" class="line" id="l1011">   1011</a>   endtry
   1031 <a href="#l1012" class="line" id="l1012">   1012</a>   return v:shell_error ? &#39;Exit status: &#39; . v:shell_error : &#39;&#39;
   1032 <a href="#l1013" class="line" id="l1013">   1013</a> endfunction
   1033 <a href="#l1014" class="line" id="l1014">   1014</a> 
   1034 <a href="#l1015" class="line" id="l1015">   1015</a> function! s:regress_bar()
   1035 <a href="#l1016" class="line" id="l1016">   1016</a>   let bar = substitute(getline(2)[1:-2], &#39;.*\zs=&#39;, &#39;x&#39;, &#39;&#39;)
   1036 <a href="#l1017" class="line" id="l1017">   1017</a>   call s:progress_bar(2, bar, len(bar))
   1037 <a href="#l1018" class="line" id="l1018">   1018</a> endfunction
   1038 <a href="#l1019" class="line" id="l1019">   1019</a> 
   1039 <a href="#l1020" class="line" id="l1020">   1020</a> function! s:is_updated(dir)
   1040 <a href="#l1021" class="line" id="l1021">   1021</a>   return !empty(s:system_chomp([&#39;git&#39;, &#39;log&#39;, &#39;--pretty=format:%h&#39;, &#39;HEAD...HEAD@{1}&#39;], a:dir))
   1041 <a href="#l1022" class="line" id="l1022">   1022</a> endfunction
   1042 <a href="#l1023" class="line" id="l1023">   1023</a> 
   1043 <a href="#l1024" class="line" id="l1024">   1024</a> function! s:do(pull, force, todo)
   1044 <a href="#l1025" class="line" id="l1025">   1025</a>   if has(&#39;nvim&#39;)
   1045 <a href="#l1026" class="line" id="l1026">   1026</a>     &quot; Reset &amp;rtp to invalidate Neovim cache of loaded Lua modules
   1046 <a href="#l1027" class="line" id="l1027">   1027</a>     &quot; See https://github.com/junegunn/vim-plug/pull/1157#issuecomment-1809226110
   1047 <a href="#l1028" class="line" id="l1028">   1028</a>     let &amp;rtp = &amp;rtp
   1048 <a href="#l1029" class="line" id="l1029">   1029</a>   endif
   1049 <a href="#l1030" class="line" id="l1030">   1030</a>   for [name, spec] in items(a:todo)
   1050 <a href="#l1031" class="line" id="l1031">   1031</a>     if !isdirectory(spec.dir)
   1051 <a href="#l1032" class="line" id="l1032">   1032</a>       continue
   1052 <a href="#l1033" class="line" id="l1033">   1033</a>     endif
   1053 <a href="#l1034" class="line" id="l1034">   1034</a>     let installed = has_key(s:update.new, name)
   1054 <a href="#l1035" class="line" id="l1035">   1035</a>     let updated = installed ? 0 :
   1055 <a href="#l1036" class="line" id="l1036">   1036</a>       \ (a:pull &amp;&amp; index(s:update.errors, name) &lt; 0 &amp;&amp; s:is_updated(spec.dir))
   1056 <a href="#l1037" class="line" id="l1037">   1037</a>     if a:force || installed || updated
   1057 <a href="#l1038" class="line" id="l1038">   1038</a>       execute &#39;cd&#39; s:esc(spec.dir)
   1058 <a href="#l1039" class="line" id="l1039">   1039</a>       call append(3, &#39;- Post-update hook for &#39;. name .&#39; ... &#39;)
   1059 <a href="#l1040" class="line" id="l1040">   1040</a>       let error = &#39;&#39;
   1060 <a href="#l1041" class="line" id="l1041">   1041</a>       let type = type(spec.do)
   1061 <a href="#l1042" class="line" id="l1042">   1042</a>       if type == s:TYPE.string
   1062 <a href="#l1043" class="line" id="l1043">   1043</a>         if spec.do[0] == &#39;:&#39;
   1063 <a href="#l1044" class="line" id="l1044">   1044</a>           if !get(s:loaded, name, 0)
   1064 <a href="#l1045" class="line" id="l1045">   1045</a>             let s:loaded[name] = 1
   1065 <a href="#l1046" class="line" id="l1046">   1046</a>             call s:reorg_rtp()
   1066 <a href="#l1047" class="line" id="l1047">   1047</a>           endif
   1067 <a href="#l1048" class="line" id="l1048">   1048</a>           call s:load_plugin(spec)
   1068 <a href="#l1049" class="line" id="l1049">   1049</a>           try
   1069 <a href="#l1050" class="line" id="l1050">   1050</a>             execute spec.do[1:]
   1070 <a href="#l1051" class="line" id="l1051">   1051</a>           catch
   1071 <a href="#l1052" class="line" id="l1052">   1052</a>             let error = v:exception
   1072 <a href="#l1053" class="line" id="l1053">   1053</a>           endtry
   1073 <a href="#l1054" class="line" id="l1054">   1054</a>           if !s:plug_window_exists()
   1074 <a href="#l1055" class="line" id="l1055">   1055</a>             cd -
   1075 <a href="#l1056" class="line" id="l1056">   1056</a>             throw &#39;Warning: vim-plug was terminated by the post-update hook of &#39;.name
   1076 <a href="#l1057" class="line" id="l1057">   1057</a>           endif
   1077 <a href="#l1058" class="line" id="l1058">   1058</a>         else
   1078 <a href="#l1059" class="line" id="l1059">   1059</a>           let error = s:bang(spec.do)
   1079 <a href="#l1060" class="line" id="l1060">   1060</a>         endif
   1080 <a href="#l1061" class="line" id="l1061">   1061</a>       elseif type == s:TYPE.funcref
   1081 <a href="#l1062" class="line" id="l1062">   1062</a>         try
   1082 <a href="#l1063" class="line" id="l1063">   1063</a>           call s:load_plugin(spec)
   1083 <a href="#l1064" class="line" id="l1064">   1064</a>           let status = installed ? &#39;installed&#39; : (updated ? &#39;updated&#39; : &#39;unchanged&#39;)
   1084 <a href="#l1065" class="line" id="l1065">   1065</a>           call spec.do({ &#39;name&#39;: name, &#39;status&#39;: status, &#39;force&#39;: a:force })
   1085 <a href="#l1066" class="line" id="l1066">   1066</a>         catch
   1086 <a href="#l1067" class="line" id="l1067">   1067</a>           let error = v:exception
   1087 <a href="#l1068" class="line" id="l1068">   1068</a>         endtry
   1088 <a href="#l1069" class="line" id="l1069">   1069</a>       else
   1089 <a href="#l1070" class="line" id="l1070">   1070</a>         let error = &#39;Invalid hook type&#39;
   1090 <a href="#l1071" class="line" id="l1071">   1071</a>       endif
   1091 <a href="#l1072" class="line" id="l1072">   1072</a>       call s:switch_in()
   1092 <a href="#l1073" class="line" id="l1073">   1073</a>       call setline(4, empty(error) ? (getline(4) . &#39;OK&#39;)
   1093 <a href="#l1074" class="line" id="l1074">   1074</a>                                  \ : (&#39;x&#39; . getline(4)[1:] . error))
   1094 <a href="#l1075" class="line" id="l1075">   1075</a>       if !empty(error)
   1095 <a href="#l1076" class="line" id="l1076">   1076</a>         call add(s:update.errors, name)
   1096 <a href="#l1077" class="line" id="l1077">   1077</a>         call s:regress_bar()
   1097 <a href="#l1078" class="line" id="l1078">   1078</a>       endif
   1098 <a href="#l1079" class="line" id="l1079">   1079</a>       cd -
   1099 <a href="#l1080" class="line" id="l1080">   1080</a>     endif
   1100 <a href="#l1081" class="line" id="l1081">   1081</a>   endfor
   1101 <a href="#l1082" class="line" id="l1082">   1082</a> endfunction

   1270 <a href="#l1251" class="line" id="l1251">   1251</a>       let lines = getline(4, &#39;$&#39;)
   1271 <a href="#l1252" class="line" id="l1252">   1252</a>       let printed = {}
   1272 <a href="#l1253" class="line" id="l1253">   1253</a>       silent! 4,$d _
   1273 <a href="#l1254" class="line" id="l1254">   1254</a>       for line in lines
   1274 <a href="#l1255" class="line" id="l1255">   1255</a>         let name = s:extract_name(line, &#39;.&#39;, &#39;&#39;)
   1275 <a href="#l1256" class="line" id="l1256">   1256</a>         if empty(name) || !has_key(printed, name)
   1276 <a href="#l1257" class="line" id="l1257">   1257</a>           call append(&#39;$&#39;, line)
   1277 <a href="#l1258" class="line" id="l1258">   1258</a>           if !empty(name)
   1278 <a href="#l1259" class="line" id="l1259">   1259</a>             let printed[name] = 1
   1279 <a href="#l1260" class="line" id="l1260">   1260</a>             if line[0] == &#39;x&#39; &amp;&amp; index(s:update.errors, name) &lt; 0
   1280 <a href="#l1261" class="line" id="l1261">   1261</a>               call add(s:update.errors, name)
   1281 <a href="#l1262" class="line" id="l1262">   1262</a>             end
   1282 <a href="#l1263" class="line" id="l1263">   1263</a>           endif
   1283 <a href="#l1264" class="line" id="l1264">   1264</a>         endif
   1284 <a href="#l1265" class="line" id="l1265">   1265</a>       endfor
   1285 <a href="#l1266" class="line" id="l1266">   1266</a>     finally
   1286 <a href="#l1267" class="line" id="l1267">   1267</a>       let &amp;imd = imd
   1287 <a href="#l1268" class="line" id="l1268">   1268</a>       call s:update_finish()
   1288 <a href="#l1269" class="line" id="l1269">   1269</a>     endtry
   1289 <a href="#l1270" class="line" id="l1270">   1270</a>   else
   1290 <a href="#l1271" class="line" id="l1271">   1271</a>     call s:update_vim()
   1291 <a href="#l1272" class="line" id="l1272">   1272</a>     while use_job &amp;&amp; sync
   1292 <a href="#l1273" class="line" id="l1273">   1273</a>       sleep 100m
   1293 <a href="#l1274" class="line" id="l1274">   1274</a>       if s:update.fin
   1294 <a href="#l1275" class="line" id="l1275">   1275</a>         break
   1295 <a href="#l1276" class="line" id="l1276">   1276</a>       endif
   1296 <a href="#l1277" class="line" id="l1277">   1277</a>     endwhile
   1297 <a href="#l1278" class="line" id="l1278">   1278</a>   endif
   1298 <a href="#l1279" class="line" id="l1279">   1279</a> endfunction
   1299 <a href="#l1280" class="line" id="l1280">   1280</a> 
   1300 <a href="#l1281" class="line" id="l1281">   1281</a> function! s:log4(name, msg)
   1301 <a href="#l1282" class="line" id="l1282">   1282</a>   call setline(4, printf(&#39;- %s (%s)&#39;, a:msg, a:name))
   1302 <a href="#l1283" class="line" id="l1283">   1283</a>   redraw
   1303 <a href="#l1284" class="line" id="l1284">   1284</a> endfunction
   1304 <a href="#l1285" class="line" id="l1285">   1285</a> 
   1305 <a href="#l1286" class="line" id="l1286">   1286</a> function! s:update_finish()
   1306 <a href="#l1287" class="line" id="l1287">   1287</a>   if exists(&#39;s:git_terminal_prompt&#39;)
   1307 <a href="#l1288" class="line" id="l1288">   1288</a>     let $GIT_TERMINAL_PROMPT = s:git_terminal_prompt
   1308 <a href="#l1289" class="line" id="l1289">   1289</a>   endif
   1309 <a href="#l1290" class="line" id="l1290">   1290</a>   if s:switch_in()
   1310 <a href="#l1291" class="line" id="l1291">   1291</a>     call append(3, &#39;- Updating ...&#39;) | 4
   1311 <a href="#l1292" class="line" id="l1292">   1292</a>     for [name, spec] in items(filter(copy(s:update.all), &#39;index(s:update.errors, v:key) &lt; 0 &amp;&amp; (s:update.force || s:update.pull || has_key(s:update.new, v:key))&#39;))
   1312 <a href="#l1293" class="line" id="l1293">   1293</a>       let [pos, _] = s:logpos(name)
   1313 <a href="#l1294" class="line" id="l1294">   1294</a>       if !pos
   1314 <a href="#l1295" class="line" id="l1295">   1295</a>         continue
   1315 <a href="#l1296" class="line" id="l1296">   1296</a>       endif
   1316 <a href="#l1297" class="line" id="l1297">   1297</a>       let out = &#39;&#39;
   1317 <a href="#l1298" class="line" id="l1298">   1298</a>       let error = 0
   1318 <a href="#l1299" class="line" id="l1299">   1299</a>       if has_key(spec, &#39;commit&#39;)
   1319 <a href="#l1300" class="line" id="l1300">   1300</a>         call s:log4(name, &#39;Checking out &#39;.spec.commit)
   1320 <a href="#l1301" class="line" id="l1301">   1301</a>         let [out, error] = s:checkout(spec)
   1321 <a href="#l1302" class="line" id="l1302">   1302</a>       elseif has_key(spec, &#39;tag&#39;)
   1322 <a href="#l1303" class="line" id="l1303">   1303</a>         let tag = spec.tag
   1323 <a href="#l1304" class="line" id="l1304">   1304</a>         if tag =~ &#39;\*&#39;
   1324 <a href="#l1305" class="line" id="l1305">   1305</a>           let tags = s:lines(s:system(&#39;git tag --list &#39;.plug#shellescape(tag).&#39; --sort -version:refname 2&gt;&amp;1&#39;, spec.dir))
   1325 <a href="#l1306" class="line" id="l1306">   1306</a>           if !v:shell_error &amp;&amp; !empty(tags)
   1326 <a href="#l1307" class="line" id="l1307">   1307</a>             let tag = tags[0]
   1327 <a href="#l1308" class="line" id="l1308">   1308</a>             call s:log4(name, printf(&#39;Latest tag for %s -&gt; %s&#39;, spec.tag, tag))
   1328 <a href="#l1309" class="line" id="l1309">   1309</a>             call append(3, &#39;&#39;)
   1329 <a href="#l1310" class="line" id="l1310">   1310</a>           endif
   1330 <a href="#l1311" class="line" id="l1311">   1311</a>         endif
   1331 <a href="#l1312" class="line" id="l1312">   1312</a>         call s:log4(name, &#39;Checking out &#39;.tag)
   1332 <a href="#l1313" class="line" id="l1313">   1313</a>         let out = s:system(&#39;git checkout -q &#39;.plug#shellescape(tag).&#39; -- 2&gt;&amp;1&#39;, spec.dir)
   1333 <a href="#l1314" class="line" id="l1314">   1314</a>         let error = v:shell_error
   1334 <a href="#l1315" class="line" id="l1315">   1315</a>       endif
   1335 <a href="#l1316" class="line" id="l1316">   1316</a>       if !error &amp;&amp; filereadable(spec.dir.&#39;/.gitmodules&#39;) &amp;&amp;
   1336 <a href="#l1317" class="line" id="l1317">   1317</a>             \ (s:update.force || has_key(s:update.new, name) || s:is_updated(spec.dir))
   1337 <a href="#l1318" class="line" id="l1318">   1318</a>         call s:log4(name, &#39;Updating submodules. This may take a while.&#39;)
   1338 <a href="#l1319" class="line" id="l1319">   1319</a>         let out .= s:bang(&#39;git submodule update --init --recursive&#39;.s:submodule_opt.&#39; 2&gt;&amp;1&#39;, spec.dir)
   1339 <a href="#l1320" class="line" id="l1320">   1320</a>         let error = v:shell_error
   1340 <a href="#l1321" class="line" id="l1321">   1321</a>       endif
   1341 <a href="#l1322" class="line" id="l1322">   1322</a>       let msg = s:format_message(v:shell_error ? &#39;x&#39;: &#39;-&#39;, name, out)
   1342 <a href="#l1323" class="line" id="l1323">   1323</a>       if error
   1343 <a href="#l1324" class="line" id="l1324">   1324</a>         call add(s:update.errors, name)
   1344 <a href="#l1325" class="line" id="l1325">   1325</a>         call s:regress_bar()
   1345 <a href="#l1326" class="line" id="l1326">   1326</a>         silent execute pos &#39;d _&#39;
   1346 <a href="#l1327" class="line" id="l1327">   1327</a>         call append(4, msg) | 4
   1347 <a href="#l1328" class="line" id="l1328">   1328</a>       elseif !empty(out)
   1348 <a href="#l1329" class="line" id="l1329">   1329</a>         call setline(pos, msg[0])
   1349 <a href="#l1330" class="line" id="l1330">   1330</a>       endif
   1350 <a href="#l1331" class="line" id="l1331">   1331</a>       redraw
   1351 <a href="#l1332" class="line" id="l1332">   1332</a>     endfor
   1352 <a href="#l1333" class="line" id="l1333">   1333</a>     silent 4 d _
   1353 <a href="#l1334" class="line" id="l1334">   1334</a>     try
   1354 <a href="#l1335" class="line" id="l1335">   1335</a>       call s:do(s:update.pull, s:update.force, filter(copy(s:update.all), &#39;index(s:update.errors, v:key) &lt; 0 &amp;&amp; has_key(v:val, &quot;do&quot;)&#39;))
   1355 <a href="#l1336" class="line" id="l1336">   1336</a>     catch
   1356 <a href="#l1337" class="line" id="l1337">   1337</a>       call s:warn(&#39;echom&#39;, v:exception)
   1357 <a href="#l1338" class="line" id="l1338">   1338</a>       call s:warn(&#39;echo&#39;, &#39;&#39;)
   1358 <a href="#l1339" class="line" id="l1339">   1339</a>       return
   1359 <a href="#l1340" class="line" id="l1340">   1340</a>     endtry
   1360 <a href="#l1341" class="line" id="l1341">   1341</a>     call s:finish(s:update.pull)
   1361 <a href="#l1342" class="line" id="l1342">   1342</a>     call setline(1, &#39;Updated. Elapsed time: &#39; . split(reltimestr(reltime(s:update.start)))[0] . &#39; sec.&#39;)
   1362 <a href="#l1343" class="line" id="l1343">   1343</a>     call s:switch_out(&#39;normal! gg&#39;)
   1363 <a href="#l1344" class="line" id="l1344">   1344</a>   endif
   1364 <a href="#l1345" class="line" id="l1345">   1345</a> endfunction
   1365 <a href="#l1346" class="line" id="l1346">   1346</a> 
   1366 <a href="#l1347" class="line" id="l1347">   1347</a> function! s:mark_aborted(name, message)
   1367 <a href="#l1348" class="line" id="l1348">   1348</a>   let attrs = { &#39;running&#39;: 0, &#39;error&#39;: 1, &#39;abort&#39;: 1, &#39;lines&#39;: [a:message] }
   1368 <a href="#l1349" class="line" id="l1349">   1349</a>   let s:jobs[a:name] = extend(get(s:jobs, a:name, {}), attrs)
   1369 <a href="#l1350" class="line" id="l1350">   1350</a> endfunction
   1370 <a href="#l1351" class="line" id="l1351">   1351</a> 
   1371 <a href="#l1352" class="line" id="l1352">   1352</a> function! s:job_abort(cancel)
   1372 <a href="#l1353" class="line" id="l1353">   1353</a>   if (!s:nvim &amp;&amp; !s:vim8) || !exists(&#39;s:jobs&#39;)
   1373 <a href="#l1354" class="line" id="l1354">   1354</a>     return
   1374 <a href="#l1355" class="line" id="l1355">   1355</a>   endif
   1375 <a href="#l1356" class="line" id="l1356">   1356</a> 
   1376 <a href="#l1357" class="line" id="l1357">   1357</a>   for [name, j] in items(s:jobs)
   1377 <a href="#l1358" class="line" id="l1358">   1358</a>     if s:nvim
   1378 <a href="#l1359" class="line" id="l1359">   1359</a>       silent! call jobstop(j.jobid)
   1379 <a href="#l1360" class="line" id="l1360">   1360</a>     elseif s:vim8
   1380 <a href="#l1361" class="line" id="l1361">   1361</a>       silent! call job_stop(j.jobid)
   1381 <a href="#l1362" class="line" id="l1362">   1362</a>     endif
   1382 <a href="#l1363" class="line" id="l1363">   1363</a>     if j.new
   1383 <a href="#l1364" class="line" id="l1364">   1364</a>       call s:rm_rf(g:plugs[name].dir)
   1384 <a href="#l1365" class="line" id="l1365">   1365</a>     endif
   1385 <a href="#l1366" class="line" id="l1366">   1366</a>     if a:cancel
   1386 <a href="#l1367" class="line" id="l1367">   1367</a>       call s:mark_aborted(name, &#39;Aborted&#39;)
   1387 <a href="#l1368" class="line" id="l1368">   1368</a>     endif
   1388 <a href="#l1369" class="line" id="l1369">   1369</a>   endfor
   1389 <a href="#l1370" class="line" id="l1370">   1370</a> 
   1390 <a href="#l1371" class="line" id="l1371">   1371</a>   if a:cancel
   1391 <a href="#l1372" class="line" id="l1372">   1372</a>     for todo in values(s:update.todo)
   1392 <a href="#l1373" class="line" id="l1373">   1373</a>       let todo.abort = 1
   1393 <a href="#l1374" class="line" id="l1374">   1374</a>     endfor
   1394 <a href="#l1375" class="line" id="l1375">   1375</a>   else
   1395 <a href="#l1376" class="line" id="l1376">   1376</a>     let s:jobs = {}
   1396 <a href="#l1377" class="line" id="l1377">   1377</a>   endif
   1397 <a href="#l1378" class="line" id="l1378">   1378</a> endfunction
   1398 <a href="#l1379" class="line" id="l1379">   1379</a> 
   1399 <a href="#l1380" class="line" id="l1380">   1380</a> function! s:last_non_empty_line(lines)
   1400 <a href="#l1381" class="line" id="l1381">   1381</a>   let len = len(a:lines)
   1401 <a href="#l1382" class="line" id="l1382">   1382</a>   for idx in range(len)
   1402 <a href="#l1383" class="line" id="l1383">   1383</a>     let line = a:lines[len-idx-1]
   1403 <a href="#l1384" class="line" id="l1384">   1384</a>     if !empty(line)
   1404 <a href="#l1385" class="line" id="l1385">   1385</a>       return line
   1405 <a href="#l1386" class="line" id="l1386">   1386</a>     endif
   1406 <a href="#l1387" class="line" id="l1387">   1387</a>   endfor
   1407 <a href="#l1388" class="line" id="l1388">   1388</a>   return &#39;&#39;
   1408 <a href="#l1389" class="line" id="l1389">   1389</a> endfunction
   1409 <a href="#l1390" class="line" id="l1390">   1390</a> 
   1410 <a href="#l1391" class="line" id="l1391">   1391</a> function! s:bullet_for(job, ...)
   1411 <a href="#l1392" class="line" id="l1392">   1392</a>   if a:job.running
   1412 <a href="#l1393" class="line" id="l1393">   1393</a>     return a:job.new ? &#39;+&#39; : &#39;*&#39;
   1413 <a href="#l1394" class="line" id="l1394">   1394</a>   endif
   1414 <a href="#l1395" class="line" id="l1395">   1395</a>   if get(a:job, &#39;abort&#39;, 0)
   1415 <a href="#l1396" class="line" id="l1396">   1396</a>     return &#39;~&#39;
   1416 <a href="#l1397" class="line" id="l1397">   1397</a>   endif
   1417 <a href="#l1398" class="line" id="l1398">   1398</a>   return a:job.error ? &#39;x&#39; : get(a:000, 0, &#39;-&#39;)
   1418 <a href="#l1399" class="line" id="l1399">   1399</a> endfunction
   1419 <a href="#l1400" class="line" id="l1400">   1400</a> 
   1420 <a href="#l1401" class="line" id="l1401">   1401</a> function! s:job_out_cb(self, data) abort
   1421 <a href="#l1402" class="line" id="l1402">   1402</a>   let self = a:self
   1422 <a href="#l1403" class="line" id="l1403">   1403</a>   let data = remove(self.lines, -1) . a:data
   1423 <a href="#l1404" class="line" id="l1404">   1404</a>   let lines = map(split(data, &quot;\n&quot;, 1), &#39;split(v:val, &quot;\r&quot;, 1)[-1]&#39;)
   1424 <a href="#l1405" class="line" id="l1405">   1405</a>   call extend(self.lines, lines)
   1425 <a href="#l1406" class="line" id="l1406">   1406</a>   &quot; To reduce the number of buffer updates
   1426 <a href="#l1407" class="line" id="l1407">   1407</a>   let self.tick = get(self, &#39;tick&#39;, -1) + 1
   1427 <a href="#l1408" class="line" id="l1408">   1408</a>   if !self.running || self.tick % len(s:jobs) == 0
   1428 <a href="#l1409" class="line" id="l1409">   1409</a>     let result = self.error ? join(self.lines, &quot;\n&quot;) : s:last_non_empty_line(self.lines)
   1429 <a href="#l1410" class="line" id="l1410">   1410</a>     if len(result)
   1430 <a href="#l1411" class="line" id="l1411">   1411</a>       call s:log(s:bullet_for(self), self.name, result)
   1431 <a href="#l1412" class="line" id="l1412">   1412</a>     endif
   1432 <a href="#l1413" class="line" id="l1413">   1413</a>   endif
   1433 <a href="#l1414" class="line" id="l1414">   1414</a> endfunction
   1434 <a href="#l1415" class="line" id="l1415">   1415</a> 
   1435 <a href="#l1416" class="line" id="l1416">   1416</a> function! s:job_exit_cb(self, data) abort
   1436 <a href="#l1417" class="line" id="l1417">   1417</a>   let a:self.running = 0
   1437 <a href="#l1418" class="line" id="l1418">   1418</a>   let a:self.error = a:data != 0
   1438 <a href="#l1419" class="line" id="l1419">   1419</a>   call s:reap(a:self.name)
   1439 <a href="#l1420" class="line" id="l1420">   1420</a>   call s:tick()
   1440 <a href="#l1421" class="line" id="l1421">   1421</a> endfunction
   1441 <a href="#l1422" class="line" id="l1422">   1422</a> 
   1442 <a href="#l1423" class="line" id="l1423">   1423</a> function! s:job_cb(fn, job, ch, data)
   1443 <a href="#l1424" class="line" id="l1424">   1424</a>   if !s:plug_window_exists() &quot; plug window closed
   1444 <a href="#l1425" class="line" id="l1425">   1425</a>     return s:job_abort(0)
   1445 <a href="#l1426" class="line" id="l1426">   1426</a>   endif
   1446 <a href="#l1427" class="line" id="l1427">   1427</a>   call call(a:fn, [a:job, a:data])
   1447 <a href="#l1428" class="line" id="l1428">   1428</a> endfunction
   1448 <a href="#l1429" class="line" id="l1429">   1429</a> 
   1449 <a href="#l1430" class="line" id="l1430">   1430</a> function! s:nvim_cb(job_id, data, event) dict abort
   1450 <a href="#l1431" class="line" id="l1431">   1431</a>   return (a:event == &#39;stdout&#39; || a:event == &#39;stderr&#39;) ?
   1451 <a href="#l1432" class="line" id="l1432">   1432</a>     \ s:job_cb(&#39;s:job_out_cb&#39;,  self, 0, join(a:data, &quot;\n&quot;)) :
   1452 <a href="#l1433" class="line" id="l1433">   1433</a>     \ s:job_cb(&#39;s:job_exit_cb&#39;, self, 0, a:data)
   1453 <a href="#l1434" class="line" id="l1434">   1434</a> endfunction
   1454 <a href="#l1435" class="line" id="l1435">   1435</a> 
   1455 <a href="#l1436" class="line" id="l1436">   1436</a> function! s:spawn(name, spec, queue, opts)
   1456 <a href="#l1437" class="line" id="l1437">   1437</a>   let job = { &#39;name&#39;: a:name, &#39;spec&#39;: a:spec, &#39;running&#39;: 1, &#39;error&#39;: 0, &#39;lines&#39;: [&#39;&#39;],
   1457 <a href="#l1438" class="line" id="l1438">   1438</a>             \ &#39;new&#39;: get(a:opts, &#39;new&#39;, 0), &#39;queue&#39;: copy(a:queue) }
   1458 <a href="#l1439" class="line" id="l1439">   1439</a>   let Item = remove(job.queue, 0)
   1459 <a href="#l1440" class="line" id="l1440">   1440</a>   let argv = type(Item) == s:TYPE.funcref ? call(Item, [a:spec]) : Item
   1460 <a href="#l1441" class="line" id="l1441">   1441</a>   let s:jobs[a:name] = job
   1461 <a href="#l1442" class="line" id="l1442">   1442</a> 
   1462 <a href="#l1443" class="line" id="l1443">   1443</a>   if s:nvim
   1463 <a href="#l1444" class="line" id="l1444">   1444</a>     if has_key(a:opts, &#39;dir&#39;)
   1464 <a href="#l1445" class="line" id="l1445">   1445</a>       let job.cwd = a:opts.dir
   1465 <a href="#l1446" class="line" id="l1446">   1446</a>     endif
   1466 <a href="#l1447" class="line" id="l1447">   1447</a>     call extend(job, {
   1467 <a href="#l1448" class="line" id="l1448">   1448</a>     \ &#39;on_stdout&#39;: function(&#39;s:nvim_cb&#39;),
   1468 <a href="#l1449" class="line" id="l1449">   1449</a>     \ &#39;on_stderr&#39;: function(&#39;s:nvim_cb&#39;),
   1469 <a href="#l1450" class="line" id="l1450">   1450</a>     \ &#39;on_exit&#39;:   function(&#39;s:nvim_cb&#39;),
   1470 <a href="#l1451" class="line" id="l1451">   1451</a>     \ })
   1471 <a href="#l1452" class="line" id="l1452">   1452</a>     let jid = s:plug_call(&#39;jobstart&#39;, argv, job)
   1472 <a href="#l1453" class="line" id="l1453">   1453</a>     if jid &gt; 0
   1473 <a href="#l1454" class="line" id="l1454">   1454</a>       let job.jobid = jid
   1474 <a href="#l1455" class="line" id="l1455">   1455</a>     else
   1475 <a href="#l1456" class="line" id="l1456">   1456</a>       let job.running = 0
   1476 <a href="#l1457" class="line" id="l1457">   1457</a>       let job.error   = 1
   1477 <a href="#l1458" class="line" id="l1458">   1458</a>       let job.lines   = [jid &lt; 0 ? argv[0].&#39; is not executable&#39; :
   1478 <a href="#l1459" class="line" id="l1459">   1459</a>             \ &#39;Invalid arguments (or job table is full)&#39;]
   1479 <a href="#l1460" class="line" id="l1460">   1460</a>     endif
   1480 <a href="#l1461" class="line" id="l1461">   1461</a>   elseif s:vim8
   1481 <a href="#l1462" class="line" id="l1462">   1462</a>     let cmd = join(map(copy(argv), &#39;plug#shellescape(v:val, {&quot;script&quot;: 0})&#39;))
   1482 <a href="#l1463" class="line" id="l1463">   1463</a>     if has_key(a:opts, &#39;dir&#39;)
   1483 <a href="#l1464" class="line" id="l1464">   1464</a>       let cmd = s:with_cd(cmd, a:opts.dir, 0)
   1484 <a href="#l1465" class="line" id="l1465">   1465</a>     endif
   1485 <a href="#l1466" class="line" id="l1466">   1466</a>     let argv = s:is_win ? [&#39;cmd&#39;, &#39;/s&#39;, &#39;/c&#39;, &#39;&quot;&#39;.cmd.&#39;&quot;&#39;] : [&#39;sh&#39;, &#39;-c&#39;, cmd]
   1486 <a href="#l1467" class="line" id="l1467">   1467</a>     let jid = job_start(s:is_win ? join(argv, &#39; &#39;) : argv, {
   1487 <a href="#l1468" class="line" id="l1468">   1468</a>     \ &#39;out_cb&#39;:   function(&#39;s:job_cb&#39;, [&#39;s:job_out_cb&#39;,  job]),
   1488 <a href="#l1469" class="line" id="l1469">   1469</a>     \ &#39;err_cb&#39;:   function(&#39;s:job_cb&#39;, [&#39;s:job_out_cb&#39;,  job]),
   1489 <a href="#l1470" class="line" id="l1470">   1470</a>     \ &#39;exit_cb&#39;:  function(&#39;s:job_cb&#39;, [&#39;s:job_exit_cb&#39;, job]),
   1490 <a href="#l1471" class="line" id="l1471">   1471</a>     \ &#39;err_mode&#39;: &#39;raw&#39;,

   1492 <a href="#l1473" class="line" id="l1473">   1473</a>     \})
   1493 <a href="#l1474" class="line" id="l1474">   1474</a>     if job_status(jid) == &#39;run&#39;
   1494 <a href="#l1475" class="line" id="l1475">   1475</a>       let job.jobid = jid
   1495 <a href="#l1476" class="line" id="l1476">   1476</a>     else

   1497 <a href="#l1478" class="line" id="l1478">   1478</a>       let job.error   = 1
   1498 <a href="#l1479" class="line" id="l1479">   1479</a>       let job.lines   = [&#39;Failed to start job&#39;]
   1499 <a href="#l1480" class="line" id="l1480">   1480</a>     endif
   1500 <a href="#l1481" class="line" id="l1481">   1481</a>   else

   1502 <a href="#l1483" class="line" id="l1483">   1483</a>     let job.error = v:shell_error != 0
   1503 <a href="#l1484" class="line" id="l1484">   1484</a>     let job.running = 0

   1507 <a href="#l1488" class="line" id="l1488">   1488</a> function! s:reap(name)
   1508 <a href="#l1489" class="line" id="l1489">   1489</a>   let job = remove(s:jobs, a:name)
   1509 <a href="#l1490" class="line" id="l1490">   1490</a>   if job.error
   1510 <a href="#l1491" class="line" id="l1491">   1491</a>     call add(s:update.errors, a:name)
   1511 <a href="#l1492" class="line" id="l1492">   1492</a>   elseif get(job, &#39;new&#39;, 0)
   1512 <a href="#l1493" class="line" id="l1493">   1493</a>     let s:update.new[a:name] = 1
   1513 <a href="#l1494" class="line" id="l1494">   1494</a>   endif
   1514 <a href="#l1495" class="line" id="l1495">   1495</a> 
   1515 <a href="#l1496" class="line" id="l1496">   1496</a>   let more = len(get(job, &#39;queue&#39;, []))
   1516 <a href="#l1497" class="line" id="l1497">   1497</a>   let result = job.error ? join(job.lines, &quot;\n&quot;) : s:last_non_empty_line(job.lines)
   1517 <a href="#l1498" class="line" id="l1498">   1498</a>   if len(result)
   1518 <a href="#l1499" class="line" id="l1499">   1499</a>     call s:log(s:bullet_for(job), a:name, result)
   1519 <a href="#l1500" class="line" id="l1500">   1500</a>   endif
   1520 <a href="#l1501" class="line" id="l1501">   1501</a> 
   1521 <a href="#l1502" class="line" id="l1502">   1502</a>   if !job.error &amp;&amp; more
   1522 <a href="#l1503" class="line" id="l1503">   1503</a>     let job.spec.queue = job.queue
   1523 <a href="#l1504" class="line" id="l1504">   1504</a>     let s:update.todo[a:name] = job.spec
   1524 <a href="#l1505" class="line" id="l1505">   1505</a>   else
   1525 <a href="#l1506" class="line" id="l1506">   1506</a>     let s:update.bar .= s:bullet_for(job, &#39;=&#39;)
   1526 <a href="#l1507" class="line" id="l1507">   1507</a>     call s:bar()
   1527 <a href="#l1508" class="line" id="l1508">   1508</a>   endif
   1528 <a href="#l1509" class="line" id="l1509">   1509</a> endfunction
   1529 <a href="#l1510" class="line" id="l1510">   1510</a> 
   1530 <a href="#l1511" class="line" id="l1511">   1511</a> function! s:bar()
   1531 <a href="#l1512" class="line" id="l1512">   1512</a>   if s:switch_in()
   1532 <a href="#l1513" class="line" id="l1513">   1513</a>     let total = len(s:update.all)
   1533 <a href="#l1514" class="line" id="l1514">   1514</a>     call setline(1, (s:update.pull ? &#39;Updating&#39; : &#39;Installing&#39;).
   1534 <a href="#l1515" class="line" id="l1515">   1515</a>           \ &#39; plugins (&#39;.len(s:update.bar).&#39;/&#39;.total.&#39;)&#39;)
   1535 <a href="#l1516" class="line" id="l1516">   1516</a>     call s:progress_bar(2, s:update.bar, total)
   1536 <a href="#l1517" class="line" id="l1517">   1517</a>     call s:switch_out()
   1537 <a href="#l1518" class="line" id="l1518">   1518</a>   endif
   1538 <a href="#l1519" class="line" id="l1519">   1519</a> endfunction
   1539 <a href="#l1520" class="line" id="l1520">   1520</a> 
   1540 <a href="#l1521" class="line" id="l1521">   1521</a> function! s:logpos(name)
   1541 <a href="#l1522" class="line" id="l1522">   1522</a>   let max = line(&#39;$&#39;)
   1542 <a href="#l1523" class="line" id="l1523">   1523</a>   for i in range(4, max &gt; 4 ? max : 4)
   1543 <a href="#l1524" class="line" id="l1524">   1524</a>     if getline(i) =~# &#39;^[-+x*] &#39;.a:name.&#39;:&#39;
   1544 <a href="#l1525" class="line" id="l1525">   1525</a>       for j in range(i + 1, max &gt; 5 ? max : 5)
   1545 <a href="#l1526" class="line" id="l1526">   1526</a>         if getline(j) !~ &#39;^ &#39;
   1546 <a href="#l1527" class="line" id="l1527">   1527</a>           return [i, j - 1]
   1547 <a href="#l1528" class="line" id="l1528">   1528</a>         endif
   1548 <a href="#l1529" class="line" id="l1529">   1529</a>       endfor
   1549 <a href="#l1530" class="line" id="l1530">   1530</a>       return [i, i]
   1550 <a href="#l1531" class="line" id="l1531">   1531</a>     endif
   1551 <a href="#l1532" class="line" id="l1532">   1532</a>   endfor
   1552 <a href="#l1533" class="line" id="l1533">   1533</a>   return [0, 0]
   1553 <a href="#l1534" class="line" id="l1534">   1534</a> endfunction
   1554 <a href="#l1535" class="line" id="l1535">   1535</a> 
   1555 <a href="#l1536" class="line" id="l1536">   1536</a> function! s:log(bullet, name, lines)
   1556 <a href="#l1537" class="line" id="l1537">   1537</a>   if s:switch_in()
   1557 <a href="#l1538" class="line" id="l1538">   1538</a>     let [b, e] = s:logpos(a:name)
   1558 <a href="#l1539" class="line" id="l1539">   1539</a>     if b &gt; 0
   1559 <a href="#l1540" class="line" id="l1540">   1540</a>       silent execute printf(&#39;%d,%d d _&#39;, b, e)
   1560 <a href="#l1541" class="line" id="l1541">   1541</a>       if b &gt; winheight(&#39;.&#39;)
   1561 <a href="#l1542" class="line" id="l1542">   1542</a>         let b = 4
   1562 <a href="#l1543" class="line" id="l1543">   1543</a>       endif
   1563 <a href="#l1544" class="line" id="l1544">   1544</a>     else
   1564 <a href="#l1545" class="line" id="l1545">   1545</a>       let b = 4
   1565 <a href="#l1546" class="line" id="l1546">   1546</a>     endif
   1566 <a href="#l1547" class="line" id="l1547">   1547</a>     &quot; FIXME For some reason, nomodifiable is set after :d in vim8
   1567 <a href="#l1548" class="line" id="l1548">   1548</a>     setlocal modifiable
   1568 <a href="#l1549" class="line" id="l1549">   1549</a>     call append(b - 1, s:format_message(a:bullet, a:name, a:lines))
   1569 <a href="#l1550" class="line" id="l1550">   1550</a>     call s:switch_out()
   1570 <a href="#l1551" class="line" id="l1551">   1551</a>   endif
   1571 <a href="#l1552" class="line" id="l1552">   1552</a> endfunction

   1590 <a href="#l1571" class="line" id="l1571">   1571</a> function! s:tick()
   1591 <a href="#l1572" class="line" id="l1572">   1572</a>   let pull = s:update.pull
   1592 <a href="#l1573" class="line" id="l1573">   1573</a>   let prog = s:progress_opt(s:nvim || s:vim8)
   1593 <a href="#l1574" class="line" id="l1574">   1574</a> while 1 &quot; Without TCO, Vim stack is bound to explode
   1594 <a href="#l1575" class="line" id="l1575">   1575</a>   if empty(s:update.todo)
   1595 <a href="#l1576" class="line" id="l1576">   1576</a>     if empty(s:jobs) &amp;&amp; !s:update.fin
   1596 <a href="#l1577" class="line" id="l1577">   1577</a>       call s:update_finish()
   1597 <a href="#l1578" class="line" id="l1578">   1578</a>       let s:update.fin = 1
   1598 <a href="#l1579" class="line" id="l1579">   1579</a>     endif
   1599 <a href="#l1580" class="line" id="l1580">   1580</a>     return
   1600 <a href="#l1581" class="line" id="l1581">   1581</a>   endif
   1601 <a href="#l1582" class="line" id="l1582">   1582</a> 
   1602 <a href="#l1583" class="line" id="l1583">   1583</a>   let name = keys(s:update.todo)[0]
   1603 <a href="#l1584" class="line" id="l1584">   1584</a>   let spec = remove(s:update.todo, name)
   1604 <a href="#l1585" class="line" id="l1585">   1585</a>   if get(spec, &#39;abort&#39;, 0)
   1605 <a href="#l1586" class="line" id="l1586">   1586</a>     call s:mark_aborted(name, &#39;Skipped&#39;)
   1606 <a href="#l1587" class="line" id="l1587">   1587</a>     call s:reap(name)
   1607 <a href="#l1588" class="line" id="l1588">   1588</a>     continue
   1608 <a href="#l1589" class="line" id="l1589">   1589</a>   endif
   1609 <a href="#l1590" class="line" id="l1590">   1590</a> 
   1610 <a href="#l1591" class="line" id="l1591">   1591</a>   let queue = get(spec, &#39;queue&#39;, [])
   1611 <a href="#l1592" class="line" id="l1592">   1592</a>   let new = empty(globpath(spec.dir, &#39;.git&#39;, 1))
   1612 <a href="#l1593" class="line" id="l1593">   1593</a> 
   1613 <a href="#l1594" class="line" id="l1594">   1594</a>   if empty(queue)
   1614 <a href="#l1595" class="line" id="l1595">   1595</a>     call s:log(new ? &#39;+&#39; : &#39;*&#39;, name, pull ? &#39;Updating ...&#39; : &#39;Installing ...&#39;)
   1615 <a href="#l1596" class="line" id="l1596">   1596</a>     redraw
   1616 <a href="#l1597" class="line" id="l1597">   1597</a>   endif
   1617 <a href="#l1598" class="line" id="l1598">   1598</a> 
   1618 <a href="#l1599" class="line" id="l1599">   1599</a>   let has_tag = has_key(spec, &#39;tag&#39;)
   1619 <a href="#l1600" class="line" id="l1600">   1600</a>   if len(queue)
   1620 <a href="#l1601" class="line" id="l1601">   1601</a>     call s:spawn(name, spec, queue, { &#39;dir&#39;: spec.dir })
   1621 <a href="#l1602" class="line" id="l1602">   1602</a>   elseif !new
   1622 <a href="#l1603" class="line" id="l1603">   1603</a>     let [error, _] = s:git_validate(spec, 0)
   1623 <a href="#l1604" class="line" id="l1604">   1604</a>     if empty(error)
   1624 <a href="#l1605" class="line" id="l1605">   1605</a>       if pull
   1625 <a href="#l1606" class="line" id="l1606">   1606</a>         let cmd = s:disable_credential_helper() ? [&#39;git&#39;, &#39;-c&#39;, &#39;credential.helper=&#39;, &#39;fetch&#39;] : [&#39;git&#39;, &#39;fetch&#39;]
   1626 <a href="#l1607" class="line" id="l1607">   1607</a>         if has_tag &amp;&amp; !empty(globpath(spec.dir, &#39;.git/shallow&#39;))
   1627 <a href="#l1608" class="line" id="l1608">   1608</a>           call extend(cmd, [&#39;--depth&#39;, &#39;99999999&#39;])
   1628 <a href="#l1609" class="line" id="l1609">   1609</a>         endif
   1629 <a href="#l1610" class="line" id="l1610">   1610</a>         if !empty(prog)
   1630 <a href="#l1611" class="line" id="l1611">   1611</a>           call add(cmd, prog)
   1631 <a href="#l1612" class="line" id="l1612">   1612</a>         endif
   1632 <a href="#l1613" class="line" id="l1613">   1613</a>         let queue = [cmd, split(&#39;git remote set-head origin -a&#39;)]
   1633 <a href="#l1614" class="line" id="l1614">   1614</a>         if !has_tag &amp;&amp; !has_key(spec, &#39;commit&#39;)
   1634 <a href="#l1615" class="line" id="l1615">   1615</a>           call extend(queue, [function(&#39;s:checkout_command&#39;), function(&#39;s:merge_command&#39;)])
   1635 <a href="#l1616" class="line" id="l1616">   1616</a>         endif
   1636 <a href="#l1617" class="line" id="l1617">   1617</a>         call s:spawn(name, spec, queue, { &#39;dir&#39;: spec.dir })
   1637 <a href="#l1618" class="line" id="l1618">   1618</a>       else
   1638 <a href="#l1619" class="line" id="l1619">   1619</a>         let s:jobs[name] = { &#39;running&#39;: 0, &#39;lines&#39;: [&#39;Already installed&#39;], &#39;error&#39;: 0 }
   1639 <a href="#l1620" class="line" id="l1620">   1620</a>       endif
   1640 <a href="#l1621" class="line" id="l1621">   1621</a>     else
   1641 <a href="#l1622" class="line" id="l1622">   1622</a>       let s:jobs[name] = { &#39;running&#39;: 0, &#39;lines&#39;: s:lines(error), &#39;error&#39;: 1 }
   1642 <a href="#l1623" class="line" id="l1623">   1623</a>     endif
   1643 <a href="#l1624" class="line" id="l1624">   1624</a>   else
   1644 <a href="#l1625" class="line" id="l1625">   1625</a>     let cmd = [&#39;git&#39;, &#39;clone&#39;]
   1645 <a href="#l1626" class="line" id="l1626">   1626</a>     if !has_tag
   1646 <a href="#l1627" class="line" id="l1627">   1627</a>       call extend(cmd, s:clone_opt)
   1647 <a href="#l1628" class="line" id="l1628">   1628</a>     endif
   1648 <a href="#l1629" class="line" id="l1629">   1629</a>     if !empty(prog)
   1649 <a href="#l1630" class="line" id="l1630">   1630</a>       call add(cmd, prog)
   1650 <a href="#l1631" class="line" id="l1631">   1631</a>     endif
   1651 <a href="#l1632" class="line" id="l1632">   1632</a>     call s:spawn(name, spec, [extend(cmd, [spec.uri, s:trim(spec.dir)]), function(&#39;s:checkout_command&#39;), function(&#39;s:merge_command&#39;)], { &#39;new&#39;: 1 })
   1652 <a href="#l1633" class="line" id="l1633">   1633</a>   endif
   1653 <a href="#l1634" class="line" id="l1634">   1634</a> 
   1654 <a href="#l1635" class="line" id="l1635">   1635</a>   if !s:jobs[name].running
   1655 <a href="#l1636" class="line" id="l1636">   1636</a>     call s:reap(name)
   1656 <a href="#l1637" class="line" id="l1637">   1637</a>   endif
   1657 <a href="#l1638" class="line" id="l1638">   1638</a>   if len(s:jobs) &gt;= s:update.threads
   1658 <a href="#l1639" class="line" id="l1639">   1639</a>     break
   1659 <a href="#l1640" class="line" id="l1640">   1640</a>   endif
   1660 <a href="#l1641" class="line" id="l1641">   1641</a> endwhile
   1661 <a href="#l1642" class="line" id="l1642">   1642</a> endfunction

   1706 <a href="#l1687" class="line" id="l1687">   1687</a> class Buffer(object):
   1707 <a href="#l1688" class="line" id="l1688">   1688</a>   def __init__(self, lock, num_plugs, is_pull):
   1708 <a href="#l1689" class="line" id="l1689">   1689</a>     self.bar = &#39;&#39;
   1709 <a href="#l1690" class="line" id="l1690">   1690</a>     self.event = &#39;Updating&#39; if is_pull else &#39;Installing&#39;
   1710 <a href="#l1691" class="line" id="l1691">   1691</a>     self.lock = lock
   1711 <a href="#l1692" class="line" id="l1692">   1692</a>     self.maxy = int(vim.eval(&#39;winheight(&quot;.&quot;)&#39;))

   1714 <a href="#l1695" class="line" id="l1695">   1695</a>   def __where(self, name):
   1715 <a href="#l1696" class="line" id="l1696">   1696</a>     &quot;&quot;&quot; Find first line with name in current buffer. Return line num. &quot;&quot;&quot;
   1716 <a href="#l1697" class="line" id="l1697">   1697</a>     found, lnum = False, 0
   1717 <a href="#l1698" class="line" id="l1698">   1698</a>     matcher = re.compile(&#39;^[-+x*] {0}:&#39;.format(name))
   1718 <a href="#l1699" class="line" id="l1699">   1699</a>     for line in vim.current.buffer:
   1719 <a href="#l1700" class="line" id="l1700">   1700</a>       if matcher.search(line) is not None:
   1720 <a href="#l1701" class="line" id="l1701">   1701</a>         found = True
   1721 <a href="#l1702" class="line" id="l1702">   1702</a>         break
   1722 <a href="#l1703" class="line" id="l1703">   1703</a>       lnum += 1
   1723 <a href="#l1704" class="line" id="l1704">   1704</a> 
   1724 <a href="#l1705" class="line" id="l1705">   1705</a>     if not found:
   1725 <a href="#l1706" class="line" id="l1706">   1706</a>       lnum = -1
   1726 <a href="#l1707" class="line" id="l1707">   1707</a>     return lnum
   1727 <a href="#l1708" class="line" id="l1708">   1708</a> 
   1728 <a href="#l1709" class="line" id="l1709">   1709</a>   def header(self):
   1729 <a href="#l1710" class="line" id="l1710">   1710</a>     curbuf = vim.current.buffer
   1730 <a href="#l1711" class="line" id="l1711">   1711</a>     curbuf[0] = self.event + &#39; plugins ({0}/{1})&#39;.format(len(self.bar), self.num_plugs)
   1731 <a href="#l1712" class="line" id="l1712">   1712</a> 
   1732 <a href="#l1713" class="line" id="l1713">   1713</a>     num_spaces = self.num_plugs - len(self.bar)
   1733 <a href="#l1714" class="line" id="l1714">   1714</a>     curbuf[1] = &#39;[{0}{1}]&#39;.format(self.bar, num_spaces * &#39; &#39;)
   1734 <a href="#l1715" class="line" id="l1715">   1715</a> 
   1735 <a href="#l1716" class="line" id="l1716">   1716</a>     with self.lock:
   1736 <a href="#l1717" class="line" id="l1717">   1717</a>       vim.command(&#39;normal! 2G&#39;)
   1737 <a href="#l1718" class="line" id="l1718">   1718</a>       vim.command(&#39;redraw&#39;)

   1739 <a href="#l1720" class="line" id="l1720">   1720</a>   def write(self, action, name, lines):
   1740 <a href="#l1721" class="line" id="l1721">   1721</a>     first, rest = lines[0], lines[1:]
   1741 <a href="#l1722" class="line" id="l1722">   1722</a>     msg = [&#39;{0} {1}{2}{3}&#39;.format(action, name, &#39;: &#39; if first else &#39;&#39;, first)]
   1742 <a href="#l1723" class="line" id="l1723">   1723</a>     msg.extend([&#39;    &#39; + line for line in rest])
   1743 <a href="#l1724" class="line" id="l1724">   1724</a> 
   1744 <a href="#l1725" class="line" id="l1725">   1725</a>     try:
   1745 <a href="#l1726" class="line" id="l1726">   1726</a>       if action == Action.ERROR:
   1746 <a href="#l1727" class="line" id="l1727">   1727</a>         self.bar += &#39;x&#39;
   1747 <a href="#l1728" class="line" id="l1728">   1728</a>         vim.command(&quot;call add(s:update.errors, &#39;{0}&#39;)&quot;.format(name))
   1748 <a href="#l1729" class="line" id="l1729">   1729</a>       elif action == Action.DONE:
   1749 <a href="#l1730" class="line" id="l1730">   1730</a>         self.bar += &#39;=&#39;
   1750 <a href="#l1731" class="line" id="l1731">   1731</a> 
   1751 <a href="#l1732" class="line" id="l1732">   1732</a>       curbuf = vim.current.buffer
   1752 <a href="#l1733" class="line" id="l1733">   1733</a>       lnum = self.__where(name)
   1753 <a href="#l1734" class="line" id="l1734">   1734</a>       if lnum != -1: # Found matching line num
   1754 <a href="#l1735" class="line" id="l1735">   1735</a>         del curbuf[lnum]
   1755 <a href="#l1736" class="line" id="l1736">   1736</a>         if lnum &gt; self.maxy and action in set([Action.INSTALL, Action.UPDATE]):
   1756 <a href="#l1737" class="line" id="l1737">   1737</a>           lnum = 3
   1757 <a href="#l1738" class="line" id="l1738">   1738</a>       else:
   1758 <a href="#l1739" class="line" id="l1739">   1739</a>         lnum = 3
   1759 <a href="#l1740" class="line" id="l1740">   1740</a>       curbuf.append(msg, lnum)
   1760 <a href="#l1741" class="line" id="l1741">   1741</a> 
   1761 <a href="#l1742" class="line" id="l1742">   1742</a>       self.header()
   1762 <a href="#l1743" class="line" id="l1743">   1743</a>     except vim.error:
   1763 <a href="#l1744" class="line" id="l1744">   1744</a>       pass
   1764 <a href="#l1745" class="line" id="l1745">   1745</a> 
   1765 <a href="#l1746" class="line" id="l1746">   1746</a> class Command(object):
   1766 <a href="#l1747" class="line" id="l1747">   1747</a>   CD = &#39;cd /d&#39; if G_IS_WIN else &#39;cd&#39;
   1767 <a href="#l1748" class="line" id="l1748">   1748</a> 
   1768 <a href="#l1749" class="line" id="l1749">   1749</a>   def __init__(self, cmd, cmd_dir=None, timeout=60, cb=None, clean=None):
   1769 <a href="#l1750" class="line" id="l1750">   1750</a>     self.cmd = cmd
   1770 <a href="#l1751" class="line" id="l1751">   1751</a>     if cmd_dir:
   1771 <a href="#l1752" class="line" id="l1752">   1752</a>       self.cmd = &#39;{0} {1} &amp;&amp; {2}&#39;.format(Command.CD, cmd_dir, self.cmd)
   1772 <a href="#l1753" class="line" id="l1753">   1753</a>     self.timeout = timeout
   1773 <a href="#l1754" class="line" id="l1754">   1754</a>     self.callback = cb if cb else (lambda msg: None)
   1774 <a href="#l1755" class="line" id="l1755">   1755</a>     self.clean = clean if clean else (lambda: None)

   1776 <a href="#l1757" class="line" id="l1757">   1757</a> 
   1777 <a href="#l1758" class="line" id="l1758">   1758</a>   @property
   1778 <a href="#l1759" class="line" id="l1759">   1759</a>   def alive(self):
   1779 <a href="#l1760" class="line" id="l1760">   1760</a>     &quot;&quot;&quot; Returns true only if command still running. &quot;&quot;&quot;
   1780 <a href="#l1761" class="line" id="l1761">   1761</a>     return self.proc and self.proc.poll() is None
   1781 <a href="#l1762" class="line" id="l1762">   1762</a> 
   1782 <a href="#l1763" class="line" id="l1763">   1763</a>   def execute(self, ntries=3):
   1783 <a href="#l1764" class="line" id="l1764">   1764</a>     &quot;&quot;&quot; Execute the command with ntries if CmdTimedOut.
   1784 <a href="#l1765" class="line" id="l1765">   1765</a>         Returns the output of the command if no Exception.
   1785 <a href="#l1766" class="line" id="l1766">   1766</a>     &quot;&quot;&quot;
   1786 <a href="#l1767" class="line" id="l1767">   1767</a>     attempt, finished, limit = 0, False, self.timeout
   1787 <a href="#l1768" class="line" id="l1768">   1768</a> 
   1788 <a href="#l1769" class="line" id="l1769">   1769</a>     while not finished:
   1789 <a href="#l1770" class="line" id="l1770">   1770</a>       try:
   1790 <a href="#l1771" class="line" id="l1771">   1771</a>         attempt += 1
   1791 <a href="#l1772" class="line" id="l1772">   1772</a>         result = self.try_command()
   1792 <a href="#l1773" class="line" id="l1773">   1773</a>         finished = True
   1793 <a href="#l1774" class="line" id="l1774">   1774</a>         return result
   1794 <a href="#l1775" class="line" id="l1775">   1775</a>       except CmdTimedOut:
   1795 <a href="#l1776" class="line" id="l1776">   1776</a>         if attempt != ntries:
   1796 <a href="#l1777" class="line" id="l1777">   1777</a>           self.notify_retry()
   1797 <a href="#l1778" class="line" id="l1778">   1778</a>           self.timeout += limit
   1798 <a href="#l1779" class="line" id="l1779">   1779</a>         else:
   1799 <a href="#l1780" class="line" id="l1780">   1780</a>           raise
   1800 <a href="#l1781" class="line" id="l1781">   1781</a> 
   1801 <a href="#l1782" class="line" id="l1782">   1782</a>   def notify_retry(self):
   1802 <a href="#l1783" class="line" id="l1783">   1783</a>     &quot;&quot;&quot; Retry required for command, notify user. &quot;&quot;&quot;
   1803 <a href="#l1784" class="line" id="l1784">   1784</a>     for count in range(3, 0, -1):
   1804 <a href="#l1785" class="line" id="l1785">   1785</a>       if G_STOP.is_set():
   1805 <a href="#l1786" class="line" id="l1786">   1786</a>         raise KeyboardInterrupt
   1806 <a href="#l1787" class="line" id="l1787">   1787</a>       msg = &#39;Timeout. Will retry in {0} second{1} ...&#39;.format(
   1807 <a href="#l1788" class="line" id="l1788">   1788</a>             count, &#39;s&#39; if count != 1 else &#39;&#39;)
   1808 <a href="#l1789" class="line" id="l1789">   1789</a>       self.callback([msg])
   1809 <a href="#l1790" class="line" id="l1790">   1790</a>       time.sleep(1)
   1810 <a href="#l1791" class="line" id="l1791">   1791</a>     self.callback([&#39;Retrying ...&#39;])
   1811 <a href="#l1792" class="line" id="l1792">   1792</a> 
   1812 <a href="#l1793" class="line" id="l1793">   1793</a>   def try_command(self):
   1813 <a href="#l1794" class="line" id="l1794">   1794</a>     &quot;&quot;&quot; Execute a cmd &amp; poll for callback. Returns list of output.
   1814 <a href="#l1795" class="line" id="l1795">   1795</a>         Raises CmdFailed   -&gt; return code for Popen isn&#39;t 0
   1815 <a href="#l1796" class="line" id="l1796">   1796</a>         Raises CmdTimedOut -&gt; command exceeded timeout without new output
   1816 <a href="#l1797" class="line" id="l1797">   1797</a>     &quot;&quot;&quot;
   1817 <a href="#l1798" class="line" id="l1798">   1798</a>     first_line = True
   1818 <a href="#l1799" class="line" id="l1799">   1799</a> 
   1819 <a href="#l1800" class="line" id="l1800">   1800</a>     try:
   1820 <a href="#l1801" class="line" id="l1801">   1801</a>       tfile = tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(mode=&#39;w+b&#39;)
   1821 <a href="#l1802" class="line" id="l1802">   1802</a>       preexec_fn = not G_IS_WIN and os.setsid or None
   1822 <a href="#l1803" class="line" id="l1803">   1803</a>       self.proc = subprocess.Popen(self.cmd, stdout=tfile,
   1823 <a href="#l1804" class="line" id="l1804">   1804</a>                                    stderr=subprocess.STDOUT,
   1824 <a href="#l1805" class="line" id="l1805">   1805</a>                                    stdin=subprocess.PIPE, shell=True,
   1825 <a href="#l1806" class="line" id="l1806">   1806</a>                                    preexec_fn=preexec_fn)
   1826 <a href="#l1807" class="line" id="l1807">   1807</a>       thrd = thr.Thread(target=(lambda proc: proc.wait()), args=(self.proc,))
   1827 <a href="#l1808" class="line" id="l1808">   1808</a>       thrd.start()
   1828 <a href="#l1809" class="line" id="l1809">   1809</a> 
   1829 <a href="#l1810" class="line" id="l1810">   1810</a>       thread_not_started = True
   1830 <a href="#l1811" class="line" id="l1811">   1811</a>       while thread_not_started:
   1831 <a href="#l1812" class="line" id="l1812">   1812</a>         try:
   1832 <a href="#l1813" class="line" id="l1813">   1813</a>           thrd.join(0.1)
   1833 <a href="#l1814" class="line" id="l1814">   1814</a>           thread_not_started = False
   1834 <a href="#l1815" class="line" id="l1815">   1815</a>         except RuntimeError:
   1835 <a href="#l1816" class="line" id="l1816">   1816</a>           pass
   1836 <a href="#l1817" class="line" id="l1817">   1817</a> 
   1837 <a href="#l1818" class="line" id="l1818">   1818</a>       while self.alive:
   1838 <a href="#l1819" class="line" id="l1819">   1819</a>         if G_STOP.is_set():
   1839 <a href="#l1820" class="line" id="l1820">   1820</a>           raise KeyboardInterrupt
   1840 <a href="#l1821" class="line" id="l1821">   1821</a> 
   1841 <a href="#l1822" class="line" id="l1822">   1822</a>         if first_line or random.random() &lt; G_LOG_PROB:
   1842 <a href="#l1823" class="line" id="l1823">   1823</a>           first_line = False
   1843 <a href="#l1824" class="line" id="l1824">   1824</a>           line = &#39;&#39; if G_IS_WIN else nonblock_read(tfile.name)
   1844 <a href="#l1825" class="line" id="l1825">   1825</a>           if line:
   1845 <a href="#l1826" class="line" id="l1826">   1826</a>             self.callback([line])
   1846 <a href="#l1827" class="line" id="l1827">   1827</a> 
   1847 <a href="#l1828" class="line" id="l1828">   1828</a>         time_diff = time.time() - os.path.getmtime(tfile.name)
   1848 <a href="#l1829" class="line" id="l1829">   1829</a>         if time_diff &gt; self.timeout:
   1849 <a href="#l1830" class="line" id="l1830">   1830</a>           raise CmdTimedOut([&#39;Timeout!&#39;])
   1850 <a href="#l1831" class="line" id="l1831">   1831</a> 
   1851 <a href="#l1832" class="line" id="l1832">   1832</a>         thrd.join(0.5)
   1852 <a href="#l1833" class="line" id="l1833">   1833</a> 
   1853 <a href="#l1834" class="line" id="l1834">   1834</a>       tfile.seek(0)
   1854 <a href="#l1835" class="line" id="l1835">   1835</a>       result = [line.decode(&#39;utf-8&#39;, &#39;replace&#39;).rstrip() for line in tfile]
   1855 <a href="#l1836" class="line" id="l1836">   1836</a> 
   1856 <a href="#l1837" class="line" id="l1837">   1837</a>       if self.proc.returncode != 0:
   1857 <a href="#l1838" class="line" id="l1838">   1838</a>         raise CmdFailed([&#39;&#39;] + result)
   1858 <a href="#l1839" class="line" id="l1839">   1839</a> 
   1859 <a href="#l1840" class="line" id="l1840">   1840</a>       return result
   1860 <a href="#l1841" class="line" id="l1841">   1841</a>     except:
   1861 <a href="#l1842" class="line" id="l1842">   1842</a>       self.terminate()
   1862 <a href="#l1843" class="line" id="l1843">   1843</a>       raise
   1863 <a href="#l1844" class="line" id="l1844">   1844</a> 
   1864 <a href="#l1845" class="line" id="l1845">   1845</a>   def terminate(self):
   1865 <a href="#l1846" class="line" id="l1846">   1846</a>     &quot;&quot;&quot; Terminate process and cleanup. &quot;&quot;&quot;
   1866 <a href="#l1847" class="line" id="l1847">   1847</a>     if self.alive:
   1867 <a href="#l1848" class="line" id="l1848">   1848</a>       if G_IS_WIN:
   1868 <a href="#l1849" class="line" id="l1849">   1849</a>         os.kill(self.proc.pid, signal.SIGINT)
   1869 <a href="#l1850" class="line" id="l1850">   1850</a>       else:

   1891 <a href="#l1872" class="line" id="l1872">   1872</a>     except KeyboardInterrupt:

   1897 <a href="#l1878" class="line" id="l1878">   1878</a>       self.write(Action.ERROR, self.name, msg.split(&#39;\n&#39;))

   1929 <a href="#l1910" class="line" id="l1910">   1910</a>     actual_uri = self.repo_uri()

   1940 <a href="#l1921" class="line" id="l1921">   1921</a>

   1946 <a href="#l1927" class="line" id="l1927">   1927</a>       com = Command(cmd, self.args[&#39;dir&#39;], G_TIMEOUT, callback)
   1947 <a href="#l1928" class="line" id="l1928">   1928</a>       result = com.execute(G_RETRIES)

   1999 <a href="#l1980" class="line" id="l1980">   1980</a> def nonblock_read(fname):
   2000 <a href="#l1981" class="line" id="l1981">   1981</a>   &quot;&quot;&quot; Read a file with nonblock flag. Return the last line. &quot;&quot;&quot;
   2001 <a href="#l1982" class="line" id="l1982">   1982</a>   fread = os.open(fname, os.O_RDONLY | os.O_NONBLOCK)
   2002 <a href="#l1983" class="line" id="l1983">   1983</a>   buf = os.read(fread, 100000).decode(&#39;utf-8&#39;, &#39;replace&#39;)
   2003 <a href="#l1984" class="line" id="l1984">   1984</a>   os.close(fread)
   2004 <a href="#l1985" class="line" id="l1985">   1985</a> 
   2005 <a href="#l1986" class="line" id="l1986">   1986</a>   line = buf.rstrip(&#39;\r\n&#39;)
   2006 <a href="#l1987" class="line" id="l1987">   1987</a>   left = max(line.rfind(&#39;\r&#39;), line.rfind(&#39;\n&#39;))
   2007 <a href="#l1988" class="line" id="l1988">   1988</a>   if left != -1:
   2008 <a href="#l1989" class="line" id="l1989">   1989</a>     left += 1
   2009 <a href="#l1990" class="line" id="l1990">   1990</a>     line = line[left:]
   2010 <a href="#l1991" class="line" id="l1991">   1991</a> 
   2011 <a href="#l1992" class="line" id="l1992">   1992</a>   return line
