   2278 <a href="#l2259" class="line" id="l2259">   2259</a> function! s:shellesc_cmd(arg, script)
   2279 <a href="#l2260" class="line" id="l2260">   2260</a>   let escaped = substitute(&#39;&quot;&#39;.a:arg.&#39;&quot;&#39;, &#39;[&amp;|&lt;&gt;()@^!&quot;]&#39;, &#39;^&amp;&#39;, &#39;g&#39;)
   2280 <a href="#l2261" class="line" id="l2261">   2261</a>   return substitute(escaped, &#39;%&#39;, (a:script ? &#39;%&#39; : &#39;^&#39;) . &#39;&amp;&#39;, &#39;g&#39;)
   2281 <a href="#l2262" class="line" id="l2262">   2262</a> endfunction
   2282 <a href="#l2263" class="line" id="l2263">   2263</a> 
   2283 <a href="#l2264" class="line" id="l2264">   2264</a> function! s:shellesc_ps1(arg)
   2284 <a href="#l2265" class="line" id="l2265">   2265</a>   return &quot;&#39;&quot;.substitute(escape(a:arg, &#39;\&quot;&#39;), &quot;&#39;&quot;, &quot;&#39;&#39;&quot;, &#39;g&#39;).&quot;&#39;&quot;
   2285 <a href="#l2266" class="line" id="l2266">   2266</a> endfunction
   2286 <a href="#l2267" class="line" id="l2267">   2267</a> 
   2287 <a href="#l2268" class="line" id="l2268">   2268</a> function! s:shellesc_sh(arg)
   2288 <a href="#l2269" class="line" id="l2269">   2269</a>   return &quot;&#39;&quot;.substitute(a:arg, &quot;&#39;&quot;, &quot;&#39;\\\\&#39;&#39;&quot;, &#39;g&#39;).&quot;&#39;&quot;
   2289 <a href="#l2270" class="line" id="l2270">   2270</a> endfunction
   2290 <a href="#l2271" class="line" id="l2271">   2271</a> 
   2291 <a href="#l2272" class="line" id="l2272">   2272</a> &quot; Escape the shell argument based on the shell.
   2292 <a href="#l2273" class="line" id="l2273">   2273</a> &quot; Vim and Neovim&#39;s shellescape() are insufficient.
   2293 <a href="#l2274" class="line" id="l2274">   2274</a> &quot; 1. shellslash determines whether to use single/double quotes.
   2294 <a href="#l2275" class="line" id="l2275">   2275</a> &quot;    Double-quote escaping is fragile for cmd.exe.
   2295 <a href="#l2276" class="line" id="l2276">   2276</a> &quot; 2. It does not work for powershell.
   2296 <a href="#l2277" class="line" id="l2277">   2277</a> &quot; 3. It does not work for *sh shells if the command is executed
   2297 <a href="#l2278" class="line" id="l2278">   2278</a> &quot;    via cmd.exe (ie. cmd.exe /c sh -c command command_args)
   2298 <a href="#l2279" class="line" id="l2279">   2279</a> &quot; 4. It does not support batchfile syntax.
   2299 <a href="#l2280" class="line" id="l2280">   2280</a> &quot;
   2300 <a href="#l2281" class="line" id="l2281">   2281</a> &quot; Accepts an optional dictionary with the following keys:
   2301 <a href="#l2282" class="line" id="l2282">   2282</a> &quot; - shell: same as Vim/Neovim &#39;shell&#39; option.
   2302 <a href="#l2283" class="line" id="l2283">   2283</a> &quot;          If unset, fallback to &#39;cmd.exe&#39; on Windows or &#39;sh&#39;.
   2303 <a href="#l2284" class="line" id="l2284">   2284</a> &quot; - script: If truthy and shell is cmd.exe, escape for batchfile syntax.
   2304 <a href="#l2285" class="line" id="l2285">   2285</a> function! plug#shellescape(arg, ...)
   2305 <a href="#l2286" class="line" id="l2286">   2286</a>   if a:arg =~# &#39;^[A-Za-z0-9_/:.-]\+$&#39;
   2306 <a href="#l2287" class="line" id="l2287">   2287</a>     return a:arg
   2307 <a href="#l2288" class="line" id="l2288">   2288</a>   endif
   2308 <a href="#l2289" class="line" id="l2289">   2289</a>   let opts = a:0 &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; type(a:1) == s:TYPE.dict ? a:1 : {}
   2309 <a href="#l2290" class="line" id="l2290">   2290</a>   let shell = get(opts, &#39;shell&#39;, s:is_win ? &#39;cmd.exe&#39; : &#39;sh&#39;)
   2310 <a href="#l2291" class="line" id="l2291">   2291</a>   let script = get(opts, &#39;script&#39;, 1)
   2311 <a href="#l2292" class="line" id="l2292">   2292</a>   if shell =~# &#39;cmd\(\.exe\)\?$&#39;
   2312 <a href="#l2293" class="line" id="l2293">   2293</a>     return s:shellesc_cmd(a:arg, script)
   2313 <a href="#l2294" class="line" id="l2294">   2294</a>   elseif s:is_powershell(shell)
   2314 <a href="#l2295" class="line" id="l2295">   2295</a>     return s:shellesc_ps1(a:arg)
   2315 <a href="#l2296" class="line" id="l2296">   2296</a>   endif
   2316 <a href="#l2297" class="line" id="l2297">   2297</a>   return s:shellesc_sh(a:arg)
   2317 <a href="#l2298" class="line" id="l2298">   2298</a> endfunction
   2318 <a href="#l2299" class="line" id="l2299">   2299</a> 
   2319 <a href="#l2300" class="line" id="l2300">   2300</a> function! s:glob_dir(path)
   2320 <a href="#l2301" class="line" id="l2301">   2301</a>   return map(filter(s:glob(a:path, &#39;**&#39;), &#39;isdirectory(v:val)&#39;), &#39;s:dirpath(v:val)&#39;)
   2321 <a href="#l2302" class="line" id="l2302">   2302</a> endfunction
   2322 <a href="#l2303" class="line" id="l2303">   2303</a> 
   2323 <a href="#l2304" class="line" id="l2304">   2304</a> function! s:progress_bar(line, bar, total)
   2324 <a href="#l2305" class="line" id="l2305">   2305</a>   call setline(a:line, &#39;[&#39; . s:lpad(a:bar, a:total) . &#39;]&#39;)
   2325 <a href="#l2306" class="line" id="l2306">   2306</a> endfunction
   2326 <a href="#l2307" class="line" id="l2307">   2307</a> 
   2327 <a href="#l2308" class="line" id="l2308">   2308</a> function! s:compare_git_uri(a, b)
   2328 <a href="#l2309" class="line" id="l2309">   2309</a>   &quot; See `git help clone&#39;
   2329 <a href="#l2310" class="line" id="l2310">   2310</a>   &quot; https:// [user@] github.com[:port] / junegunn/vim-plug [.git]
   2330 <a href="#l2311" class="line" id="l2311">   2311</a>   &quot;          [git@]  github.com[:port] : junegunn/vim-plug [.git]
   2331 <a href="#l2312" class="line" id="l2312">   2312</a>   &quot; file://                            / junegunn/vim-plug        [/]
   2332 <a href="#l2313" class="line" id="l2313">   2313</a>   &quot;                                    / junegunn/vim-plug        [/]
   2333 <a href="#l2314" class="line" id="l2314">   2314</a>   let pat = &#39;^\%(\w\+://\)\=&#39;.&#39;\%([^@/]*@\)\=&#39;.&#39;\([^:/]*\%(:[0-9]*\)\=\)&#39;.&#39;[:/]&#39;.&#39;\(.\{-}\)&#39;.&#39;\%(\.git\)\=/\?$&#39;
   2334 <a href="#l2315" class="line" id="l2315">   2315</a>   let ma = matchlist(a:a, pat)
   2335 <a href="#l2316" class="line" id="l2316">   2316</a>   let mb = matchlist(a:b, pat)
   2336 <a href="#l2317" class="line" id="l2317">   2317</a>   return ma[1:2] ==# mb[1:2]
   2337 <a href="#l2318" class="line" id="l2318">   2318</a> endfunction
   2338 <a href="#l2319" class="line" id="l2319">   2319</a> 
   2339 <a href="#l2320" class="line" id="l2320">   2320</a> function! s:format_message(bullet, name, message)
   2340 <a href="#l2321" class="line" id="l2321">   2321</a>   if a:bullet != &#39;x&#39;
   2341 <a href="#l2322" class="line" id="l2322">   2322</a>     return [printf(&#39;%s %s: %s&#39;, a:bullet, a:name, s:lastline(a:message))]
   2342 <a href="#l2323" class="line" id="l2323">   2323</a>   else
   2343 <a href="#l2324" class="line" id="l2324">   2324</a>     let lines = map(s:lines(a:message), &#39;&quot;    &quot;.v:val&#39;)
   2344 <a href="#l2325" class="line" id="l2325">   2325</a>     return extend([printf(&#39;x %s:&#39;, a:name)], lines)
   2345 <a href="#l2326" class="line" id="l2326">   2326</a>   endif
   2346 <a href="#l2327" class="line" id="l2327">   2327</a> endfunction
   2347 <a href="#l2328" class="line" id="l2328">   2328</a> 
   2348 <a href="#l2329" class="line" id="l2329">   2329</a> function! s:with_cd(cmd, dir, ...)
   2349 <a href="#l2330" class="line" id="l2330">   2330</a>   let script = a:0 &gt; 0 ? a:1 : 1
   2350 <a href="#l2331" class="line" id="l2331">   2331</a>   let pwsh = s:is_powershell(&amp;shell)
   2351 <a href="#l2332" class="line" id="l2332">   2332</a>   let cd = s:is_win &amp;&amp; !pwsh ? &#39;cd /d&#39; : &#39;cd&#39;
   2352 <a href="#l2333" class="line" id="l2333">   2333</a>   let sep = pwsh ? &#39;;&#39; : &#39;&amp;&amp;&#39;
   2353 <a href="#l2334" class="line" id="l2334">   2334</a>   return printf(&#39;%s %s %s %s&#39;, cd, plug#shellescape(a:dir, {&#39;script&#39;: script, &#39;shell&#39;: &amp;shell}), sep, a:cmd)
   2354 <a href="#l2335" class="line" id="l2335">   2335</a> endfunction
   2355 <a href="#l2336" class="line" id="l2336">   2336</a> 
   2356 <a href="#l2337" class="line" id="l2337">   2337</a> function! s:system(cmd, ...)
   2357 <a href="#l2338" class="line" id="l2338">   2338</a>   let batchfile = &#39;&#39;
   2358 <a href="#l2339" class="line" id="l2339">   2339</a>   try
   2359 <a href="#l2340" class="line" id="l2340">   2340</a>     let [sh, shellcmdflag, shrd] = s:chsh(1)
   2360 <a href="#l2341" class="line" id="l2341">   2341</a>     if type(a:cmd) == s:TYPE.list
   2361 <a href="#l2342" class="line" id="l2342">   2342</a>       &quot; Neovim&#39;s system() supports list argument to bypass the shell
   2362 <a href="#l2343" class="line" id="l2343">   2343</a>       &quot; but it cannot set the working directory for the command.
   2363 <a href="#l2344" class="line" id="l2344">   2344</a>       &quot; Assume that the command does not rely on the shell.
   2364 <a href="#l2345" class="line" id="l2345">   2345</a>       if has(&#39;nvim&#39;) &amp;&amp; a:0 == 0
   2365 <a href="#l2346" class="line" id="l2346">   2346</a>         return system(a:cmd)
   2366 <a href="#l2347" class="line" id="l2347">   2347</a>       endif
   2367 <a href="#l2348" class="line" id="l2348">   2348</a>       let cmd = join(map(copy(a:cmd), &#39;plug#shellescape(v:val, {&quot;shell&quot;: &amp;shell, &quot;script&quot;: 0})&#39;))
   2368 <a href="#l2349" class="line" id="l2349">   2349</a>       if s:is_powershell(&amp;shell)
   2369 <a href="#l2350" class="line" id="l2350">   2350</a>         let cmd = &#39;&amp; &#39; . cmd
   2370 <a href="#l2351" class="line" id="l2351">   2351</a>       endif
   2371 <a href="#l2352" class="line" id="l2352">   2352</a>     else
   2372 <a href="#l2353" class="line" id="l2353">   2353</a>       let cmd = a:cmd
   2373 <a href="#l2354" class="line" id="l2354">   2354</a>     endif
   2374 <a href="#l2355" class="line" id="l2355">   2355</a>     if a:0 &gt; 0
   2375 <a href="#l2356" class="line" id="l2356">   2356</a>       let cmd = s:with_cd(cmd, a:1, type(a:cmd) != s:TYPE.list)
   2376 <a href="#l2357" class="line" id="l2357">   2357</a>     endif
   2377 <a href="#l2358" class="line" id="l2358">   2358</a>     if s:is_win &amp;&amp; type(a:cmd) != s:TYPE.list
   2378 <a href="#l2359" class="line" id="l2359">   2359</a>       let [batchfile, cmd] = s:batchfile(cmd)
   2379 <a href="#l2360" class="line" id="l2360">   2360</a>     endif
   2380 <a href="#l2361" class="line" id="l2361">   2361</a>     return system(cmd)
   2381 <a href="#l2362" class="line" id="l2362">   2362</a>   finally
   2382 <a href="#l2363" class="line" id="l2363">   2363</a>     let [&amp;shell, &amp;shellcmdflag, &amp;shellredir] = [sh, shellcmdflag, shrd]
   2383 <a href="#l2364" class="line" id="l2364">   2364</a>     if s:is_win &amp;&amp; filereadable(batchfile)
   2384 <a href="#l2365" class="line" id="l2365">   2365</a>       call delete(batchfile)
   2385 <a href="#l2366" class="line" id="l2366">   2366</a>     endif
   2386 <a href="#l2367" class="line" id="l2367">   2367</a>   endtry
   2387 <a href="#l2368" class="line" id="l2368">   2368</a> endfunction
   2388 <a href="#l2369" class="line" id="l2369">   2369</a> 
   2389 <a href="#l2370" class="line" id="l2370">   2370</a> function! s:system_chomp(...)
   2390 <a href="#l2371" class="line" id="l2371">   2371</a>   let ret = call(&#39;s:system&#39;, a:000)
   2391 <a href="#l2372" class="line" id="l2372">   2372</a>   return v:shell_error ? &#39;&#39; : substitute(ret, &#39;\n$&#39;, &#39;&#39;, &#39;&#39;)
   2392 <a href="#l2373" class="line" id="l2373">   2373</a> endfunction
   2393 <a href="#l2374" class="line" id="l2374">   2374</a> 
   2394 <a href="#l2375" class="line" id="l2375">   2375</a> function! s:git_validate(spec, check_branch)
   2395 <a href="#l2376" class="line" id="l2376">   2376</a>   let err = &#39;&#39;
   2396 <a href="#l2377" class="line" id="l2377">   2377</a>   if isdirectory(a:spec.dir)
   2397 <a href="#l2378" class="line" id="l2378">   2378</a>     let result = [s:git_local_branch(a:spec.dir), s:git_origin_url(a:spec.dir)]
   2398 <a href="#l2379" class="line" id="l2379">   2379</a>     let remote = result[-1]
   2399 <a href="#l2380" class="line" id="l2380">   2380</a>     if empty(remote)
   2400 <a href="#l2381" class="line" id="l2381">   2381</a>       let err = join([remote, &#39;PlugClean required.&#39;], &quot;\n&quot;)
   2401 <a href="#l2382" class="line" id="l2382">   2382</a>     elseif !s:compare_git_uri(remote, a:spec.uri)
   2402 <a href="#l2383" class="line" id="l2383">   2383</a>       let err = join([&#39;Invalid URI: &#39;.remote,
   2403 <a href="#l2384" class="line" id="l2384">   2384</a>                     \ &#39;Expected:    &#39;.a:spec.uri,
   2404 <a href="#l2385" class="line" id="l2385">   2385</a>                     \ &#39;PlugClean required.&#39;], &quot;\n&quot;)
   2405 <a href="#l2386" class="line" id="l2386">   2386</a>     elseif a:check_branch &amp;&amp; has_key(a:spec, &#39;commit&#39;)
   2406 <a href="#l2387" class="line" id="l2387">   2387</a>       let sha = s:git_revision(a:spec.dir)
   2407 <a href="#l2388" class="line" id="l2388">   2388</a>       if empty(sha)
   2408 <a href="#l2389" class="line" id="l2389">   2389</a>         let err = join(add(result, &#39;PlugClean required.&#39;), &quot;\n&quot;)
   2409 <a href="#l2390" class="line" id="l2390">   2390</a>       elseif !s:hash_match(sha, a:spec.commit)
   2410 <a href="#l2391" class="line" id="l2391">   2391</a>         let err = join([printf(&#39;Invalid HEAD (expected: %s, actual: %s)&#39;,
   2411 <a href="#l2392" class="line" id="l2392">   2392</a>                               \ a:spec.commit[:6], sha[:6]),
   2412 <a href="#l2393" class="line" id="l2393">   2393</a>                       \ &#39;PlugUpdate required.&#39;], &quot;\n&quot;)
   2413 <a href="#l2394" class="line" id="l2394">   2394</a>       endif
   2414 <a href="#l2395" class="line" id="l2395">   2395</a>     elseif a:check_branch
   2415 <a href="#l2396" class="line" id="l2396">   2396</a>       let current_branch = result[0]
   2416 <a href="#l2397" class="line" id="l2397">   2397</a>       &quot; Check tag
   2417 <a href="#l2398" class="line" id="l2398">   2398</a>       let origin_branch = s:git_origin_branch(a:spec)
   2418 <a href="#l2399" class="line" id="l2399">   2399</a>       if has_key(a:spec, &#39;tag&#39;)
   2419 <a href="#l2400" class="line" id="l2400">   2400</a>         let tag = s:system_chomp(&#39;git describe --exact-match --tags HEAD 2&gt;&amp;1&#39;, a:spec.dir)
   2420 <a href="#l2401" class="line" id="l2401">   2401</a>         if a:spec.tag !=# tag &amp;&amp; a:spec.tag !~ &#39;\*&#39;
   2421 <a href="#l2402" class="line" id="l2402">   2402</a>           let err = printf(&#39;Invalid tag: %s (expected: %s). Try PlugUpdate.&#39;,
   2422 <a href="#l2403" class="line" id="l2403">   2403</a>                 \ (empty(tag) ? &#39;N/A&#39; : tag), a:spec.tag)
   2423 <a href="#l2404" class="line" id="l2404">   2404</a>         endif
   2424 <a href="#l2405" class="line" id="l2405">   2405</a>       &quot; Check branch
   2425 <a href="#l2406" class="line" id="l2406">   2406</a>       elseif origin_branch !=# current_branch
   2426 <a href="#l2407" class="line" id="l2407">   2407</a>         let err = printf(&#39;Invalid branch: %s (expected: %s). Try PlugUpdate.&#39;,
   2427 <a href="#l2408" class="line" id="l2408">   2408</a>               \ current_branch, origin_branch)
   2428 <a href="#l2409" class="line" id="l2409">   2409</a>       endif
   2429 <a href="#l2410" class="line" id="l2410">   2410</a>       if empty(err)
   2430 <a href="#l2411" class="line" id="l2411">   2411</a>         let ahead_behind = split(s:lastline(s:system([
   2431 <a href="#l2412" class="line" id="l2412">   2412</a>           \ &#39;git&#39;, &#39;rev-list&#39;, &#39;--count&#39;, &#39;--left-right&#39;,
   2432 <a href="#l2413" class="line" id="l2413">   2413</a>           \ printf(&#39;HEAD...origin/%s&#39;, origin_branch)
   2433 <a href="#l2414" class="line" id="l2414">   2414</a>           \ ], a:spec.dir)), &#39;\t&#39;)
   2434 <a href="#l2415" class="line" id="l2415">   2415</a>         if v:shell_error || len(ahead_behind) != 2
   2435 <a href="#l2416" class="line" id="l2416">   2416</a>           let err = &quot;Failed to compare with the origin. The default branch might have changed.\nPlugClean required.&quot;
   2436 <a href="#l2417" class="line" id="l2417">   2417</a>         else
   2437 <a href="#l2418" class="line" id="l2418">   2418</a>           let [ahead, behind] = ahead_behind
   2438 <a href="#l2419" class="line" id="l2419">   2419</a>           if ahead &amp;&amp; behind
   2439 <a href="#l2420" class="line" id="l2420">   2420</a>             &quot; Only mention PlugClean if diverged, otherwise it&#39;s likely to be
   2440 <a href="#l2421" class="line" id="l2421">   2421</a>             &quot; pushable (and probably not that messed up).
   2441 <a href="#l2422" class="line" id="l2422">   2422</a>             let err = printf(
   2442 <a href="#l2423" class="line" id="l2423">   2423</a>                   \ &quot;Diverged from origin/%s (%d commit(s) ahead and %d commit(s) behind!\n&quot;
   2443 <a href="#l2424" class="line" id="l2424">   2424</a>                   \ .&#39;Backup local changes and run PlugClean and PlugUpdate to reinstall it.&#39;, origin_branch, ahead, behind)
   2444 <a href="#l2425" class="line" id="l2425">   2425</a>           elseif ahead
   2445 <a href="#l2426" class="line" id="l2426">   2426</a>             let err = printf(&quot;Ahead of origin/%s by %d commit(s).\n&quot;
   2446 <a href="#l2427" class="line" id="l2427">   2427</a>                   \ .&#39;Cannot update until local changes are pushed.&#39;,
   2447 <a href="#l2428" class="line" id="l2428">   2428</a>                   \ origin_branch, ahead)
   2448 <a href="#l2429" class="line" id="l2429">   2429</a>           endif
   2449 <a href="#l2430" class="line" id="l2430">   2430</a>         endif
   2450 <a href="#l2431" class="line" id="l2431">   2431</a>       endif
   2451 <a href="#l2432" class="line" id="l2432">   2432</a>     endif
   2452 <a href="#l2433" class="line" id="l2433">   2433</a>   else
   2453 <a href="#l2434" class="line" id="l2434">   2434</a>     let err = &#39;Not found&#39;
   2454 <a href="#l2435" class="line" id="l2435">   2435</a>   endif
   2455 <a href="#l2436" class="line" id="l2436">   2436</a>   return [err, err =~# &#39;PlugClean&#39;]
   2456 <a href="#l2437" class="line" id="l2437">   2437</a> endfunction
   2457 <a href="#l2438" class="line" id="l2438">   2438</a> 
   2458 <a href="#l2439" class="line" id="l2439">   2439</a> function! s:rm_rf(dir)
   2459 <a href="#l2440" class="line" id="l2440">   2440</a>   if isdirectory(a:dir)
   2460 <a href="#l2441" class="line" id="l2441">   2441</a>     return s:system(s:is_win
   2461 <a href="#l2442" class="line" id="l2442">   2442</a>     \ ? &#39;rmdir /S /Q &#39;.plug#shellescape(a:dir)
   2462 <a href="#l2443" class="line" id="l2443">   2443</a>     \ : [&#39;rm&#39;, &#39;-rf&#39;, a:dir])
   2463 <a href="#l2444" class="line" id="l2444">   2444</a>   endif
   2464 <a href="#l2445" class="line" id="l2445">   2445</a> endfunction
   2465 <a href="#l2446" class="line" id="l2446">   2446</a> 
   2466 <a href="#l2447" class="line" id="l2447">   2447</a> function! s:clean(force)
   2467 <a href="#l2448" class="line" id="l2448">   2448</a>   call s:prepare()
   2468 <a href="#l2449" class="line" id="l2449">   2449</a>   call append(0, &#39;Searching for invalid plugins in &#39;.g:plug_home)
   2469 <a href="#l2450" class="line" id="l2450">   2450</a>   call append(1, &#39;&#39;)
   2470 <a href="#l2451" class="line" id="l2451">   2451</a> 
   2471 <a href="#l2452" class="line" id="l2452">   2452</a>   &quot; List of valid directories
   2472 <a href="#l2453" class="line" id="l2453">   2453</a>   let dirs = []
   2473 <a href="#l2454" class="line" id="l2454">   2454</a>   let errs = {}
   2474 <a href="#l2455" class="line" id="l2455">   2455</a>   let [cnt, total] = [0, len(g:plugs)]
   2475 <a href="#l2456" class="line" id="l2456">   2456</a>   for [name, spec] in items(g:plugs)
   2476 <a href="#l2457" class="line" id="l2457">   2457</a>     if !s:is_managed(name) || get(spec, &#39;frozen&#39;, 0)
   2477 <a href="#l2458" class="line" id="l2458">   2458</a>       call add(dirs, spec.dir)
   2478 <a href="#l2459" class="line" id="l2459">   2459</a>     else
   2479 <a href="#l2460" class="line" id="l2460">   2460</a>       let [err, clean] = s:git_validate(spec, 1)
   2480 <a href="#l2461" class="line" id="l2461">   2461</a>       if clean
   2481 <a href="#l2462" class="line" id="l2462">   2462</a>         let errs[spec.dir] = s:lines(err)[0]
   2482 <a href="#l2463" class="line" id="l2463">   2463</a>       else
   2483 <a href="#l2464" class="line" id="l2464">   2464</a>         call add(dirs, spec.dir)
   2484 <a href="#l2465" class="line" id="l2465">   2465</a>       endif
   2485 <a href="#l2466" class="line" id="l2466">   2466</a>     endif
   2486 <a href="#l2467" class="line" id="l2467">   2467</a>     let cnt += 1
   2487 <a href="#l2468" class="line" id="l2468">   2468</a>     call s:progress_bar(2, repeat(&#39;=&#39;, cnt), total)
   2488 <a href="#l2469" class="line" id="l2469">   2469</a>     normal! 2G
   2489 <a href="#l2470" class="line" id="l2470">   2470</a>     redraw
   2490 <a href="#l2471" class="line" id="l2471">   2471</a>   endfor
   2491 <a href="#l2472" class="line" id="l2472">   2472</a> 
   2492 <a href="#l2473" class="line" id="l2473">   2473</a>   let allowed = {}
   2493 <a href="#l2474" class="line" id="l2474">   2474</a>   for dir in dirs
   2494 <a href="#l2475" class="line" id="l2475">   2475</a>     let allowed[s:dirpath(s:plug_fnamemodify(dir, &#39;:h:h&#39;))] = 1
   2495 <a href="#l2476" class="line" id="l2476">   2476</a>     let allowed[dir] = 1
   2496 <a href="#l2477" class="line" id="l2477">   2477</a>     for child in s:glob_dir(dir)
   2497 <a href="#l2478" class="line" id="l2478">   2478</a>       let allowed[child] = 1
   2498 <a href="#l2479" class="line" id="l2479">   2479</a>     endfor
   2499 <a href="#l2480" class="line" id="l2480">   2480</a>   endfor
   2500 <a href="#l2481" class="line" id="l2481">   2481</a> 
   2501 <a href="#l2482" class="line" id="l2482">   2482</a>   let todo = []
   2502 <a href="#l2483" class="line" id="l2483">   2483</a>   let found = sort(s:glob_dir(g:plug_home))
   2503 <a href="#l2484" class="line" id="l2484">   2484</a>   while !empty(found)
   2504 <a href="#l2485" class="line" id="l2485">   2485</a>     let f = remove(found, 0)
   2505 <a href="#l2486" class="line" id="l2486">   2486</a>     if !has_key(allowed, f) &amp;&amp; isdirectory(f)
   2506 <a href="#l2487" class="line" id="l2487">   2487</a>       call add(todo, f)
   2507 <a href="#l2488" class="line" id="l2488">   2488</a>       call append(line(&#39;$&#39;), &#39;- &#39; . f)
   2508 <a href="#l2489" class="line" id="l2489">   2489</a>       if has_key(errs, f)
   2509 <a href="#l2490" class="line" id="l2490">   2490</a>         call append(line(&#39;$&#39;), &#39;    &#39; . errs[f])
   2510 <a href="#l2491" class="line" id="l2491">   2491</a>       endif
   2511 <a href="#l2492" class="line" id="l2492">   2492</a>       let found = filter(found, &#39;stridx(v:val, f) != 0&#39;)
   2512 <a href="#l2493" class="line" id="l2493">   2493</a>     end
   2513 <a href="#l2494" class="line" id="l2494">   2494</a>   endwhile
   2514 <a href="#l2495" class="line" id="l2495">   2495</a> 
   2515 <a href="#l2496" class="line" id="l2496">   2496</a>   4
   2516 <a href="#l2497" class="line" id="l2497">   2497</a>   redraw
   2517 <a href="#l2498" class="line" id="l2498">   2498</a>   if empty(todo)
   2518 <a href="#l2499" class="line" id="l2499">   2499</a>     call append(line(&#39;$&#39;), &#39;Already clean.&#39;)
   2519 <a href="#l2500" class="line" id="l2500">   2500</a>   else
   2520 <a href="#l2501" class="line" id="l2501">   2501</a>     let s:clean_count = 0
   2521 <a href="#l2502" class="line" id="l2502">   2502</a>     call append(3, [&#39;Directories to delete:&#39;, &#39;&#39;])
   2522 <a href="#l2503" class="line" id="l2503">   2503</a>     redraw!
   2523 <a href="#l2504" class="line" id="l2504">   2504</a>     if a:force || s:ask_no_interrupt(&#39;Delete all directories?&#39;)
   2524 <a href="#l2505" class="line" id="l2505">   2505</a>       call s:delete([6, line(&#39;$&#39;)], 1)
   2525 <a href="#l2506" class="line" id="l2506">   2506</a>     else
   2526 <a href="#l2507" class="line" id="l2507">   2507</a>       call setline(4, &#39;Cancelled.&#39;)
   2527 <a href="#l2508" class="line" id="l2508">   2508</a>       nnoremap &lt;silent&gt; &lt;buffer&gt; d :set opfunc=&lt;sid&gt;delete_op&lt;cr&gt;g@
   2528 <a href="#l2509" class="line" id="l2509">   2509</a>       nmap     &lt;silent&gt; &lt;buffer&gt; dd d_
   2529 <a href="#l2510" class="line" id="l2510">   2510</a>       xnoremap &lt;silent&gt; &lt;buffer&gt; d :&lt;c-u&gt;call &lt;sid&gt;delete_op(visualmode(), 1)&lt;cr&gt;
   2530 <a href="#l2511" class="line" id="l2511">   2511</a>       echo &#39;Delete the lines (d{motion}) to delete the corresponding directories&#39;
   2531 <a href="#l2512" class="line" id="l2512">   2512</a>     endif
   2532 <a href="#l2513" class="line" id="l2513">   2513</a>   endif
   2533 <a href="#l2514" class="line" id="l2514">   2514</a>   4
   2534 <a href="#l2515" class="line" id="l2515">   2515</a>   setlocal nomodifiable
   2535 <a href="#l2516" class="line" id="l2516">   2516</a> endfunction
   2536 <a href="#l2517" class="line" id="l2517">   2517</a> 
   2537 <a href="#l2518" class="line" id="l2518">   2518</a> function! s:delete_op(type, ...)
   2538 <a href="#l2519" class="line" id="l2519">   2519</a>   call s:delete(a:0 ? [line(&quot;&#39;&lt;&quot;), line(&quot;&#39;&gt;&quot;)] : [line(&quot;&#39;[&quot;), line(&quot;&#39;]&quot;)], 0)
   2539 <a href="#l2520" class="line" id="l2520">   2520</a> endfunction
   2540 <a href="#l2521" class="line" id="l2521">   2521</a> 
   2541 <a href="#l2522" class="line" id="l2522">   2522</a> function! s:delete(range, force)
   2542 <a href="#l2523" class="line" id="l2523">   2523</a>   let [l1, l2] = a:range
   2543 <a href="#l2524" class="line" id="l2524">   2524</a>   let force = a:force
   2544 <a href="#l2525" class="line" id="l2525">   2525</a>   let err_count = 0
   2545 <a href="#l2526" class="line" id="l2526">   2526</a>   while l1 &lt;= l2
   2546 <a href="#l2527" class="line" id="l2527">   2527</a>     let line = getline(l1)
   2547 <a href="#l2528" class="line" id="l2528">   2528</a>     if line =~ &#39;^- &#39; &amp;&amp; isdirectory(line[2:])
   2548 <a href="#l2529" class="line" id="l2529">   2529</a>       execute l1
   2549 <a href="#l2530" class="line" id="l2530">   2530</a>       redraw!
   2550 <a href="#l2531" class="line" id="l2531">   2531</a>       let answer = force ? 1 : s:ask(&#39;Delete &#39;.line[2:].&#39;?&#39;, 1)
   2551 <a href="#l2532" class="line" id="l2532">   2532</a>       let force = force || answer &gt; 1
   2552 <a href="#l2533" class="line" id="l2533">   2533</a>       if answer
   2553 <a href="#l2534" class="line" id="l2534">   2534</a>         let err = s:rm_rf(line[2:])
   2554 <a href="#l2535" class="line" id="l2535">   2535</a>         setlocal modifiable
   2555 <a href="#l2536" class="line" id="l2536">   2536</a>         if empty(err)
   2556 <a href="#l2537" class="line" id="l2537">   2537</a>           call setline(l1, &#39;~&#39;.line[1:])
   2557 <a href="#l2538" class="line" id="l2538">   2538</a>           let s:clean_count += 1
   2558 <a href="#l2539" class="line" id="l2539">   2539</a>         else
   2559 <a href="#l2540" class="line" id="l2540">   2540</a>           delete _
   2560 <a href="#l2541" class="line" id="l2541">   2541</a>           call append(l1 - 1, s:format_message(&#39;x&#39;, line[1:], err))
   2561 <a href="#l2542" class="line" id="l2542">   2542</a>           let l2 += len(s:lines(err))
   2562 <a href="#l2543" class="line" id="l2543">   2543</a>           let err_count += 1
   2563 <a href="#l2544" class="line" id="l2544">   2544</a>         endif
   2564 <a href="#l2545" class="line" id="l2545">   2545</a>         let msg = printf(&#39;Removed %d directories.&#39;, s:clean_count)
   2565 <a href="#l2546" class="line" id="l2546">   2546</a>         if err_count &gt; 0
   2566 <a href="#l2547" class="line" id="l2547">   2547</a>           let msg .= printf(&#39; Failed to remove %d directories.&#39;, err_count)
   2567 <a href="#l2548" class="line" id="l2548">   2548</a>         endif
   2568 <a href="#l2549" class="line" id="l2549">   2549</a>         call setline(4, msg)
   2569 <a href="#l2550" class="line" id="l2550">   2550</a>         setlocal nomodifiable
   2570 <a href="#l2551" class="line" id="l2551">   2551</a>       endif
   2571 <a href="#l2552" class="line" id="l2552">   2552</a>     endif
   2572 <a href="#l2553" class="line" id="l2553">   2553</a>     let l1 += 1
   2573 <a href="#l2554" class="line" id="l2554">   2554</a>   endwhile
   2574 <a href="#l2555" class="line" id="l2555">   2555</a> endfunction
   2575 <a href="#l2556" class="line" id="l2556">   2556</a> 
   2576 <a href="#l2557" class="line" id="l2557">   2557</a> function! s:upgrade()
   2577 <a href="#l2558" class="line" id="l2558">   2558</a>   echo &#39;Downloading the latest version of vim-plug&#39;
   2578 <a href="#l2559" class="line" id="l2559">   2559</a>   redraw
   2579 <a href="#l2560" class="line" id="l2560">   2560</a>   let tmp = s:plug_tempname()
   2580 <a href="#l2561" class="line" id="l2561">   2561</a>   let new = tmp . &#39;/plug.vim&#39;
   2581 <a href="#l2562" class="line" id="l2562">   2562</a> 
   2582 <a href="#l2563" class="line" id="l2563">   2563</a>   try
   2583 <a href="#l2564" class="line" id="l2564">   2564</a>     let out = s:system([&#39;git&#39;, &#39;clone&#39;, &#39;--depth&#39;, &#39;1&#39;, s:plug_src, tmp])
   2584 <a href="#l2565" class="line" id="l2565">   2565</a>     if v:shell_error
   2585 <a href="#l2566" class="line" id="l2566">   2566</a>       return s:err(&#39;Error upgrading vim-plug: &#39;. out)
   2586 <a href="#l2567" class="line" id="l2567">   2567</a>     endif
   2587 <a href="#l2568" class="line" id="l2568">   2568</a> 
   2588 <a href="#l2569" class="line" id="l2569">   2569</a>     if readfile(s:me) ==# readfile(new)
   2589 <a href="#l2570" class="line" id="l2570">   2570</a>       echo &#39;vim-plug is already up-to-date&#39;
   2590 <a href="#l2571" class="line" id="l2571">   2571</a>       return 0
   2591 <a href="#l2572" class="line" id="l2572">   2572</a>     else
   2592 <a href="#l2573" class="line" id="l2573">   2573</a>       call rename(s:me, s:me . &#39;.old&#39;)
   2593 <a href="#l2574" class="line" id="l2574">   2574</a>       call rename(new, s:me)
   2594 <a href="#l2575" class="line" id="l2575">   2575</a>       unlet g:loaded_plug
   2595 <a href="#l2576" class="line" id="l2576">   2576</a>       echo &#39;vim-plug has been upgraded&#39;
   2596 <a href="#l2577" class="line" id="l2577">   2577</a>       return 1
   2597 <a href="#l2578" class="line" id="l2578">   2578</a>     endif
   2598 <a href="#l2579" class="line" id="l2579">   2579</a>   finally
   2599 <a href="#l2580" class="line" id="l2580">   2580</a>     silent! call s:rm_rf(tmp)
   2600 <a href="#l2581" class="line" id="l2581">   2581</a>   endtry
   2601 <a href="#l2582" class="line" id="l2582">   2582</a> endfunction
   2602 <a href="#l2583" class="line" id="l2583">   2583</a> 
   2603 <a href="#l2584" class="line" id="l2584">   2584</a> function! s:upgrade_specs()
   2604 <a href="#l2585" class="line" id="l2585">   2585</a>   for spec in values(g:plugs)
   2605 <a href="#l2586" class="line" id="l2586">   2586</a>     let spec.frozen = get(spec, &#39;frozen&#39;, 0)
   2606 <a href="#l2587" class="line" id="l2587">   2587</a>   endfor
   2607 <a href="#l2588" class="line" id="l2588">   2588</a> endfunction
   2608 <a href="#l2589" class="line" id="l2589">   2589</a> 
   2609 <a href="#l2590" class="line" id="l2590">   2590</a> function! s:status()
   2610 <a href="#l2591" class="line" id="l2591">   2591</a>   call s:prepare()
   2611 <a href="#l2592" class="line" id="l2592">   2592</a>   call append(0, &#39;Checking plugins&#39;)
   2612 <a href="#l2593" class="line" id="l2593">   2593</a>   call append(1, &#39;&#39;)
   2613 <a href="#l2594" class="line" id="l2594">   2594</a> 
   2614 <a href="#l2595" class="line" id="l2595">   2595</a>   let ecnt = 0
   2615 <a href="#l2596" class="line" id="l2596">   2596</a>   let unloaded = 0
   2616 <a href="#l2597" class="line" id="l2597">   2597</a>   let [cnt, total] = [0, len(g:plugs)]
   2617 <a href="#l2598" class="line" id="l2598">   2598</a>   for [name, spec] in items(g:plugs)
   2618 <a href="#l2599" class="line" id="l2599">   2599</a>     let is_dir = isdirectory(spec.dir)
   2619 <a href="#l2600" class="line" id="l2600">   2600</a>     if has_key(spec, &#39;uri&#39;)
   2620 <a href="#l2601" class="line" id="l2601">   2601</a>       if is_dir
   2621 <a href="#l2602" class="line" id="l2602">   2602</a>         let [err, _] = s:git_validate(spec, 1)
   2622 <a href="#l2603" class="line" id="l2603">   2603</a>         let [valid, msg] = [empty(err), empty(err) ? &#39;OK&#39; : err]
   2623 <a href="#l2604" class="line" id="l2604">   2604</a>       else
   2624 <a href="#l2605" class="line" id="l2605">   2605</a>         let [valid, msg] = [0, &#39;Not found. Try PlugInstall.&#39;]
   2625 <a href="#l2606" class="line" id="l2606">   2606</a>       endif
   2626 <a href="#l2607" class="line" id="l2607">   2607</a>     else
   2627 <a href="#l2608" class="line" id="l2608">   2608</a>       if is_dir
   2628 <a href="#l2609" class="line" id="l2609">   2609</a>         let [valid, msg] = [1, &#39;OK&#39;]
   2629 <a href="#l2610" class="line" id="l2610">   2610</a>       else
   2630 <a href="#l2611" class="line" id="l2611">   2611</a>         let [valid, msg] = [0, &#39;Not found.&#39;]
   2631 <a href="#l2612" class="line" id="l2612">   2612</a>       endif
   2632 <a href="#l2613" class="line" id="l2613">   2613</a>     endif
   2633 <a href="#l2614" class="line" id="l2614">   2614</a>     let cnt += 1
   2634 <a href="#l2615" class="line" id="l2615">   2615</a>     let ecnt += !valid
   2635 <a href="#l2616" class="line" id="l2616">   2616</a>     &quot; `s:loaded` entry can be missing if PlugUpgraded
   2636 <a href="#l2617" class="line" id="l2617">   2617</a>     if is_dir &amp;&amp; get(s:loaded, name, -1) == 0
   2637 <a href="#l2618" class="line" id="l2618">   2618</a>       let unloaded = 1
   2638 <a href="#l2619" class="line" id="l2619">   2619</a>       let msg .= &#39; (not loaded)&#39;
   2639 <a href="#l2620" class="line" id="l2620">   2620</a>     endif
   2640 <a href="#l2621" class="line" id="l2621">   2621</a>     call s:progress_bar(2, repeat(&#39;=&#39;, cnt), total)
   2641 <a href="#l2622" class="line" id="l2622">   2622</a>     call append(3, s:format_message(valid ? &#39;-&#39; : &#39;x&#39;, name, msg))
   2642 <a href="#l2623" class="line" id="l2623">   2623</a>     normal! 2G
   2643 <a href="#l2624" class="line" id="l2624">   2624</a>     redraw
   2644 <a href="#l2625" class="line" id="l2625">   2625</a>   endfor
   2645 <a href="#l2626" class="line" id="l2626">   2626</a>   call setline(1, &#39;Finished. &#39;.ecnt.&#39; error(s).&#39;)
   2646 <a href="#l2627" class="line" id="l2627">   2627</a>   normal! gg
   2647 <a href="#l2628" class="line" id="l2628">   2628</a>   setlocal nomodifiable
   2648 <a href="#l2629" class="line" id="l2629">   2629</a>   if unloaded
   2649 <a href="#l2630" class="line" id="l2630">   2630</a>     echo &quot;Press &#39;L&#39; on each line to load plugin, or &#39;U&#39; to update&quot;
   2650 <a href="#l2631" class="line" id="l2631">   2631</a>     nnoremap &lt;silent&gt; &lt;buffer&gt; L :call &lt;SID&gt;status_load(line(&#39;.&#39;))&lt;cr&gt;
   2651 <a href="#l2632" class="line" id="l2632">   2632</a>     xnoremap &lt;silent&gt; &lt;buffer&gt; L :call &lt;SID&gt;status_load(line(&#39;.&#39;))&lt;cr&gt;
   2652 <a href="#l2633" class="line" id="l2633">   2633</a>   end
   2653 <a href="#l2634" class="line" id="l2634">   2634</a> endfunction
   2654 <a href="#l2635" class="line" id="l2635">   2635</a> 
   2655 <a href="#l2636" class="line" id="l2636">   2636</a> function! s:extract_name(str, prefix, suffix)
   2656 <a href="#l2637" class="line" id="l2637">   2637</a>   return matchstr(a:str, &#39;^&#39;.a:prefix.&#39; \zs[^:]\+\ze:.*&#39;.a:suffix.&#39;$&#39;)
   2657 <a href="#l2638" class="line" id="l2638">   2638</a> endfunction
   2658 <a href="#l2639" class="line" id="l2639">   2639</a> 
   2659 <a href="#l2640" class="line" id="l2640">   2640</a> function! s:status_load(lnum)
   2660 <a href="#l2641" class="line" id="l2641">   2641</a>   let line = getline(a:lnum)
   2661 <a href="#l2642" class="line" id="l2642">   2642</a>   let name = s:extract_name(line, &#39;-&#39;, &#39;(not loaded)&#39;)
   2662 <a href="#l2643" class="line" id="l2643">   2643</a>   if !empty(name)
   2663 <a href="#l2644" class="line" id="l2644">   2644</a>     call plug#load(name)
   2664 <a href="#l2645" class="line" id="l2645">   2645</a>     setlocal modifiable
   2665 <a href="#l2646" class="line" id="l2646">   2646</a>     call setline(a:lnum, substitute(line, &#39; (not loaded)$&#39;, &#39;&#39;, &#39;&#39;))
   2666 <a href="#l2647" class="line" id="l2647">   2647</a>     setlocal nomodifiable
   2667 <a href="#l2648" class="line" id="l2648">   2648</a>   endif
   2668 <a href="#l2649" class="line" id="l2649">   2649</a> endfunction

   2687 <a href="#l2668" class="line" id="l2668">   2668</a> function! s:find_name(lnum)
   2688 <a href="#l2669" class="line" id="l2669">   2669</a>   for lnum in reverse(range(1, a:lnum))
   2689 <a href="#l2670" class="line" id="l2670">   2670</a>     let line = getline(lnum)
   2690 <a href="#l2671" class="line" id="l2671">   2671</a>     if empty(line)
   2691 <a href="#l2672" class="line" id="l2672">   2672</a>       return &#39;&#39;
   2692 <a href="#l2673" class="line" id="l2673">   2673</a>     endif
   2693 <a href="#l2674" class="line" id="l2674">   2674</a>     let name = s:extract_name(line, &#39;-&#39;, &#39;&#39;)
   2694 <a href="#l2675" class="line" id="l2675">   2675</a>     if !empty(name)
   2695 <a href="#l2676" class="line" id="l2676">   2676</a>       return name
   2696 <a href="#l2677" class="line" id="l2677">   2677</a>     endif
   2697 <a href="#l2678" class="line" id="l2678">   2678</a>   endfor
   2698 <a href="#l2679" class="line" id="l2679">   2679</a>   return &#39;&#39;

   2701 <a href="#l2682" class="line" id="l2682">   2682</a> function! s:preview_commit()
   2702 <a href="#l2683" class="line" id="l2683">   2683</a>   if b:plug_preview &lt; 0
   2703 <a href="#l2684" class="line" id="l2684">   2684</a>     let b:plug_preview = !s:is_preview_window_open()
   2704 <a href="#l2685" class="line" id="l2685">   2685</a>   endif
   2705 <a href="#l2686" class="line" id="l2686">   2686</a> 
   2706 <a href="#l2687" class="line" id="l2687">   2687</a>   let sha = matchstr(getline(&#39;.&#39;), &#39;^  \X*\zs[0-9a-f]\{7,9}&#39;)
   2707 <a href="#l2688" class="line" id="l2688">   2688</a>   if empty(sha)
   2708 <a href="#l2689" class="line" id="l2689">   2689</a>     let name = matchstr(getline(&#39;.&#39;), &#39;^- \zs[^:]*\ze:$&#39;)
   2709 <a href="#l2690" class="line" id="l2690">   2690</a>     if empty(name)
   2710 <a href="#l2691" class="line" id="l2691">   2691</a>       return
   2711 <a href="#l2692" class="line" id="l2692">   2692</a>     endif
   2712 <a href="#l2693" class="line" id="l2693">   2693</a>     let title = &#39;HEAD@{1}..&#39;
   2713 <a href="#l2694" class="line" id="l2694">   2694</a>     let command = &#39;git diff --no-color HEAD@{1}&#39;
   2714 <a href="#l2695" class="line" id="l2695">   2695</a>   else
   2715 <a href="#l2696" class="line" id="l2696">   2696</a>     let title = sha
   2716 <a href="#l2697" class="line" id="l2697">   2697</a>     let command = &#39;git show --no-color --pretty=medium &#39;.sha
   2717 <a href="#l2698" class="line" id="l2698">   2698</a>     let name = s:find_name(line(&#39;.&#39;))
   2718 <a href="#l2699" class="line" id="l2699">   2699</a>   endif
   2719 <a href="#l2700" class="line" id="l2700">   2700</a> 
   2720 <a href="#l2701" class="line" id="l2701">   2701</a>   if empty(name) || !has_key(g:plugs, name) || !isdirectory(g:plugs[name].dir)
   2721 <a href="#l2702" class="line" id="l2702">   2702</a>     return
   2722 <a href="#l2703" class="line" id="l2703">   2703</a>   endif
   2723 <a href="#l2704" class="line" id="l2704">   2704</a> 
   2724 <a href="#l2705" class="line" id="l2705">   2705</a>   if !s:is_preview_window_open()
   2725 <a href="#l2706" class="line" id="l2706">   2706</a>     execute get(g:, &#39;plug_pwindow&#39;, &#39;vertical rightbelow new&#39;)
   2726 <a href="#l2707" class="line" id="l2707">   2707</a>     execute &#39;e&#39; title
   2727 <a href="#l2708" class="line" id="l2708">   2708</a>   else
   2728 <a href="#l2709" class="line" id="l2709">   2709</a>     execute &#39;pedit&#39; title
   2729 <a href="#l2710" class="line" id="l2710">   2710</a>     wincmd P
   2730 <a href="#l2711" class="line" id="l2711">   2711</a>   endif
   2731 <a href="#l2712" class="line" id="l2712">   2712</a>   setlocal previewwindow filetype=git buftype=nofile bufhidden=wipe nobuflisted modifiable
   2732 <a href="#l2713" class="line" id="l2713">   2713</a>   let batchfile = &#39;&#39;
   2733 <a href="#l2714" class="line" id="l2714">   2714</a>   try
   2734 <a href="#l2715" class="line" id="l2715">   2715</a>     let [sh, shellcmdflag, shrd] = s:chsh(1)
   2735 <a href="#l2716" class="line" id="l2716">   2716</a>     let cmd = &#39;cd &#39;.plug#shellescape(g:plugs[name].dir).&#39; &amp;&amp; &#39;.command
   2736 <a href="#l2717" class="line" id="l2717">   2717</a>     if s:is_win
   2737 <a href="#l2718" class="line" id="l2718">   2718</a>       let [batchfile, cmd] = s:batchfile(cmd)
   2738 <a href="#l2719" class="line" id="l2719">   2719</a>     endif
   2739 <a href="#l2720" class="line" id="l2720">   2720</a>     execute &#39;silent %!&#39; cmd
   2740 <a href="#l2721" class="line" id="l2721">   2721</a>   finally
   2741 <a href="#l2722" class="line" id="l2722">   2722</a>     let [&amp;shell, &amp;shellcmdflag, &amp;shellredir] = [sh, shellcmdflag, shrd]
   2742 <a href="#l2723" class="line" id="l2723">   2723</a>     if s:is_win &amp;&amp; filereadable(batchfile)
   2743 <a href="#l2724" class="line" id="l2724">   2724</a>       call delete(batchfile)
   2744 <a href="#l2725" class="line" id="l2725">   2725</a>     endif
   2745 <a href="#l2726" class="line" id="l2726">   2726</a>   endtry
   2746 <a href="#l2727" class="line" id="l2727">   2727</a>   setlocal nomodifiable
   2747 <a href="#l2728" class="line" id="l2728">   2728</a>   nnoremap &lt;silent&gt; &lt;buffer&gt; q :q&lt;cr&gt;
   2748 <a href="#l2729" class="line" id="l2729">   2729</a>   wincmd p
   2749 <a href="#l2730" class="line" id="l2730">   2730</a> endfunction

   2751 <a href="#l2732" class="line" id="l2732">   2732</a> function! s:section(flags)
   2752 <a href="#l2733" class="line" id="l2733">   2733</a>   call search(&#39;\(^[x-] \)\@&lt;=[^:]\+:&#39;, a:flags)

   2754 <a href="#l2735" class="line" id="l2735">   2735</a> 
   2755 <a href="#l2736" class="line" id="l2736">   2736</a> function! s:format_git_log(line)
   2756 <a href="#l2737" class="line" id="l2737">   2737</a>   let indent = &#39;  &#39;
   2757 <a href="#l2738" class="line" id="l2738">   2738</a>   let tokens = split(a:line, nr2char(1))
   2758 <a href="#l2739" class="line" id="l2739">   2739</a>   if len(tokens) != 5
   2759 <a href="#l2740" class="line" id="l2740">   2740</a>     return indent.substitute(a:line, &#39;\s*$&#39;, &#39;&#39;, &#39;&#39;)
   2760 <a href="#l2741" class="line" id="l2741">   2741</a>   endif
   2761 <a href="#l2742" class="line" id="l2742">   2742</a>   let [graph, sha, refs, subject, date] = tokens
   2762 <a href="#l2743" class="line" id="l2743">   2743</a>   let tag = matchstr(refs, &#39;tag: [^,)]\+&#39;)
   2763 <a href="#l2744" class="line" id="l2744">   2744</a>   let tag = empty(tag) ? &#39; &#39; : &#39; (&#39;.tag.&#39;) &#39;
   2764 <a href="#l2745" class="line" id="l2745">   2745</a>   return printf(&#39;%s%s%s%s%s (%s)&#39;, indent, graph, sha, tag, subject, date)
   2765 <a href="#l2746" class="line" id="l2746">   2746</a> endfunction
   2766 <a href="#l2747" class="line" id="l2747">   2747</a> 
   2767 <a href="#l2748" class="line" id="l2748">   2748</a> function! s:append_ul(lnum, text)
   2768 <a href="#l2749" class="line" id="l2749">   2749</a>   call append(a:lnum, [&#39;&#39;, a:text, repeat(&#39;-&#39;, len(a:text))])
   2769 <a href="#l2750" class="line" id="l2750">   2750</a> endfunction
   2770 <a href="#l2751" class="line" id="l2751">   2751</a> 
   2771 <a href="#l2752" class="line" id="l2752">   2752</a> function! s:diff()
   2772 <a href="#l2753" class="line" id="l2753">   2753</a>   call s:prepare()
   2773 <a href="#l2754" class="line" id="l2754">   2754</a>   call append(0, [&#39;Collecting changes ...&#39;, &#39;&#39;])
   2774 <a href="#l2755" class="line" id="l2755">   2755</a>   let cnts = [0, 0]
   2775 <a href="#l2756" class="line" id="l2756">   2756</a>   let bar = &#39;&#39;
   2776 <a href="#l2757" class="line" id="l2757">   2757</a>   let total = filter(copy(g:plugs), &#39;s:is_managed(v:key) &amp;&amp; isdirectory(v:val.dir)&#39;)
   2777 <a href="#l2758" class="line" id="l2758">   2758</a>   call s:progress_bar(2, bar, len(total))
   2778 <a href="#l2759" class="line" id="l2759">   2759</a>   for origin in [1, 0]
   2779 <a href="#l2760" class="line" id="l2760">   2760</a>     let plugs = reverse(sort(items(filter(copy(total), (origin ? &#39;&#39; : &#39;!&#39;).&#39;(has_key(v:val, &quot;commit&quot;) || has_key(v:val, &quot;tag&quot;))&#39;))))
   2780 <a href="#l2761" class="line" id="l2761">   2761</a>     if empty(plugs)
   2781 <a href="#l2762" class="line" id="l2762">   2762</a>       continue
   2782 <a href="#l2763" class="line" id="l2763">   2763</a>     endif
   2783 <a href="#l2764" class="line" id="l2764">   2764</a>     call s:append_ul(2, origin ? &#39;Pending updates:&#39; : &#39;Last update:&#39;)
   2784 <a href="#l2765" class="line" id="l2765">   2765</a>     for [k, v] in plugs
   2785 <a href="#l2766" class="line" id="l2766">   2766</a>       let branch = s:git_origin_branch(v)
   2786 <a href="#l2767" class="line" id="l2767">   2767</a>       if len(branch)
   2787 <a href="#l2768" class="line" id="l2768">   2768</a>         let range = origin ? &#39;..origin/&#39;.branch : &#39;HEAD@{1}..&#39;
   2788 <a href="#l2769" class="line" id="l2769">   2769</a>         let cmd = [&#39;git&#39;, &#39;log&#39;, &#39;--graph&#39;, &#39;--color=never&#39;]
   2789 <a href="#l2770" class="line" id="l2770">   2770</a>         if s:git_version_requirement(2, 10, 0)
   2790 <a href="#l2771" class="line" id="l2771">   2771</a>           call add(cmd, &#39;--no-show-signature&#39;)
   2791 <a href="#l2772" class="line" id="l2772">   2772</a>         endif
   2792 <a href="#l2773" class="line" id="l2773">   2773</a>         call extend(cmd, [&#39;--pretty=format:%x01%h%x01%d%x01%s%x01%cr&#39;, range])
   2793 <a href="#l2774" class="line" id="l2774">   2774</a>         if has_key(v, &#39;rtp&#39;)
   2794 <a href="#l2775" class="line" id="l2775">   2775</a>           call extend(cmd, [&#39;--&#39;, v.rtp])
   2795 <a href="#l2776" class="line" id="l2776">   2776</a>         endif
   2796 <a href="#l2777" class="line" id="l2777">   2777</a>         let diff = s:system_chomp(cmd, v.dir)
   2797 <a href="#l2778" class="line" id="l2778">   2778</a>         if !empty(diff)
   2798 <a href="#l2779" class="line" id="l2779">   2779</a>           let ref = has_key(v, &#39;tag&#39;) ? (&#39; (tag: &#39;.v.tag.&#39;)&#39;) : has_key(v, &#39;commit&#39;) ? (&#39; &#39;.v.commit) : &#39;&#39;
   2799 <a href="#l2780" class="line" id="l2780">   2780</a>           call append(5, extend([&#39;&#39;, &#39;- &#39;.k.&#39;:&#39;.ref], map(s:lines(diff), &#39;s:format_git_log(v:val)&#39;)))
   2800 <a href="#l2781" class="line" id="l2781">   2781</a>           let cnts[origin] += 1
   2801 <a href="#l2782" class="line" id="l2782">   2782</a>         endif
   2802 <a href="#l2783" class="line" id="l2783">   2783</a>       endif
   2803 <a href="#l2784" class="line" id="l2784">   2784</a>       let bar .= &#39;=&#39;
   2804 <a href="#l2785" class="line" id="l2785">   2785</a>       call s:progress_bar(2, bar, len(total))
   2805 <a href="#l2786" class="line" id="l2786">   2786</a>       normal! 2G
   2806 <a href="#l2787" class="line" id="l2787">   2787</a>       redraw
   2807 <a href="#l2788" class="line" id="l2788">   2788</a>     endfor
   2808 <a href="#l2789" class="line" id="l2789">   2789</a>     if !cnts[origin]
   2809 <a href="#l2790" class="line" id="l2790">   2790</a>       call append(5, [&#39;&#39;, &#39;N/A&#39;])
   2810 <a href="#l2791" class="line" id="l2791">   2791</a>     endif
   2811 <a href="#l2792" class="line" id="l2792">   2792</a>   endfor
   2812 <a href="#l2793" class="line" id="l2793">   2793</a>   call setline(1, printf(&#39;%d plugin(s) updated.&#39;, cnts[0])
   2813 <a href="#l2794" class="line" id="l2794">   2794</a>         \ . (cnts[1] ? printf(&#39; %d plugin(s) have pending updates.&#39;, cnts[1]) : &#39;&#39;))
   2814 <a href="#l2795" class="line" id="l2795">   2795</a> 
   2815 <a href="#l2796" class="line" id="l2796">   2796</a>   if cnts[0] || cnts[1]
   2816 <a href="#l2797" class="line" id="l2797">   2797</a>     nnoremap &lt;silent&gt; &lt;buffer&gt; &lt;plug&gt;(plug-preview) :silent! call &lt;SID&gt;preview_commit()&lt;cr&gt;
   2817 <a href="#l2798" class="line" id="l2798">   2798</a>     if empty(maparg(&quot;\&lt;cr&gt;&quot;, &#39;n&#39;))
   2818 <a href="#l2799" class="line" id="l2799">   2799</a>       nmap &lt;buffer&gt; &lt;cr&gt; &lt;plug&gt;(plug-preview)
   2819 <a href="#l2800" class="line" id="l2800">   2800</a>     endif
   2820 <a href="#l2801" class="line" id="l2801">   2801</a>     if empty(maparg(&#39;o&#39;, &#39;n&#39;))
   2821 <a href="#l2802" class="line" id="l2802">   2802</a>       nmap &lt;buffer&gt; o &lt;plug&gt;(plug-preview)
   2822 <a href="#l2803" class="line" id="l2803">   2803</a>     endif
   2823 <a href="#l2804" class="line" id="l2804">   2804</a>   endif
   2824 <a href="#l2805" class="line" id="l2805">   2805</a>   if cnts[0]
   2825 <a href="#l2806" class="line" id="l2806">   2806</a>     nnoremap &lt;silent&gt; &lt;buffer&gt; X :call &lt;SID&gt;revert()&lt;cr&gt;
   2826 <a href="#l2807" class="line" id="l2807">   2807</a>     echo &quot;Press &#39;X&#39; on each block to revert the update&quot;
   2827 <a href="#l2808" class="line" id="l2808">   2808</a>   endif
   2828 <a href="#l2809" class="line" id="l2809">   2809</a>   normal! gg
   2829 <a href="#l2810" class="line" id="l2810">   2810</a>   setlocal nomodifiable
   2830 <a href="#l2811" class="line" id="l2811">   2811</a> endfunction
   2831 <a href="#l2812" class="line" id="l2812">   2812</a> 
   2832 <a href="#l2813" class="line" id="l2813">   2813</a> function! s:revert()
   2833 <a href="#l2814" class="line" id="l2814">   2814</a>   if search(&#39;^Pending updates&#39;, &#39;bnW&#39;)
   2834 <a href="#l2815" class="line" id="l2815">   2815</a>     return
   2835 <a href="#l2816" class="line" id="l2816">   2816</a>   endif
   2836 <a href="#l2817" class="line" id="l2817">   2817</a> 
   2837 <a href="#l2818" class="line" id="l2818">   2818</a>   let name = s:find_name(line(&#39;.&#39;))
   2838 <a href="#l2819" class="line" id="l2819">   2819</a>   if empty(name) || !has_key(g:plugs, name) ||
   2839 <a href="#l2820" class="line" id="l2820">   2820</a>     \ input(printf(&#39;Revert the update of %s? (y/N) &#39;, name)) !~? &#39;^y&#39;
   2840 <a href="#l2821" class="line" id="l2821">   2821</a>     return
   2841 <a href="#l2822" class="line" id="l2822">   2822</a>   endif
   2842 <a href="#l2823" class="line" id="l2823">   2823</a> 
   2843 <a href="#l2824" class="line" id="l2824">   2824</a>   call s:system(&#39;git reset --hard HEAD@{1} &amp;&amp; git checkout &#39;.plug#shellescape(g:plugs[name].branch).&#39; --&#39;, g:plugs[name].dir)
   2844 <a href="#l2825" class="line" id="l2825">   2825</a>   setlocal modifiable
   2845 <a href="#l2826" class="line" id="l2826">   2826</a>   normal! &quot;_dap
   2846 <a href="#l2827" class="line" id="l2827">   2827</a>   setlocal nomodifiable
   2847 <a href="#l2828" class="line" id="l2828">   2828</a>   echo &#39;Reverted&#39;
   2848 <a href="#l2829" class="line" id="l2829">   2829</a> endfunction
   2849 <a href="#l2830" class="line" id="l2830">   2830</a> 
   2850 <a href="#l2831" class="line" id="l2831">   2831</a> function! s:snapshot(force, ...) abort
   2851 <a href="#l2832" class="line" id="l2832">   2832</a>   call s:prepare()
   2852 <a href="#l2833" class="line" id="l2833">   2833</a>   setf vim
   2853 <a href="#l2834" class="line" id="l2834">   2834</a>   call append(0, [&#39;&quot; Generated by vim-plug&#39;,
   2854 <a href="#l2835" class="line" id="l2835">   2835</a>                 \ &#39;&quot; &#39;.strftime(&quot;%c&quot;),
   2855 <a href="#l2836" class="line" id="l2836">   2836</a>                 \ &#39;&quot; :source this file in vim to restore the snapshot&#39;,
   2856 <a href="#l2837" class="line" id="l2837">   2837</a>                 \ &#39;&quot; or execute: vim -S snapshot.vim&#39;,
   2857 <a href="#l2838" class="line" id="l2838">   2838</a>                 \ &#39;&#39;, &#39;&#39;, &#39;PlugUpdate!&#39;])
   2858 <a href="#l2839" class="line" id="l2839">   2839</a>   1
   2859 <a href="#l2840" class="line" id="l2840">   2840</a>   let anchor = line(&#39;$&#39;) - 3
   2860 <a href="#l2841" class="line" id="l2841">   2841</a>   let names = sort(keys(filter(copy(g:plugs),
   2861 <a href="#l2842" class="line" id="l2842">   2842</a>         \&#39;has_key(v:val, &quot;uri&quot;) &amp;&amp; isdirectory(v:val.dir)&#39;)))
   2862 <a href="#l2843" class="line" id="l2843">   2843</a>   for name in reverse(names)
   2863 <a href="#l2844" class="line" id="l2844">   2844</a>     let sha = has_key(g:plugs[name], &#39;commit&#39;) ? g:plugs[name].commit : s:git_revision(g:plugs[name].dir)
   2864 <a href="#l2845" class="line" id="l2845">   2845</a>     if !empty(sha)
   2865 <a href="#l2846" class="line" id="l2846">   2846</a>       call append(anchor, printf(&quot;silent! let g:plugs[&#39;%s&#39;].commit = &#39;%s&#39;&quot;, name, sha))
   2866 <a href="#l2847" class="line" id="l2847">   2847</a>       redraw
   2867 <a href="#l2848" class="line" id="l2848">   2848</a>     endif
   2868 <a href="#l2849" class="line" id="l2849">   2849</a>   endfor
   2869 <a href="#l2850" class="line" id="l2850">   2850</a> 
   2870 <a href="#l2851" class="line" id="l2851">   2851</a>   if a:0 &gt; 0
   2871 <a href="#l2852" class="line" id="l2852">   2852</a>     let fn = s:plug_expand(a:1)
   2872 <a href="#l2853" class="line" id="l2853">   2853</a>     if filereadable(fn) &amp;&amp; !(a:force || s:ask(a:1.&#39; already exists. Overwrite?&#39;))
   2873 <a href="#l2854" class="line" id="l2854">   2854</a>       return
   2874 <a href="#l2855" class="line" id="l2855">   2855</a>     endif
   2875 <a href="#l2856" class="line" id="l2856">   2856</a>     call writefile(getline(1, &#39;$&#39;), fn)
   2876 <a href="#l2857" class="line" id="l2857">   2857</a>     echo &#39;Saved as &#39;.a:1
   2877 <a href="#l2858" class="line" id="l2858">   2858</a>     silent execute &#39;e&#39; s:esc(fn)
   2878 <a href="#l2859" class="line" id="l2859">   2859</a>     setf vim
   2879 <a href="#l2860" class="line" id="l2860">   2860</a>   endif
   2880 <a href="#l2861" class="line" id="l2861">   2861</a> endfunction
   2881 <a href="#l2862" class="line" id="l2862">   2862</a> 
   2882 <a href="#l2863" class="line" id="l2863">   2863</a> function! s:split_rtp()
   2883 <a href="#l2864" class="line" id="l2864">   2864</a>   return split(&amp;rtp, &#39;\\\@&lt;!,&#39;)
   2884 <a href="#l2865" class="line" id="l2865">   2865</a> endfunction
   2885 <a href="#l2866" class="line" id="l2866">   2866</a> 
   2886 <a href="#l2867" class="line" id="l2867">   2867</a> let s:first_rtp = s:escrtp(get(s:split_rtp(), 0, &#39;&#39;))
   2887 <a href="#l2868" class="line" id="l2868">   2868</a> let s:last_rtp  = s:escrtp(get(s:split_rtp(), -1, &#39;&#39;))
   2888 <a href="#l2869" class="line" id="l2869">   2869</a> 
   2889 <a href="#l2870" class="line" id="l2870">   2870</a> if exists(&#39;g:plugs&#39;)
   2890 <a href="#l2871" class="line" id="l2871">   2871</a>   let g:plugs_order = get(g:, &#39;plugs_order&#39;, keys(g:plugs))
   2891 <a href="#l2872" class="line" id="l2872">   2872</a>   call s:upgrade_specs()
   2892 <a href="#l2873" class="line" id="l2873">   2873</a>   call s:define_commands()
   2893 <a href="#l2874" class="line" id="l2874">   2874</a> endif
   2894 <a href="#l2875" class="line" id="l2875">   2875</a> 
   2895 <a href="#l2876" class="line" id="l2876">   2876</a> let &amp;cpo = s:cpo_save
   2896 <a href="#l2877" class="line" id="l2877">   2877</a> unlet s:cpo_save
